## Clone Wars

### Beginning

* [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"),[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) [establishment](/wiki/Emergency_Powers_Act "Emergency Powers Act") of the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") (declaration of war)[[13]](#cite_note-Rise-13)
* 22 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) (open warfare begins)[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

### End

* [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") (collapse of [Separatist command structure](/wiki/Separatist_officer "Separatist officer"))[[16]](#cite_note-Aftermath-16)
* 19 BBY,[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) [Mission to Mustafar](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) (official end)[[11]](#cite_note-Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel-11)

### Place

[The galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

### Outcome

* [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire")/[Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") victory[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") [reorganizes](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") into the Galactic Empire, restoring the [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"), and declares himself as [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + The [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") becomes the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + The deactivation of the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") throughout [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + The [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") is [reinregrated](/wiki/Separatist_Reintegration_Day "Separatist Reintegration Day") into the Galactic Empire[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17)
  + [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") becomes [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader following his fall to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + Extermination of majority of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") following the issuance of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), beginning the Great [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") Purge[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)
  + Beginning of the outlawing of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") in the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy")[[18]](#cite_note-Head_to_Head-18)
  + The Empire begins its occupation of various [worlds](/wiki/Planet "Planet")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)[[16]](#cite_note-Aftermath-16)[[19]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-19)[[20]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-20)
  + Billions of [casualties](/wiki/Death "Death")[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)
  + End of the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") and beginning of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era")[[22]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-22)

:   "*Designed by the Dark Lord of the Sith, this web is. For now, play his game, we must.*"
:   ―Jedi Grand Master Yoda[[60]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-60)

The **Clone Wars** ([22](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY")–[19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY")) were a [galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")-spanning conflict between the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), which had seceded from the Republic. Also referred to as the **Clone War**, it was named after the [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") used by the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"). Due to the high volume of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") deployed in the conflict, the war would also be known as the **Droid War**. Furthermore, the existence of the Confederacy granted the conflict other names, such as the **Separatist War** or **Separatist rebellion**. With both [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") and [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") being fielded in enormous numbers by each respective side, they were the largest military forces in [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"), and fighting between them swept through the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") for three, nearly four, [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year").

Prior to the conflict, [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), under his alter ego Sheev Palpatine, had spent years amassing [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") power, eventually using the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation")'s [invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") to become the Republic's [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"). Through his [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), he sparked the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), causing thousands of Republic [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") to secede and form a new government as the Confederacy, with Dooku as its [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State"). Beginning with the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), the conflict quickly spread throughout the galaxy with both sides scoring significant victories. At different points in the war it seemed that either side was likely to triumph over the other. At the war's outset, both sides vied for control of major [hyperspace lanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") to gain strategic advantage. That particular struggle ended with a Republic victory when [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and his [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), secured an [alliance](/wiki/Hutt%E2%80%93Republic_treaty "Hutt–Republic treaty") between the Republic and the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan").

Battles, skirmishes, raids, and other actions continued for the next two years, with notable battles occurring on [Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth"), [Felucia](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia "First Battle of Felucia"), [Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare"), and [Kamino](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino"). During this [time](/wiki/Time "Time"), the Separatists developed various super weapons, including more traditional weapons such as the [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon") of the [battleship](/wiki/Battleship "Battleship") *[Malevolence](/wiki/Malevolence "Malevolence")*, as well as biological weapons such as a variant of the [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus "Blue Shadow Virus"). Meanwhile, the Republic launched several key offensives, including the [Second Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis"), which obliterated [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis")' battle droid foundries, and a failed Jedi-led [operation](/wiki/Battle_of_Saleucami "Battle of Saleucami") to capture [Supreme Commander of the Droid Army](/wiki/Supreme_Martial_Commander_of_the_Separatist_Droid_Armies "Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies") [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") at [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"). Amidst the escalating conflict, many planets—including [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") and other members of the [Council of Neutral Systems](/wiki/Council_of_Neutral_Systems "Council of Neutral Systems")—struggled to maintain their neutrality, but found it difficult to escape the carnage.

Over a year into the war, Republic [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") and Separatist Senator [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri") collaborated on an [initiative](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_initiative "Confederate–Republic peace initiative") to end the fighting. However, their collaboration ended after Dooku and Grievous' [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_Coruscant%27s_central_power_distribution_grid "Bombing of Coruscant's central power distribution grid") of the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). Later, a [peace conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference") on Mandalore also failed to resolve the conflict. With no end in sight, the Jedi worked with local militaries, including [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala")'s [military](/wiki/Mon_Cala_planetary_defense_services "Mon Cala planetary defense services") and [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo")'s [Gungan Grand Army](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army"), and covertly trained an insurgent [rebel cell](/wiki/Onderon_rebels "Onderon rebels") to [retake](/wiki/Onderonian_Civil_War "Onderonian Civil War") [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon") from Separatist occupation. Similarly, the Confederacy relied upon factions such as the [Umbaran Militia](/wiki/Umbaran_Militia "Umbaran Militia") and the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire"). Furthermore, a proxy war materialized when [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Talzin](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin") and her son, the now rogue Sith Lord [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), strove to exact their revenge on both the Sith and the Jedi.

During the war's third and final year, the Republic drove the Separatists into redoubts within the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), initiating a campaign termed the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges"). In an effort to reverse the course of the war, Grievous launched a [massive strike](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") on Coruscant through the [Deep Core](/wiki/Deep_Core "Deep Core"). Much of the [Confederate fleet](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems_Navy "Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy") was lost in the assault, along with [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State") Count Dooku. The Confederacy quickly lost its core leadership in quick succession, with Grievous subsequently falling in battle during the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"), and the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") being [massacred](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). This, coupled with the issuing of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and the deactivation of the droid army, led to the total capitulation of the Confederacy and, with it, an end to the war.

Unbeknownst to the majority of those involved—combatants and bureaucrats alike—the conflict was orchestrated, facilitated, instigated, and eventually resolved by Darth Sidious, whose ultimate goal was to restore the [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire") and to transform the Republic into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") with himself as [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") by completely eradicating the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). Sidious was deceiving both sides. Sidious's deception was eventually exposed by Sidious himself who revealed himself as the Sith Lord and cause of the Clone Wars. [Evading arrest](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") by [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") and a cadre of Jedi, Sidious would succeed in this endeavor with the aid of Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, who Sidious seduced to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and molded into his new apprentice [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader. Sidious publicly branded the Jedi as traitors and triggered Order 66, which [forced](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") the Republic's clone troopers to betray and execute their Jedi Generals, thereby initiating a galaxy-wide [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"). Palpatine then declared an end to the Clone Wars in an extraordinary session of the [Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") and [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the transformation of the Republic into the First Galactic Empire, and the Galactic Senate into the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate").

## Prelude[]

### A millennium-old vendetta[]

:   "*At last we will reveal ourselves to the Jedi. At last we will have revenge.*"
:   ―Maul — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250307223813)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac "File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac"))[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61)

 [![The Old Republic collapsed amidst the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Sith Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) [![The Old Republic collapsed amidst the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Sith Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220502004842)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) 

The Old Republic collapsed amidst the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Sith Order.

 

The origins of the Clone Wars dated back to the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Old Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"),[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62) which reigned over a [millennium](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the war. That era marked a [dark age](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic") in [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") history,[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) as the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") battled their ancient enemies, the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), for control of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[63]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-63) The Sith suffered from infighting,[[64]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-64) which ultimately led to their defeat at the hands of the Jedi, but although the Jedi believed they had vanquished their foes,[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61) the Sith had merely retreated into hiding. [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane"), the last surviving [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"), founded a philosophy known as the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), which dictated that the entire Sith Order would be comprised solely of a [master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and an [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice").[[64]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-64) Operating in the shadows, the Sith accumulated power and influence in preparation for the endgame of their [grand plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan"): galactic domination and revenge against the Jedi.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

From the remnants of the Old Republic, a modern Galactic Republic was formed. For the first time, a [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") afforded [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") representation to hundreds of [worlds](/wiki/Planet "Planet") and [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system"). The Old Republic's armed forces were disbanded,[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) leading the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") to assume a peacekeeping role within the Republic, serving at the behest of the Senate and its [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor").[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61) Over time, the Senate incurred notoriety for its stagnant bureaucracy and corruption,[[65]](#cite_note-Databank:_Senate-65) and rifts emerged as the central [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds")—including the Republic's capital, [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant")—became reputed for their willingness to exploit the resources of the outlying [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) Adding to the morass of bureaucracy and inaction was the fact that corporate blocs such as the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), and the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union") were granted Senate representation alongside the Republic's member worlds.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

Nearly a thousand years into the Republic's reign,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") became the ruling Dark [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") of the Sith after betraying and murdering his master [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis"). Sidious planned to continue the Siths' revenge plot by using his Sith persona and alter ego Sheev Palpatine. His double identity would allow him to deceive and eventually destroy the Galactic Republic and Jedi. In order to infiltrate the Republic, Palpatine became the senator of his home planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). As the senator of Naboo, he devised a complex scheme to unseat the incumbent Supreme Chancellor, [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum"), and install himself as the Republic's next head of state: as the Republic became embroiled in a dispute over the taxation of trade routes, Sidious secretly allied himself with [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray"), the [Viceroy of the Trade Federation](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation"), and ordered the Trade Federation to [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of Naboo. When the Senate's characteristic stagnation proved ineffectual at overturning the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), Palpatine manipulated and deceived [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") of Naboo into calling for a [Vote of No Confidence](/wiki/Vote_of_No_Confidence "Vote of No Confidence") in Valorum's leadership.[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61)

 [![After the Jedi nearly eradicated them, the Sith withdrew into the shadows, plotting their revenge.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105820) [![After the Jedi nearly eradicated them, the Sith withdrew into the shadows, plotting their revenge.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20201008105820)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105820) 

After the Jedi nearly eradicated them, the Sith withdrew into the shadows, plotting their revenge.

 

The Senate thereafter elected Palpatine as Valorum's successor, and the Jedi Order aided the [Royal Naboo Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces") in [ending](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") the blockade, though not before the Sith revealed themselves in the form of [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), Sidious' current apprentice. Maul was defeated by the Jedi Knights and presumed [dead](/wiki/Death "Death"), leading the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") to suspect the existence of a second [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord").[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61) Now the Supreme Chancellor, Palpatine was seen as a crusading reformer in the face of the Republic's failings, while three of those major failings—the maze of bureaucracy, the lack of any formal military, and weak central power—were showcased to the galaxy at large. Additionally, thanks to the Invasion of Naboo, Palpatine was able to vilify galactic corporations, which helped lead to the Separatist government. Though an open war was still ten years away, the fight for Naboo had served as the first spark of the Clone Wars in a number of ways.[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51)

### The creation of the clone army[]

:   "*A clone army, and I must say, one of the finest we've ever created.*"  
    "*Tell me, Prime Minister, when my Master first contacted you about the army, did—did he say who it was for?*"  
    "*Of course he did. This army is for the Republic.*"
:   ―Lama Su and Obi-Wan Kenobi on Sifo-Dyas's role in creating the clone army[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

 [![Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas became a pawn in the Sith's plan to create a clone army for the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) [![Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas became a pawn in the Sith's plan to create a clone army for the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20200224151650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) 

Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas became a pawn in the Sith's plan to create a clone army for the Galactic Republic.

 

Sidious found a replacement for Maul in [Count Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), a former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who had left the Order and become integral to the Sith plan for galactic conquest. Sidious and Dooku, the latter of whom adopted the name [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Tyranus, plotted to manipulate the Republic into a sham war with an opposing state. The Jedi would be forced to serve as [generals](/wiki/General "General") for a Republic [army](/wiki/Army "Army") of [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"),[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) who would eventually serve as their executioners. Furthermore, the conflict would destabilize the Republic and render it vulnerable to the Sith takeover.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

Prior to the Invasion of Naboo, the Jedi High Council dismissed one of its members, Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), due to his unorthodox belief that the Republic would need to raise an army for a full-scale conflict that he had foreseen.[[60]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-60) Undeterred, Sifo-Dyas contacted the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan"), a [species](/wiki/Species "Species") reputed for its [cloning](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") industry, and ordered the production of a clone army on behalf of the Republic. In so doing, Sifo-Dyas circumvented both the Senate and the High Council, purporting to have the support of the former.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) When the Sith discovered the existence of the clone army, they went to extreme lengths to hijack the project. At the time, then-Chancellor Valorum asked Sifo-Dyas to oversee [confidential negotiations](/wiki/Mission_to_Oba_Diah_(Sifo-Dyas) "Mission to Oba Diah (Sifo-Dyas)") between the Republic and the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate"), a rising [spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice") cartel that had begun to dominate the [Coruscant Underworld](/wiki/Coruscant_Underworld "Coruscant Underworld"). Unaware of Valorum's request, the High Council separately dispatched Sifo-Dyas to resolve a tribal dispute on the planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia").[[60]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-60)

Sifo-Dyas never reached Felucia, and the resulting events became enmeshed in a web of subterfuge that took the Jedi Order many years to unravel. Dooku, as Tyranus, betrayed his friend by hiring the [Pykes](/wiki/Pyke "Pyke") to [assassinate](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") Sifo-Dyas, and his [T-6 shuttle](/wiki/775519 "775519") was subsequently shot down over the [moon](/wiki/Oba_Diah_moon "Oba Diah moon") of their homeworld [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah"), killing Sifo-Dyas in the crash, while Valorum's personal [attaché](/wiki/Aide "Aide") [Silman](/wiki/Silman "Silman"), who had accompanied him on the mission, survived the attack. The Pykes delivered Sifo-Dyas's corpse to Tyranus, but covertly kept Silman hostage as potential leverage in the future. The Jedi Order, meanwhile, believed Sifo-Dyas to have died on Felucia after he failed to negotiate peace between the local tribes.[[60]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-60)

 [![Jango Fett was chosen by the Sith to become the genetic template of the clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) [![Jango Fett was chosen by the Sith to become the genetic template of the clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20190111035238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) 

Jango Fett was chosen by the Sith to become the genetic template of the clone army.

 

After seizing control of the cloning project, the Sith selected the renowned [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") as the [genetic template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") for their army.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se") served as one of the project's main engineers.[[38]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-38) On the Kaminoan home-world of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"), Fett provided both genetic samples and training for his so-called [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), who were subjected to growth acceleration and thereby aged at twice the normal rate of [humans](/wiki/Human "Human"). As a result, the first generation of [troops](/wiki/Troop "Troop") was ready within a [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") of Sifo-Dyas's original order.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

Sifo-Dyas wanted an [inhibitor chip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") implanted in the [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain") of each Clone, as a safeguard against rogue Jedi. However, Dooku and Sidious retooled the chips in order to ensure the Jedi's destruction. Posing as a Jedi, Dooku presented the chip to the Kaminoan [scientists](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") and deceived them into believing the chips were designed to preclude aggression within each subject, as well as that Sifo-Dyas had ordered the installation of the chips[[66]](#cite_note-Fugitive-66) as a countermeasure against betrayal from rogue Jedi.[[38]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-38)In truth, the chips would force each clone to comply with [Protocol 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), a directive for the soldiers to execute their Jedi [commanders](/wiki/Commander "Commander") for being perceived traitors to the Republic.[[66]](#cite_note-Fugitive-66) Thus, the Sith would be able to massacre the entire Jedi Order via its subordinate soldiers.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

### Separatist Crisis[]

:   "*I will not let this Republic that has stood for a thousand years be split in two. My negotiations will not fail.*"  
    "*If they do, you must realize there aren't enough Jedi to protect the Republic. We're keepers of the peace, not soldiers.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Mace Windu[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis")
 [![Count Dooku recruited the majority of the galaxy's trade guilds to join the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/SecessionistMovement.png/revision/latest?cb=20180629190252) [![Count Dooku recruited the majority of the galaxy's trade guilds to join the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/SecessionistMovement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20180629190252)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/SecessionistMovement.png/revision/latest?cb=20180629190252) 

Count Dooku recruited the majority of the galaxy's trade guilds to join the Confederacy of Independent Systems.

 

Eight years after the Invasion of Naboo, a pan-galactic [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") began to take shape when [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") Dooku commandeered a [HoloNet relay](/wiki/HoloNet_relay "HoloNet relay") station in the [Raxus system](/wiki/Raxus_system "Raxus system") and berated the Republic with condemning rhetoric. Over the next two years,[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) a [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") arose when thousands of [star](/wiki/Star "Star") systems seceded from the Republic and flocked to the Confederacy.[[65]](#cite_note-Databank:_Senate-65)[[67]](#cite_note-Databank:_Confederacy-67) The Separatist Crisis sent the Republic into a frenzy, particularly as Dooku repeatedly spurned Palpatine's public requests for negotiation.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) The Republic Senate soon became divided over the passage of a [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"). Advocates of the bill argued that the Republic required a military force to defend itself from the Separatists, whereas others such as now-Senator Padmé Amidala believed that the measure would provoke full-scale civil war between the Republic and the Confederacy. Such a war became increasingly inevitable,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) with the Sith Lords poised to lead both sides of the approaching conflict that would tear the galaxy asunder.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

Fearful that such meetings would grant the CIS state legitimacy, the Republic Senate also declared it illegal under[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) the [Republic Senate non-communication law](/wiki/Republic_Senate_non-communication_law "Republic Senate non-communication law")[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) for Republic representatives to meet with Separatists in formal talks.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) By 22 BBY,[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) the Sith had nearly completed preparations for open conflict between the Republic and the Confederacy. Nominally the Confederacy functioned as a democracy,[[67]](#cite_note-Databank:_Confederacy-67) and delegates from its myriad member worlds formed a [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate"),[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) though in truth it was ruled by the Sith.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) At the same time, the galaxy's major corporations pledged their support and resources to the Confederacy, and their leaders thereby earned seats on Dooku's [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council").[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) Its members included [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [San Hill](/wiki/San_Hill "San Hill") of the InterGalactic Banking Clan, [Foreman](/wiki/Foreman "Foreman") [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor") of the Techno Union, [Magistrate](/wiki/Magistrate "Magistrate") [Passel Argente](/wiki/Passel_Argente "Passel Argente") of the [Corporate Alliance](/wiki/Corporate_Alliance "Corporate Alliance"), [Presidente](/wiki/Presidente "Presidente") [Shu Mai](/wiki/Shu_Mai "Shu Mai") of the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild"), and [Archduke](/wiki/Archduke "Archduke") [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser") of the [Geonosian hives](/wiki/Geonosian_hive "Geonosian hive"), as well as Senators [Po Nudo](/wiki/Po_Nudo "Po Nudo") of [Ando](/wiki/Ando "Ando") and [Tikkes](/wiki/Tikkes "Tikkes") of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala").[[68]](#cite_note-Databank:_Separatist_Council-68)[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14)

Nute Gunray's condition for joining the Separatist Council was that Amidala be killed in revenge for her humiliating defeat of him at the Battle of Naboo. Jango Fett and his associate, [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell"), undertook the [bounty](/wiki/Bounty "Bounty") that Gunray subsequently issued on Amidala. Just before the Senate's vote on the Military Creation Act, Wesell mounted an [unsuccessful attempt](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala") on Amidala's life, resulting in the High Council designating [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and his [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker")—both of whom had been instrumental in the Republic's victory at the Battle of Naboo—as Amidala's personal [bodyguards](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard"). Wesell's second attempt on Amidala's life similarly failed, and Fett used a [Kamino saberdart](/wiki/Kamino_saberdart "Kamino saberdart") to execute Wesell before Kenobi and Skywalker could extract information from her. Nevertheless, Kenobi identified the saberdart's connection to Kamino, and was alarmed when his research revealed that the planet had been erased from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives"). With the help of [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), he pinpointed Kamino's location above the galactic plane, just south of the [Rishi Maze](/wiki/Rishi_Maze "Rishi Maze"), and traveled there as part of his [investigation](/wiki/Mission_to_Kamino_(Separatist_Crisis) "Mission to Kamino (Separatist Crisis)") into Amidala's assailant.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's discovery of the clone army on Kamino precipitated the opening battle of the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183044) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's discovery of the clone army on Kamino precipitated the opening battle of the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20080117183044)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183044) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi's discovery of the clone army on Kamino precipitated the opening battle of the Clone Wars.

 

When Kenobi arrived at Kamino's capital of [Tipoca City](/wiki/Tipoca_City "Tipoca City"), [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") greeted him and revealed the existence of the clone army. By this time, 200,000 [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") were ready for deployment, with a million more soldiers nearing completion of their training. A shocked Kenobi reported his discovery to the High Council, which ordered him to detain Fett and bring him to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on Coruscant for questioning. Fett escaped from Tipoca [City](/wiki/City "City") with his son, an unaltered clone whom he named [Boba](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"), and fled to[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) the Confederate capital of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis").[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) Kenobi tracked the Fetts and, after engaging in a [starfighter dogfight](/wiki/Dogfight_over_Geonosis "Dogfight over Geonosis") that led them to believe him dead, followed them to the planetary surface. There, he discovered that the [Geonosians](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") were manufacturing millions of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") in their [droid foundries](/wiki/Geonosis_droid_factories "Geonosis droid factories"). He also witnessed a meeting between Dooku and the Separatist Council, discovering that they were preparing to merge their resources into a [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"). The Geonosians thereafter captured Kenobi, though not before he sent a message to Skywalker.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

Skywalker was with Amidala on the nearby world of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") and relayed Kenobi's message to Coruscant, where Palpatine and the High Council heard the news that the commerce guilds had joined the Confederacy. Against the Council's orders, Amidala and Skywalker rushed to rescue Kenobi on Geonosis. While Kenobi was in his [custody](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner"), Dooku claimed that the entire Republic was under the sway of a Dark Lord of the Sith named Darth Sidious, and tried to persuade Kenobi to help him destroy the Sith. Kenobi refused, and after Amidala and Skywalker were similarly captured, the Geonosians sentenced all three of them to execution in[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) the [Petranaki Arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena").[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14)

Despite Kenobi's report that the Confederacy was raising an army, Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") and other members of the Senate still believed that the Military Creation Act would not be passed in time to contend with the Separatists. Consequently, [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") of Naboo motioned that the Senate grant emergency powers to Palpatine, who could then use his newfound authority to formally approve the creation of a [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). Though Palpatine promised to relinquish his emergency powers once the crisis had passed,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) that was never to be the case.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) While Master Yoda traveled to Kamino to marshal the clone troopers for the Grand Army, Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") assembled an [assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team")[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) of 212 Jedi,[[70]](#cite_note-CVD_NE-70) drawn from the Masters of the High Council and the Order's ranks of Knights and Padawans, to save Kenobi from [imprisonment](/wiki/Prison "Prison") on Geonosis. The galaxy teetered on the brink of civil war.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

## The war[]

### Year one (22 BBY–21 BBY)[]

#### First Battle of Geonosis[]

:   "*This is just the beginning!*"
:   ―Dooku[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis")
 [![Mace Windu and his allies held out long enough for Yoda to arrive with the clone troopers of the Grand Army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/JediCircle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150809165802) [![Mace Windu and his allies held out long enough for Yoda to arrive with the clone troopers of the Grand Army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/JediCircle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20150809165802)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/JediCircle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150809165802) 

Mace Windu and his allies held out long enough for Yoda to arrive with the clone troopers of the Grand Army.

 

The [Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis")[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) commenced when Windu and his Jedi strike team infiltrated the Petranaki arena to save Amidala, Kenobi, and Skywalker from gladiatorial combat with three beasts: an [acklay](/wiki/Acklay "Acklay"), a [nexu](/wiki/Nexu "Nexu"), and a [reek](/wiki/Reek "Reek"). While the Geonosian spectators fled the arena, Dooku unleashed a massive [infantry](/wiki/Infantry "Infantry") of [B1 battle droids](/wiki/B1-series_battle_droid "B1-series battle droid"), [B2 super battle droids](/wiki/B2-series_super_battle_droid "B2-series super battle droid"), and [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka") against the Jedi. During the ensuing ground battle,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) Council member [Coleman Trebor](/wiki/Coleman_Trebor "Coleman Trebor")[[71]](#cite_note-Databank:_Trebor-71) came within [seconds](/wiki/Second "Second") of ending the conflict when he nearly managed to kill Dooku, but Jango Fett gunned him down before he could do so. Windu thereafter beheaded Fett, an act that would earn him the ire of his son, Boba. Within a short span, only Amidala, Kenobi, Skywalker, Windu, and a fraction of their Jedi allies were still standing. With his battle [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") encircling the ring of survivors, Dooku demanded their unconditional surrender, but Windu refused to allow himself and his comrades to become hostages.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

Just as Windu and the other survivors were about to be executed, Yoda swept in with reinforcements, the Grand Army of the Republic:[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) 192,000 clone troopers[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) aboard [*Acclamator*-class transgalactic military assault ships](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship"), with [LAAT/i gunships](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport/infantry "Low Altitude Assault Transport/infantry") ferrying them into the Petranaki arena to defend and extract the surviving Jedi. Amidala, Kenobi, Skywalker, Windu, and the other surviving Jedi withdrew from the arena aboard Yoda's [gunships](/wiki/Gunship "Gunship") and rushed to Geonosis's [red](/wiki/Color "Color") sand [plains](/wiki/Desert "Desert"), where a ground campaign was taking shape. Jedi such as [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura"), [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), and many others immediately accepted command positions and led the clone troopers into battle against the Separatist Droid Army, working to decimate the enemy infantry and prevent the Techno Union's [Hardcell transports](/wiki/Hardcell-class_interstellar_transport "Hardcell-class interstellar transport") from escaping. While Yoda proceeded to the Republic's forward command center, Windu oversaw an assembly area,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) where Clone Commander [Ponds](/wiki/Ponds "Ponds")[[72]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-72)[[73]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia:_Ponds-73) handed him command of five special [commando](/wiki/Commando "Commando") units.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Meebur Gascon](/wiki/Meebur_Gascon "Meebur Gascon") and other top strategists from [Republic High Command](/wiki/Republic_High_Command "Republic High Command") advised the Grand Army on its battlefield tactics.[[74]](#cite_note-Secret_Weapons-74)

A frenetic offensive ensued, as the Republic's [All Terrain Tactical Enforcers](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer") went head-to-head with the Separatists' [IG-227 *Hailfire*-class droid tanks](/wiki/IG-227_Hailfire-class_droid_tank "IG-227 Hailfire-class droid tank") and [OG-9 homing spider droids](/wiki/OG-9_homing_spider_droid "OG-9 homing spider droid"). Yoda ordered the Grand Army's [Self-Propelled Heavy Artillery](/wiki/Self-Propelled_Heavy_Artillery "Self-Propelled Heavy Artillery") Turbolaser [walkers](/wiki/Walker "Walker") to ground a number of Trade Federation [core ships](/wiki/Core_ship "Core ship") before they could escape. On the ground, the Jedi and their clone troopers were forced to contend with the enemy battle droids and [DSD1 dwarf spider droids](/wiki/DSD1_dwarf_spider_droid "DSD1 dwarf spider droid"), but they made gradual headway against the Separatists. Overwhelmed by the Republic's assault, Dooku and the Separatist Council ordered a retreat. Poggle the Lesser entrusted Dooku with the Geonosians' plans to the [Ultimate Weapon](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), and Dooku headed for a remote [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") where his [*Punworcca 116*-class interstellar sloop](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_solar_sailer "Count Dooku's solar sailer") was docked. En route to the hangar, Dooku crossed paths with Amidala, Kenobi, and Skywalker and they gave chase aboard their LAAT/i gunship. When Dooku's escort of [*Nantex*-class territorial defense starfighters](/wiki/Nantex-class_territorial_defense_starfighter "Nantex-class territorial defense starfighter") retaliated, Amidala was dislodged from the gunship, while Kenobi and Skywalker pursued the Count.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

 [![Beginning on Geonosis, the Clone Wars soon spread to countless worlds across the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) [![Beginning on Geonosis, the Clone Wars soon spread to countless worlds across the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20170325151752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) 

Beginning on Geonosis, the Clone Wars soon spread to countless worlds across the galaxy.

 

When Kenobi and Skywalker reached the hangar, Dooku defeated them in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"), injuring Kenobi and severing Skywalker's right [forearm](/wiki/Limb "Limb"). The duel continued when Yoda, Dooku's former Jedi Master, arrived and proved more than a challenge for the Sith Lord. Dooku was able to escape only by collapsing a pillar on top of Kenobi and Skywalker, forcing Yoda to choose between pressing his attack and saving his fellow Jedi. Amidala arrived at the hangar with another gunship, but she and her [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of clone troopers were unable to shoot down Dooku's [solar sailer](/wiki/Solar_sailer "Solar sailer"). Although Dooku and the Separatist Council had escaped with their forces, the Republic declared victory in the Battle of Geonosis.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

The beginning of the Clone Wars shifted the balance of the Force itself.[[75]](#cite_note-Battle_of_GeoTrailer-75) Dooku secretly traveled to Coruscant, where he met with Darth Sidious and reported that the intergalactic conflict which they had worked to instigate was finally underway. Though Kenobi believed that the clone troopers had been instrumental to the Republic's victory on Geonosis, Yoda knew that it was not a victory: The Clone Wars had begun. From Coruscant, the Republic deployed tens of thousands of clone troopers and a [fleet](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet") of [warships](/wiki/Warship "Warship") and assault craft, which formed the [Republic Navy](/wiki/Republic_Navy "Republic Navy"), as part of its war machine.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) The Confederacy, meanwhile, moved its capital from Geonosis[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) to the planet [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"), which served as the [headquarters](/wiki/Separatist_Senate_Building "Separatist Senate Building") of the Separatist Senate.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

#### Conflict spreads[]

:   "*I have to admit that without the clones, it would not have been a victory.*"  
    "*Victory? Victory, you say, Master Obi-Wan? Not victory. The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun, the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda, following the Battle of Geonosis[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

 [![The Grand Army became the backbone of the Republic's growing war effort against the Confederacy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918154725) [![The Grand Army became the backbone of the Republic's growing war effort against the Confederacy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20090918154725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918154725) 

The Grand Army became the backbone of the Republic's growing war effort against the Confederacy.

 

As the Clone Wars engulfed world after world across the galaxy[[76]](#cite_note-Databank:_Jedi_Order-76) incredibly quickly, Amidala's [handmaiden](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens") [Dormé](/wiki/Dorm%C3%A9 "Dormé") suspected the Confederacy had its forces lying in wait on the impression the events on Geonosis would end in a Separatist triumph, only for the Republic's own forces to be able to confront the CIS.[[77]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-77) Windu also suspected the Separatists were moving to establish a foothold in the Outer Rim and then move inwards to the Core, eventually having enough strength to strike at Coruscant itself. As such, the Republic was forced to move forces into the Rim to prevent the Confederacy from completing a foothold that they could push in with.[[78]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-78) Furthermore, in practice, the Separatists knew that they would not have to win every battle; instead, they understood victory could be achieved by making the conflict too costly—in both financial[[13]](#cite_note-Rise-13) and personnel terms[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)—for the Republic to continue it.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise-13)

The Confederacy's corporate sponsors began an economic strangulation of the Republic,[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17) just as [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") of the planet [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu") had foreseen,[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) but the CIS's corporate backers also publicly distanced themselves from the new power. Claiming themselves neutral,[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17) they continued their business with the Republic in the name of war profiteering from both sides.[[79]](#cite_note-Umbara_Commentary-79) In total truth, corporations like the Trade Federation and Techno Union—thanks to their actions during the war—were almost entirely open in their support of the Separatist cause, yet the neutrality claim managed to stand throughout the war.[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17) The Jedi were forced to relinquish their traditional roles as peacekeepers[[76]](#cite_note-Databank:_Jedi_Order-76) in favor of military commands within the Grand Army of the Republic. Knights and Masters accepted the new rank of [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General"). Even Padawans contributed to the Republic's war effort, serving as [Jedi Commanders](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") on the battlefield[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) at the suggestion of Palpatine.[[80]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-80) Among the newly promoted Jedi Generals was Anakin Skywalker, whom the Jedi High Council elevated to Knighthood.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Unbeknownst to his colleagues, Skywalker had secretly [married Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala") following the Battle of Geonosis,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) a relationship that would have repercussions for the entire war.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

Amidala and Skywalker were also involved in a [mission to Nooroyo](/wiki/Mission_to_Nooroyo "Mission to Nooroyo") between the Battle of Geonosis and their wedding, during which they escaped Gunray's forces when the Viceroy arrived for in person negotiations over [Nooroyo](/wiki/Nooroyo "Nooroyo")'s spice export.[[77]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-77) To satisfy the Republic's increased demand for troops, Kamino continued its production and training of clone troopers. In turn, the Republic Navy blockaded Kamino,[[81]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-81) and the Grand Army established a network of [listening posts](/wiki/Listening_post "Listening post") to monitor Separatist activity in the vicinity.[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82) Due to the death of Jango Fett, the Kaminoan scientists stretched the preexisting samples of his [DNA](/wiki/DNA "DNA") in order to [decant](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") more clones. The Jedi High Council selected one of its members, Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti"), to oversee the training of [clone cadets](/wiki/Clone_cadet "Clone cadet") in Kamino's Tipoca City, assisted by contracted [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") such as [Bric](/wiki/Bric "Bric") and [El-Les](/wiki/El-Les "El-Les") to help supervise the clones' combat instruction.[[81]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-81) The clones quickly started to show signs of individuality, which only improved their effectiveness.[[77]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-77)

 [![General Grievous and Asajj Ventress served as Dooku's primary agents and assassins.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505212856) [![General Grievous and Asajj Ventress served as Dooku's primary agents and assassins.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130505212856)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505212856) 

General Grievous and Asajj Ventress served as Dooku's primary agents and assassins.

 

The Republic attracted both internal and external criticism for its use of clone troopers, whom some viewed as [slaves](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") to the Jedi.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83) One trooper deserted from the Grand Army after the Confederacy [annihilated](/wiki/Attack_on_a_Republic_troop_transport "Attack on a Republic troop transport") his unit; he fled to the planet [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"), where he took the name [Cut Lawquane](/wiki/Cut_Lawquane "Cut Lawquane") with a family.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84) On the other hand, the Separatist citizenry took pride in the fact that [officers](/wiki/Officer "Officer") in the [Confederacy military](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military") were willing participants, while its armed forces mainly sacrificed expendable battle droids for their cause.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21) At the same time, the Confederate populace was insulated from reports of war crimes that were committed in its name. The primary cause of the carnage was General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"),[[85]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia:_Mina-85) a [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord")-turned-[cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") from [Kalee](/wiki/Kalee "Kalee") who oversaw the Droid Army[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) and would lead its numbers to many victories over the course of the war.[[86]](#cite_note-DoubleVision-86)

In addition to Grievous, Dooku recruited another agent as his [lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") and [emissary](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat"):[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87) [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"), a slave-turned-Jedi from [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir") who fell to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and became Dooku's apprentice.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) Though Grievous and Ventress developed a long-standing rivalry,[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) both were motivated by a deep-seated hatred for the Jedi Order.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29) Grievous and Ventress made a habit of claiming as trophies the [lightsabers](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") of their fallen Jedi victims, and Dooku collected the pilfered weapons in his [palace](/wiki/Castle_Serenno "Castle Serenno") on [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno"). Ventress acquired one such lightsaber from Jedi Master [Tholme](/wiki/Tholme "Tholme"), whom she bested in combat during a [major campaign](/wiki/Battle_of_unidentified_planet_(Tholme_and_Ventress) "Battle of unidentified planet (Tholme and Ventress)"). She elected to slay Tholme rather than accept his surrender.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)

The outbreak of the Clone Wars shifted the balance of power on numerous worlds. Since the Separatist Crisis, a [schism](/wiki/Antar_4_schism "Antar 4 schism") had fractured the [Gotal](/wiki/Gotal "Gotal") population of [Antar 4](/wiki/Antar_4 "Antar 4"), with the Confederacy backing [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorist "Terrorist") groups to combat the [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon")'s Republic loyalists. The loyalists remained in power until shortly after the Battle of Geonosis, when the Confederacy conquered Antar 4, and the moon briefly served as a headquarters for Dooku. While millions of Gotal [refugees](/wiki/Refugee "Refugee") fled to their colony world of [Atzerri](/wiki/Atzerri "Atzerri"), an influx of [Koorivar](/wiki/Koorivar "Koorivar"), [Gossams](/wiki/Gossam "Gossam"), and other Confederate-allied species immigrated to Antar 4. The resulting political crisis on the moon gave rise to one of the Republic's first resistance cells. Gotal and Koorivar loyalists executed numerous acts of sabotage against the Separatist regime, with the Republic covertly sponsoring their guerrilla campaign. Despite their efforts, the Confederacy retained control of Antar 4 throughout the war.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1)

 [![The Confederacy captured the planet Lola Sayu early in the war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/LolaSayu-CR.png/revision/latest?cb=20130529012125) [![The Confederacy captured the planet Lola Sayu early in the war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/LolaSayu-CR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130529012125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/LolaSayu-CR.png/revision/latest?cb=20130529012125) 

The Confederacy captured the planet Lola Sayu early in the war.

 

Early in the Clone Wars,[[88]](#cite_note-Databank:_Citadel-88) the Confederacy [seized](/wiki/Capture_of_Lola_Sayu "Capture of Lola Sayu") the Outer Rim world of [Lola Sayu](/wiki/Lola_Sayu "Lola Sayu"),[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) the site of the infamous Republic prison known as the [Citadel](/wiki/Citadel "Citadel"). The Citadel had been constructed five [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") earlier to hold Jedi who turned against the Republic. The Separatists converted the facility into a prisoner-of-war camp, using it to house Republic captives.[[88]](#cite_note-Databank:_Citadel-88) The Separatists also invaded [Millius Prime](/wiki/Millius_Prime "Millius Prime"), one of the thousand moons of the remote planet [Iego](/wiki/Iego "Iego"), and drove away its inhabitants, the peaceful [Angels](/wiki/Diathim "Diathim"). The Separatists established military sites on both Iego and Millius Prime, but later withdrew from the system. Before departing, they seeded Iego's [asteroid field](/wiki/Asteroid_field "Asteroid field") with a [security grid](/wiki/Laser_web "Laser web") of laser emitters that trapped its residents on the surface.[[89]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-89)

#### Various battles[]

:   "*Tech… what was the war like?"  
    "It was a primary mission objective comprised of battles on various fronts."  
    "But… what was it like?"  
    "Hmm? I just told you.*"
:   ―[Omega](/wiki/Omega "Omega") asking [Tech](/wiki/Tech "Tech") about the war[[90]](#cite_note-Reunion-90)

With the war spread across the galaxy, many planets and parts of space were left to become battlegrounds,[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91) creating numerous fronts.[[90]](#cite_note-Reunion-90) With the conflict's nature as a galaxy-wide war, many such fronts could all be active at the same time.[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91) Over the course of the Clone Wars, planets swept up in the conflict included [Akiva](/wiki/Akiva "Akiva"), where a Confederate [droid factory](/wiki/Akiva_production_plant "Akiva production plant") turned the planet into a [battlefield](/wiki/Battle_of_Akiva "Battle of Akiva") between the Jedi and the Separatists;[[92]](#cite_note-Aftermath_novel-92) and [Sedratis](/wiki/Sedratis "Sedratis"), which hosted the [Battle of Sedratis](/wiki/Battle_of_Sedratis "Battle of Sedratis"). During the latter campaign, Jedi ace [pilots](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") Skywalker and [Huulik](/wiki/Huulik "Huulik") proved instrumental in securing a Republic victory over the Confederacy's [droid starfighter](/wiki/Droid_starfighter "Droid starfighter") forces.[[93]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-93) During the war, a number of manufacturers converted [freighters](/wiki/Freighter "Freighter") and [transports](/wiki/Transport "Transport") into combat vessels. New vehicles loaded with weapons were also made.[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) During the conflict, because repair facilities were often heavily damaged during battles, [Nomad](/wiki/Nomad_(starship) "Nomad (starship)") starships would arrive in star systems after the fleets had departed and the fighting was over. The Nomads would help the local population with repairs to compensate for the damaged facilities.[[94]](#cite_note-Thrawn-94) The [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") fought for the Republic in several systems.[[95]](#cite_note-Rebels_VG-95)

 [![Battle droids under General Grievous clash with Republic clone troopers on one of the war's many battlefronts.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest?cb=20230529060353) [![Battle droids under General Grievous clash with Republic clone troopers on one of the war's many battlefronts.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230529060353)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest?cb=20230529060353) 

Battle droids under General Grievous clash with Republic clone troopers on one of the war's many battlefronts.

 

At one point, a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Crombach_Nebula "Battle of Crombach Nebula") was fought in the [Crombach Nebula](/wiki/Crombach_Nebula "Crombach Nebula"), during which Jedi Master [Wom-Nii Gnaden](/wiki/Wom-Nii_Gnaden "Wom-Nii Gnaden")'s [NTB-630 naval bomber](/wiki/NTB-630_naval_bomber "NTB-630 naval bomber") collided with a [*Munificent*-class star frigate](/wiki/Munificent-class_star_frigate "Munificent-class star frigate").[[96]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles_2018-96) [One Confederate officer](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri%27s_husband "Mina Bonteri's husband"), the [husband](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage") of Separatist Senator [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri"), was slain while [defending](/wiki/Attack_on_Aargonar "Attack on Aargonar") a [new base](/wiki/Aargonar_Separatist_base "Aargonar Separatist base") on the planet [Aargonar](/wiki/Aargonar "Aargonar") from Republic forces.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) During a space battle at one point, clone pilot [Sicko](/wiki/Sicko "Sicko") piloted a LAAT/i gunship towards a force of [vulture droid starfighters](/wiki/Vulture-class_starfighter "Vulture-class starfighter"), allowing the gunship's crew to take out many of the droids.[[97]](#cite_note-Hotshots_2-97) Under the command of General [Darrus Jeht](/wiki/Darrus_Jeht "Darrus Jeht"), the [*Maelstrom*-class battle cruiser](/wiki/Maelstrom-class_battle_cruiser "Maelstrom-class battle cruiser") named the [*Maelstrom*](/wiki/Maelstrom_(Maelstrom-class) "Maelstrom (Maelstrom-class)") served with distinction at the [Battle of Kromus](/wiki/Battle_of_Kromus "Battle of Kromus") and later the [Battle of Cularin](/wiki/Battle_of_Cularin "Battle of Cularin").[[98]](#cite_note-LBE-98) The [Humbarine sector](/wiki/Humbarine_sector "Humbarine sector") saw heavy fighting during the war, with its capital planet [Humbarine](/wiki/Humbarine "Humbarine") suffering a [Separatist bombardment](/wiki/Bombardment_of_Humbarine "Bombardment of Humbarine") that completely seared the world's surface.[[99]](#cite_note-Dawn_of_Rebellion_Visual-99)

#### Back and forth of Christophsis[]

:   "*Your technology will not save you, and your friends on the planet below shall perish as a result of your* failure*. The people of Christophsis and her resources shall join the Separatist Alliance.*"
:   ―Admiral Trench, in a message to his Republic opponents[[55]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-55)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Battle of Christophsis](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis")

In the immediate aftermath of the Battle of Geonosis, Grievous and the Separatist Droid Army wrested control of the galaxy's major [hyperspace lanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), isolating the Republic from the bulk of its Grand Army.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Encircled by the Confederacy[[100]](#cite_note-Propaganda-100) and with their forces spread thin, the Jedi Generals were unable to gain traction in the Outer Rim Territories, especially as worlds continued to flock to the Confederacy.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) As the next phase of the Clone Wars began,[[100]](#cite_note-Propaganda-100) the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan")—which controlled [Hutt Space](/wiki/Hutt_Space "Hutt Space") with its network of supply routes reaching to the Outer Rim—became a coveted ally for both the Republic and the Confederacy.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

 [![Anakin Skywalker's and Trench's fleets exchange heavy fire over Christophsis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BlockadeChristophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20200720062217) [![Anakin Skywalker's and Trench's fleets exchange heavy fire over Christophsis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BlockadeChristophsis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20200720062217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BlockadeChristophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20200720062217) 

Anakin Skywalker's and Trench's fleets exchange heavy fire over Christophsis.

 

In a bid to secure the Hutts' supply routes for the Separatists, Dooku hatched a plot to kidnap [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta "Rotta"), the son of Hutt [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure"), and frame the Jedi Order for the crime. Dooku collaborated with Jabba's uncle [Ziro](/wiki/Ziro_Desilijic_Tiure "Ziro Desilijic Tiure"), who hoped to depose his nephew as leader of the Hutt Clan. The first stage of Dooku's plan required that the Jedi's attention be diverted elsewhere; to that end, Dooku ordered his forces to conquer [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"),[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) a [crystalline](/wiki/Crystal "Crystal") Outer Rim world valued for its location and resources,[[101]](#cite_note-Databank:_Christophsis-101) and also the site of a Republic relief effort overseen by Senator Bail Organa. The Confederate [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Trench](/wiki/Trench "Trench") [blockaded](/wiki/Christophsis_blockade "Christophsis blockade") Christophsis with a massive detachment from the [Confederacy navy](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems_Navy "Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy"), while Separatist ground forces subjugated the planet's inhabitants.[[55]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-55) After a number of native [Christophsians](/wiki/Christophsian "Christophsian") mounted a futile defense of their homeworld, they requested aid from the Jedi High Council.[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83)

Jedi Generals Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker, alongside Admiral [Wullf Yularen](/wiki/Wullf_Yularen "Wullf Yularen"), were dispatched with a task force to [rescue](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis") Organa and the besieged Christophsians. Although their fleet of [*Venator*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") was unable to penetrate Trench's immense blockade of warships, Skywalker and Yularen used an experimental [stealth ship](/wiki/IPV-2C_Stealth_Corvette "IPV-2C Stealth Corvette") to outmaneuver Trench and obliterate his [flagship](/wiki/Flagship "Flagship"), the *[Invincible](/wiki/Invincible "Invincible")*[[55]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-55) (although Trench narrowly survived his [dreadnought's](/wiki/Providence-class_Dreadnought "Providence-class Dreadnought") vaporization and later returned to active duty[[102]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-102)). Having broken through the blockade, Skywalker and Yularen delivered the much-needed relief supplies to Organa's refugee camp on the surface, while Kenobi exploited the hole in the Confederate armada to overwhelm the opposing fleet[[55]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-55) long enough to land a Republic invasion force on the planet. The Separatists likewise fortified their ground troops with reinforcements, concealing their true numbers from the Republic.[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83)

By this time, Dooku had dispatched Asajj Ventress to Christophsis to further hamper the Republic's progress. As Kenobi and Skywalker planned to ambush the battle droid forces in a major city plaza, a [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") within the Republic ranks, [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant") [Slick](/wiki/Slick "Slick"), apprised the Separatists of the Jedi's attack plan. Slick's actions transformed a potential Republic victory into a retreat, and Kenobi and Skywalker withdrew their men to the Republic's [base](/wiki/Christophsis_Republic_base "Christophsis Republic base"). Suspecting the existence of an informant, Kenobi and Skywalker departed to gather information behind enemy lines, while [Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Marshal_Commander "Clone Marshal Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody") and [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex") personally launched an investigation into the source of the intelligence leak. After they exposed Slick as the spy, he bombed the Republic's weapons depot, leading Rex and Cody to mobilize a swift manhunt. They arrested Slick and sent him to lock-up, though the damage was already done. Most of the Republic's arsenal was reduced to wreckage, with only a quartet of [AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannons](/wiki/AV-7_Anti-vehicle_Artillery_Cannon "AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannon") surviving his sabotage.[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83)

At the [Confederate headquarters](/wiki/Christophsis_Separatist_headquarters "Christophsis Separatist headquarters"), Kenobi and Skywalker encountered Ventress and engaged her in a lightsaber duel,[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) which she used to buy time for Slick's sabotage.[[103]](#cite_note-Databank:_Ventress-103) Both Jedi halted their attack once they witnessed the sheer size of the Separatists' landing force. After Kenobi and Skywalker escaped back to their base, General [Whorm Loathsom](/wiki/Whorm_Loathsom "Whorm Loathsom") assumed command of the droid infantry and commenced an assault on the city, while Ventress left to execute the next phase of Dooku's plan:[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83) for everything that the world had been able to offer the Confederacy,[[55]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-55) Dooku elected to turn the battle for Christophsis into little more than a distraction, ordering Ventress to depart to carry out the kidnapping Rotta the Huttlet while Loathsom's forces distracted the Republic via the continued Christophsian campaign. She traveled to Tatooine aboard her personal [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship"), the [*Trident*](/wiki/Trident_(starship) "Trident (starship)"), and spirited Rotta away from his homeworld.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

In addition to Slick's sabotage of their weapons depot,[[83]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-83) the Republic forces lost their [naval](/wiki/Navy "Navy") support when the Separatists' [orbital](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit") defenses ousted Yularen and his fleet from the [Christoph system](/wiki/Christoph_system "Christoph system"). Though they were severely outnumbered, Kenobi, Skywalker, and their clone soldiers managed to repel Loathsom's infantry from the city. [Octuptarra tri-droids](/wiki/Octuptarra_tri-droid "Octuptarra tri-droid") lent their support to the Separatists' second wave, but the AV-7 Anti-vehicle Cannons halted the advance of Loathsom's rearguard of [Armored Assault Tanks](/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank_Mk_I "Armored Assault Tank Mk I"). Meanwhile, believing that renegades had kidnapped Rotta, Jabba contacted Sheev Palpatine to request the Republic's assistance in rescuing his son. Since Kenobi and Skywalker were the only Jedi available for such a task, Yoda dispatched a messenger to Christophsis to recall the two Jedi Generals from the battlefront. The messenger was Skywalker's new Padawan learner, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano").[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

 [![Yoda arrives on Christophsis to relay new orders to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and Ahsoka Tano.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013042053) [![Yoda arrives on Christophsis to relay new orders to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and Ahsoka Tano.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121013042053)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013042053) 

Yoda arrives on Christophsis to relay new orders to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and Ahsoka Tano.

 

Yularen briefly returned to Christophsis aboard his flagship, the *[Resolute](/wiki/Resolute "Resolute")*, to send Tano to the planetary surface aboard a [shuttle](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle"), then withdrew to rendezvous with reinforcements from the Republic Navy. Tano reached Kenobi and Skywalker just as they were preparing defenses for the next droid attack. Due to the continued lack of support from the Republic Navy, Kenobi and Skywalker remained trapped on-world with their troops, unable to comply with Yoda's order to return to Coruscant. Loathsom mounted another strike on the Republic forces, this time utilizing a mobile [deflector shield](/wiki/Deflector_shield "Deflector shield") to maintain a perimeter just beyond his advancing droid troops. The shield rendered the AV-7 Anti-vehicle Cannons useless, forcing the Jedi and clones to devise another strategy.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

While Kenobi and Rex scrambled their men in a last-ditch defense of the city, and Kenobi feigned surrender to buy time for Skywalker and Tano to infiltrate the Separatist lines and destroy the [shield generator](/wiki/Deflector_shield_generator "Deflector shield generator"), exposing droids to renewed barrages from the AV-7 Anti-Vehicle Cannons, and forcing Loathsom to capitulate. The Republic victory coincided with the arrival of naval reinforcements led by Yularen and Yoda, who smashed the Separatist blockade and drove it into retreat. Even as Yularen's fleet deployed infantry reinforcements to aid the invasion force in securing Christophsis, much of the planet remained in ruins.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) The Republic, meanwhile, imprisoned Loathsom on Coruscant for [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason").[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14)

#### Alliance with the Hutt Clan[]

##### Clash at Teth[]

:   "*Kidnapped, Jabba the Hutt's son has been. Negotiate the treaty with Jabba, Obi-Wan will. Find the renegades who hold Jabba's son, your mission will be, Skywalker.*"
:   ―Yoda briefing Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and Ahsoka Tano — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Kidnapped-TCWf.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250404190214)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Kidnapped-TCWf.flac "File:Kidnapped-TCWf.flac"))[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Battle of Teth](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth")
 [![Torrent Company wages a vertical assault to reach the B'omarr Order Monastery on Teth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ATTE_scale_cliff.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013052836) [![Torrent Company wages a vertical assault to reach the B'omarr Order Monastery on Teth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ATTE_scale_cliff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121013052836)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ATTE_scale_cliff.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013052836) 

Torrent Company wages a vertical assault to reach the B'omarr Order Monastery on Teth.

 

All while a number of new battles rocked the Outer Rim,[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Ventress brought the captive Rotta to an abandoned [B'omarr Order Monastery](/wiki/B%27omarr_Order_Monastery "B'omarr Order Monastery") on the [jungle](/wiki/Jungle "Jungle") planet [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth"),[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) located in [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"), and fortified the site with two full [battalions](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") of battle droids.
