After a [scouting](/wiki/Scout "Scout") team of Republic [Advanced Recon Force Scout Troopers](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Force_trooper "Advanced Recon Force trooper") tracked Rotta to Teth, Skywalker and Tano proceeded there with [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") Rex and[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) [Torrent Company](/wiki/Torrent_Company "Torrent Company"),[[104]](#cite_note-Databank:_Cody-104) Rex's command [unit](/wiki/Company "Company") within the Grand Army's famed [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion"),[[105]](#cite_note-Databank:_Rex-105) to rescue the Huttlet. Kenobi, meanwhile, entered into negotiations with Jabba, who granted the Republic a single [planetary rotation](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") to save Rotta and return him safely to Tatooine.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

As the monastery sat perched atop a cliff, Skywalker, Tano, and Torrent Company were forced to mount a [vertical assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth"), relying on [ascension cables](/wiki/Ascension_cable "Ascension cable") and a pair of AT-TE walkers to reach the fortress at the summit. Though they lost one of their AT-TE walkers and endured numerous casualties, the Jedi and clones broke through the Separatist droid defenses and retrieved Rotta from the monastery's detention level. However, Tano discovered that Rotta was severely ill, jeopardizing their chances of delivering him to Tatooine alive. Skywalker suspected Dooku's involvement in the kidnapping, given that both the Republic and the Confederacy sought an alliance with the Hutt Clan.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

Unbeknownst to the Jedi, Ventress used the [protocol droid](/wiki/RA-7_protocol_droid "RA-7 protocol droid") 4-A7 to record Skywalker and Tano as they retrieved Rotta. Ventress transmitted the [holorecording](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") to Dooku, who presented it to Jabba as evidence that the Jedi were responsible for Rotta's abduction. After persuading Jabba to consider joining the Confederacy, Dooku ordered Ventress to recover Rotta so that they could claim credit for his rescue. Marshaling her assault force of battle droids, Ventress mounted a counter-strike on the monastery, swiftly crushing the Republic's last AT-TE walker and remaining assault craft. With no means of escape, Rex, Skywalker, and Tano barricaded themselves inside the monastery's antechamber with Rotta and Torrent Company. While Rex remained behind with Torrent Company to hold off Ventress and her droid infantry, Skywalker and Tano departed with Rotta to find a secondary exit from the monastery.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

Despite their best efforts, Rex and his men were vastly outnumbered, and the battle droids slew all of them save for Rex and five other troopers. The droids held the clone survivors prisoner in the compound's eastern courtyard. Nonetheless, it was not long before Kenobi arrived at Teth with [Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") Cody and a detachment of reinforcements. After punching through the Separatists' aerial [squadrons](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") of [vulture droid starfighters](/wiki/Vulture-class_starfighter "Vulture-class starfighter"), Cody and his soldiers reached the monastery aboard LAAT/i gunships. They and Kenobi provided support for Rex and the survivors of Torrent Company, while Skywalker and Tano narrowly evaded Ventress and escaped with Rotta on board an old spice [freighter](/wiki/G9_Rigger-class_light_freighter "G9 Rigger-class light freighter") called the *[Twilight](/wiki/Twilight "Twilight")*.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

 [![Asajj Ventress duels Obi-Wan Kenobi on Teth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Obi-Wan_vs_Ventress_Teth.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164406) [![Asajj Ventress duels Obi-Wan Kenobi on Teth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Obi-Wan_vs_Ventress_Teth.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120612164406)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Obi-Wan_vs_Ventress_Teth.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164406) 

Asajj Ventress duels Obi-Wan Kenobi on Teth.

 

When Kenobi entered the monastery in search of Skywalker, he instead crossed lightsabers with Ventress. Upon learning that Skywalker had escaped with Rotta, Ventress broke off from her duel with Kenobi and fled the battlefield. Meanwhile, Skywalker and Tano piloted the *Twilight* into orbit of Teth, where Wullf Yularen and his *Venator*-class [Star Destroyer](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer") were battling a Confederate armada of *Munificent*-class star frigates. As the Jedi tried to board Yularen's Star Destroyer, a trio of vulture droids firebombed the [cruiser](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser")'s main hangar. Unable to dock with Yularen's flagship, Skywalker and Tano headed directly to Tatooine aboard the *Twilight*.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

##### Cementing an alliance[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Mission to Jabba's Palace (Clone Wars)](/wiki/Mission_to_Jabba%27s_Palace_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Jabba's Palace (Clone Wars)") and [Raid on Ziro's Palace](/wiki/Raid_on_Ziro%27s_Palace "Raid on Ziro's Palace")

Dooku was not pleased to learn from Ventress that the Jedi had extracted Rotta from Teth, but he continued to manipulate Jabba and the Hutt Clan towards joining the Confederacy. During a holographic report to Dooku, Ventress falsely stated that Skywalker had murdered Rotta before leaving for Tatooine. Using this deception, Dooku convinced Jabba that the Jedi Order intended to eradicate the Hutt Clan. Dooku thus departed from [Jabba's Palace](/wiki/Boba_Fett%27s_Palace "Boba Fett's Palace") to personally kill Rotta, which would ensure he was never reunited with his [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"). All the while, Palpatine used the sudden eruption of the Battle of Teth, along with the several other concurrent engagements in the Rim, to justify a series of new security measures on Naboo.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

On Coruscant, Padmé Amidala—having wanted to meet with Palpatine to discuss Naboo's new security measures—received word of the Jedi's ongoing efforts to return Rotta to Tatooine. Concerned for her husband's safety after learning Jabba blamed him for the kidnapping, she became determined to convince Jabba of the truth and broker the Republic's treaty with the Hutt Clan. Because Jabba was refusing all communication with the Republic, Amidala visited Ziro the Hutt, who lived in a [palace](/wiki/Ziro%27s_Palace "Ziro's Palace") on Coruscant. After Ziro rebuffed her attempt to reopen dialogue between the Hutts and the Republic, Amidala lingered around the palace and witnessed Ziro contact Dooku via hologram. Dooku informed Ziro that thanks to the Sith's web of deceit, Jabba would kill the Jedi when they arrived at his palace on Tatooine, after which the Republic would be forced to arrest Jabba. Accordingly, Ziro would be able to seize his nephew's control of the Hutt Clan. However, Ziro discovered Amidala eavesdropping on the conversation, and on Dooku's advice, he incarcerated Amidala within his palace.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

As Skywalker and Tano arrived over Tatooine with Rotta aboard the *Twilight*, a pair of Confederate [*Rogue*-class Porax-38 starfighters](/wiki/Rogue-class_Porax-38_starfighter "Rogue-class Porax-38 starfighter") [assaulted](/wiki/Mission_to_Jabba%27s_Palace_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Jabba's Palace (Clone Wars)") their freighter, causing them to crash-land in the [Dune Sea](/wiki/Dune_Sea "Dune Sea"). While Skywalker diverted Dooku's attention by engaging him in a lightsaber duel, Tano proceeded with Rotta to Jabba's Palace, but a trio of [IG-100 MagnaGuards](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard") intercepted her outside the compound. Skywalker abandoned his confrontation with Dooku to rescue Tano, but he incorrectly assumed that she was already at Jabba's Palace. Skywalker thus arrived there ahead of his Padawan—much to the ire of Jabba, who still believed that Skywalker had slaughtered his son. With help from Skywalker's [astromech droid](/wiki/R2-series_astromech_droid "R2-series astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), Tano defeated her MagnaGuard assailants and reunited Rotta with his father. In spite of the Jedi's efforts, Jabba remained determined to execute Skywalker and Tano, and he ordered his bounty hunters to do so.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

 [![Padmé Amidala convinces Jabba Desilijic Tiure of the truth, paving the way for a Hutt Clan&ndash;Republic treaty.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Padme_talks_to_Jabba.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013043012) [![Padmé Amidala convinces Jabba Desilijic Tiure of the truth, paving the way for a Hutt Clan&ndash;Republic treaty.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Padme_talks_to_Jabba.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121013043012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Padme_talks_to_Jabba.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013043012) 

Padmé Amidala convinces Jabba Desilijic Tiure of the truth, paving the way for a Hutt Clan–Republic treaty.

 

Back on Coruscant, Amidala was able to send word of her capture to the Republic via her [protocol droid](/wiki/3PO-series_protocol_droid "3PO-series protocol droid"), [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO").[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Clone Commander [Fox](/wiki/Fox "Fox")[[106]](#cite_note-Databank:_Fox-106) immediately responded with a squad of [clone shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper") from the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard"), and they [raided](/wiki/Raid_on_Ziro%27s_Palace "Raid on Ziro's Palace") Ziro's Palace to rescue her. Once Fox and his soldiers had arrested Ziro, Amidala used Ziro's personal [holoprojector](/wiki/Holoprojector "Holoprojector") to contact Jabba, who received her message just as he was about to have Skywalker and Tano killed. Jabba was incensed to learn of Dooku and Ziro's conspiracy to unseat him, but he agreed to end all hostilities with the Jedi. Jabba subsequently signed a [treaty](/wiki/Hutt%E2%80%93Republic_treaty "Hutt–Republic treaty") with the Republic and granted the Grand Army its exclusive, long-awaited access to Hutt Space's supply routes. At the same time, Kenobi finished securing the Republic's victory on Teth and headed to Tatooine with Yoda, so that they could formalize the treaty with Jabba.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23)

The Republic's alliance with the Hutt Clan resulted in a major setback for the Confederacy. Yet, Darth Sidious remained unconcerned, downplaying the impact of the Jedi's victory after Dooku apprised him of the news.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Nonetheless, the treaty also posed problems for the Republic, as making formal treaties with the Hutts ended up legitimizing their businesses,[[107]](#cite_note-Scum_and_Villainy-107) which the treaty also allowed to spread into the Mid Rim.[[108]](#cite_note-HL_3-108) Beyond the cartel lawyers masterfully editing the proposed treaties to give the Hutts unmitigated access to Republic intel,[[107]](#cite_note-Scum_and_Villainy-107) the treaty also saw the Hutts confirm that their organizations would stay out of the war and only work as non-combatants, while the Republic was forced to promise it would not bring the fighting into Hutt territory despite having secured their cooperation[[108]](#cite_note-HL_3-108) and hyperlanes.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) The Republic incarcerated Ziro within the [Judiciary Central Detention Center](/wiki/Republic_Judiciary_Central_Detention_Center "Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center") on Coruscant, and his lengthy sentence caused him to develop a deep resentment toward Amidala.[[4]](#cite_note-Assassin-4)

#### The war reaches Ryloth[]

:   "*Our cities lie in ruins. Our transportation hubs are all but destroyed, so I cannot return home. Our crops burn. The Twi'lek people are* starving*! And they* will *die if no aid comes to them.*"
:   ―Orn Free Taa, the senator of Ryloth, appeals to Toydaria's King Katuunko for aid[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109)

 [![Jedi General Ima-Gun Di was the last survivor of the Republic's initial battle group on Ryloth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/LastStandOfImaGunDi-SL.png/revision/latest?cb=20130506233102) [![Jedi General Ima-Gun Di was the last survivor of the Republic's initial battle group on Ryloth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/LastStandOfImaGunDi-SL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130506233102)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/LastStandOfImaGunDi-SL.png/revision/latest?cb=20130506233102) 

Jedi General Ima-Gun Di was the last survivor of the Republic's initial battle group on Ryloth.

 

The [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") homeworld of [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") became the next major battlefront of the Clone Wars when the Techno Union invaded the planet,[[24]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-24) aiming to pillage its wealth and resources.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46) The Separatist navy installed a [blockade](/wiki/Ryloth_blockade "Ryloth blockade") of [battleships](/wiki/Battleship "Battleship") in orbit of Ryloth, while the Separatist Droid Army subjected the civilian population to a brutal occupation. Besides losing a number of cities and transport hubs, the Twi'leks were cut off from [food](/wiki/Foodstuff "Foodstuff") and relief supplies and thus began to starve. In response, political activist [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla") founded[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109) a [Twi'lek Resistance](/wiki/Twi%27lek_Resistance "Twi'lek Resistance")[[110]](#cite_note-Databank:_Twi'lek_Resistance-110) to combat the Confederate occupation. Jedi General [Ima-Gun Di](/wiki/Ima-Gun_Di "Ima-Gun Di"), Clone Captain [Keeli](/wiki/Keeli "Keeli"), and their unit of soldiers provided aid to Syndulla and his freedom fighters. As [open warfare](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth") engulfed Ryloth, the Separatist blockade eliminated Admiral [Dao](/wiki/Dao "Dao")'s Republic [fleet](/wiki/Dao%27s_fleet "Dao's fleet"), severing the Republic's supply lines to Ryloth and trapping Di, Syndulla, and their men in a canyon alongside many Twi'lek families.[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109)

With Ryloth in dire need of aid, the Jedi High Council prepared a shipment of food and medical supplies for the Twi'leks. Yet, because the Republic's [*Pelta*-class frigates](/wiki/Pelta-class_frigate "Pelta-class frigate") did not have enough range to reach Ryloth, the High Council selected the planet [Toydaria](/wiki/Toydaria "Toydaria") as a suitable staging ground for the blockade runners. Complicating matters was the fact that Toydaria had declared neutrality in the war. As a result, the High Council asked Senator Bail Organa to oversee negotiations on Toydaria, alongside Jar Jar Binks. However, the Separatist navy intercepted the transmission between Organa and the High Council. Dooku thus dispatched Senator [Lott Dod](/wiki/Lott_Dod "Lott Dod") of the Trade Federation to thwart Organa's diplomatic efforts with [King](/wiki/King "King") [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko "Katuunko"), the monarch of the [Toydarians](/wiki/Toydarian "Toydarian").[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109)

Thanks to Dod's intervention, Katuunko publicly [declined](/wiki/The_Matter_of_Using_Toydarian_Territory_to_Aid_the_Shipment_of_Relief_Supplies_to_the_Citizens_of_Ryloth "The Matter of Using Toydarian Territory to Aid the Shipment of Relief Supplies to the Citizens of Ryloth") to have Toydaria sponsor the Republic's humanitarian shipment to Ryloth. However, Katuunko privately agreed to let Organa transfer his supplies from Toydaria to Ryloth. To prevent the Trade Federation from learning of the subterfuge, Binks distracted Dod and his staff at a formal banquet that night, while Organa oversaw the shipment's departure from Toydaria. By that time, the Separatist Droid Army had nearly overrun the Republic's defenses on Ryloth. Di, Keeli, and their men sacrificed their lives so that Syndulla and his comrades could escape from the canyon with their families. Shortly thereafter, the Republic's trio of *Pelta*-class [frigates](/wiki/Frigate "Frigate") penetrated the Confederate blockade and deployed their relief supplies to the Twi'leks. Nevertheless, the Grand Army's inability to provide further military support to the Twi'lek Resistance eroded Syndulla's faith in the Republic.[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109)

Without reinforcements from the Republic, only Syndulla and his Twi'lek Resistance stood against the Separatist occupation of Ryloth. The Twi'leks suffered heavily in a confrontation with the Droid Army, and the Separatists forced the freedom fighters to surrender and disarm themselves. Still, the droid infantry continued to massacre the Twi'lek fighters, leading them to carve out hideouts in the shells of downed Confederate [C-9979 landing craft](/wiki/C-9979_landing_craft "C-9979 landing craft"). Syndulla and his rebels resorted to executing a guerrilla campaign, periodically eliminating battle droid patrols in the region. For the time being, the Twi'leks were left to wage the ongoing Battle of Ryloth on their own.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

 [![King Katuunko aligned Toydaria with the Republic after Yoda defeated Asajj Ventress on Rugosa.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/Mission_to_Rugosa3.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916031047) [![King Katuunko aligned Toydaria with the Republic after Yoda defeated Asajj Ventress on Rugosa.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/Mission_to_Rugosa3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120916031047)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/Mission_to_Rugosa3.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916031047) 

King Katuunko aligned Toydaria with the Republic after Yoda defeated Asajj Ventress on Rugosa.

 

Organa and Binks's determination to help the Twi'leks of Ryloth convinced Katuunko to consider bringing Toydaria into the Republic.[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109) Since the Jedi Order hoped to establish a supply base in the [Toydaria system](/wiki/Toydaria_system "Toydaria system"), Master Yoda sought a [meeting](/wiki/Battle_of_Rugosa "Battle of Rugosa") with Katuunko on the [coral](/wiki/Coral "Coral") moon of [Rugosa](/wiki/Rugosa "Rugosa"). However, Dooku learned of the rendezvous and sent Asajj Ventress to negotiate with the [Toydarian Royal Delegation](/wiki/Toydarian_royal_delegation "Toydarian royal delegation") on behalf of the Confederacy. After a pair of Confederate *Munificent*-class star frigates intercepted his [Republic frigate](/wiki/Consular-class_cruiser_(Charger_c70_retrofit) "Consular-class cruiser (Charger c70 retrofit)"), Yoda reached the surface of Rugosa in an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") alongside his three-man detail from the Coruscant Guard: Lieutenant [Thire](/wiki/Thire "Thire") and troopers [Jek](/wiki/Jek "Jek") and [Rys](/wiki/Rys "Rys").[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87)

To circumvent a political debate with Yoda, Ventress proposed a contest. She would send her best troops to capture Yoda, who would face the challenge of evading apprehension. Katuunko, accordingly, would consider aligning Toydaria with the side of the victor. Although Katuunko was loath to subject Yoda to such a trial, Yoda accepted Ventress's terms and promised to arrive at their location by nightfall. Though they gravely lacked an advantage in numbers, Yoda and his troopers prevailed over Ventress's battalion of battle droids, even after she reneged on her agreement with Katuunko—first by ordering her droids to shoot to kill, and later by deploying droidekas as reinforcements.[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87)

When Katuunko informed Dooku of his desire to join the Republic, Dooku commanded his apprentice to assassinate Katuunko. Yoda and his men arrived just in time to save Katuunko, with Yoda using [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") to halt Ventress's [lightsabers](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress%27s_lightsabers "Asajj Ventress's lightsabers") in mid-air, just [centimeters](/wiki/Centimeter "Centimeter") from Katuunko's throat. Instead of surrendering, Ventress distracted Yoda by detonating pre-planted explosives near Katuunko's starship, the *[Thief's Eye](/wiki/Thief%27s_Eye "Thief's Eye")*. While Yoda's focus was consumed with telekinetically redirecting the incoming rubble, Ventress took the opportunity to escape aboard her solar sailer. In the wake of Yoda's victory, Katuunko formally pledged Toydaria's support to the Republic and agreed to host a base in his system. He and his delegation thereafter departed from Rugosa alongside Yoda and his soldiers.[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87)

#### Rise of the *Malevolence*[]

:   "*This mystery weapon has struck in a dozen systems, and disappeared without a trace.*"  
    "*We cannot afford to lose any more ships, my friends.*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Sheev Palpatine[[25]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-25)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Malevolence Campaign](/wiki/Malevolence_Campaign "Malevolence Campaign")
 [![Grievous's flagship, the Malevolence, tears through Plo Koon's flotilla in the Abregado system.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Battle_of_Abregado.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100111013846) [![Grievous's flagship, the Malevolence, tears through Plo Koon's flotilla in the Abregado system.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Battle_of_Abregado.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20100111013846)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Battle_of_Abregado.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100111013846) 

Grievous's flagship, the *Malevolence*, tears through Plo Koon's flotilla in the Abregado system.

 

The Confederacy military wasted no time in developing new projects for its war machine. One result was the *[Malevolence](/wiki/Malevolence "Malevolence")*,[[25]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-25) a colossal [*Subjugator*-class heavy cruiser](/wiki/Subjugator-class_heavy_cruiser "Subjugator-class heavy cruiser")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) that became the prized flagship of General Grievous. The *Malevolence*'s maiden voyage cut a swath through Republic territory, [striking in several star systems](/wiki/Malevolence_Campaign "Malevolence Campaign") and annihilating all of the Republic ships that it encountered. Key to the battleship's success were its dual [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon"), which disabled enemy starships' deflector shields and the rest of their onboard systems, thereby leaving the targets vulnerable to heavy [turbolaser](/wiki/Turbolaser "Turbolaser") fire. Because the *Malevolence* left behind no witnesses, the Republic citizenry dubbed the unidentified threat Grievous's "mystery weapon," sowing fear throughout the Republic.[[25]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-25)

The Jedi High Council soon sent one of its members, General [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon"), to hunt down Grievous's weapon. Koon and his [flotilla](/wiki/Plo_Koon%27s_fleet "Plo Koon's fleet") of three *Venator*-class Star Destroyers tracked the *Malevolence* to the [Abregado system](/wiki/Abregado_system "Abregado system"), where Dooku and Grievous were overseeing the [heavy cruiser](/wiki/Heavy_cruiser "Heavy cruiser")'s testing. The result of the [ensuing battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Abregado "Battle of Abregado") was identical to those of its predecessors: the *Malevolence* disabled Koon's cruisers with an ion wave, then tore apart the defenseless craft using its array of turbolasers. Most of the remaining personnel who fled aboard escape pods were killed when Grievous sent teams of [B1-series rocket battle droids](/wiki/B1-series_rocket_battle_droid "B1-series rocket battle droid") aboard [*Droch*-class boarding ships](/wiki/Droch-class_boarding_ship "Droch-class boarding ship") after them.[[25]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-25)

Both Chancellor Palpatine and the Jedi Council were reluctant to spare resources on a search for survivors of Koon's fleet. However, Anakin Skywalker and Ahsoka Tano—whose fleet was stationed in the nearby [Bith system](/wiki/Bith_system "Bith system")—took it upon themselves to do so. When they reached the Abregado system aboard the *Twilight*, the only remaining survivors were Koon and Clone Commander [Wolffe](/wiki/Wolffe "Wolffe"), along with Clone Sergeant [Sinker](/wiki/Sinker "Sinker") and trooper [Boost](/wiki/Boost "Boost") of the [104th Battalion](/wiki/104th_Battalion "104th Battalion")'s Wolfpack squad. Skywalker and Tano rescued Koon and the clones, and they escaped from the system aboard the *Twilight*, narrowly avoiding becoming the *Malevolence*'s next victims. Dooku was greatly displeased by Grievous's failure to prevent their escape.[[25]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-25)

With the veil over Grievous's mystery weapon lifted, the Senate commissioned Skywalker and the Republic Navy's [Shadow Squadron](/wiki/Shadow_Squadron "Shadow Squadron") of [Y-wing starfighter](/wiki/BTL-B_Y-wing_starfighter/bomber "BTL-B Y-wing starfighter/bomber") [pilots](/wiki/Clone_trooper_pilot "Clone trooper pilot") to eradicate the *Malevolence*. After the *Malevolence* [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Ryndellia_system "Battle of the Ryndellia system") a Republic medical [convoy](/wiki/Unidentified_convoy "Unidentified convoy") in the [Ryndellia system](/wiki/Ryndellia_system "Ryndellia system"), Skywalker correctly deduced that Grievous's next target was the [Kaliida Shoals Medical Center](/wiki/Kaliida_Shoals_Medical_Center "Kaliida Shoals Medical Center"), a classified Outer Rim [facility](/wiki/Haven-class_medical_station "Haven-class medical station") that was treating over 60,000 wounded clone troopers. Using a [smugglers](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler")' shortcut known as the [Balmorra Run](/wiki/Balmorra_Run "Balmorra Run"), Skywalker, Tano, Koon, and Shadow Squadron barely beat the *Malevolence* to the Republic [medcenter](/wiki/Medcenter "Medcenter"), which sat on the fringes of the [Kaliida Nebula](/wiki/Kaliida_Nebula "Kaliida Nebula"). While Shadow Squadron initiated its [assault](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Kaliida_Nebula "Battle of the Kaliida Nebula") on the *Malevolence*, [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") Nala Se and the rest of her staff began evacuating the medcenter with the help of the [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)"). Yet, they were unable to clear out all of the patients before the *Malevolence* completed its targeting cycle.[[111]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Malevolence-111)

 [![Shadow Squadron intercepts the Malevolence before it can destroy the Kaliida Shoals Medical Center.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Battle_of_Kaliida.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110917201423) [![Shadow Squadron intercepts the Malevolence before it can destroy the Kaliida Shoals Medical Center.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Battle_of_Kaliida.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20110917201423)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Battle_of_Kaliida.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110917201423) 

Shadow Squadron intercepts the *Malevolence* before it can destroy the Kaliida Shoals Medical Center.

 

Shadow Squadron's initial attack on the *Malevolence* claimed the lives of almost half of the unit's twelve-pilot roster. On account of those casualties, Skywalker heeded Tano and Koon's recommendation to abandon their original target of the *Malevolence*'s [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)"). Instead, they concentrated their assault on the heavy cruiser's starboard ion cannon. Their [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") inflicted enough damage to cause the ion cannon to overload when Grievous tried to fire it upon the medcenter. Obi-Wan Kenobi and Wullf Yularen thereafter arrived with a three-cruiser fleet of Star Destroyers, and promptly opened fire on the *Malevolence*. With both the ion cannons and the [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") disabled, Grievous was forced to order the *Malevolence* to retreat, setting course for Confederate [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace").[[111]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Malevolence-111)

The Separatists dispatched a fleet of reinforcements to aid the beleaguered *Malevolence*, but Jedi General [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli")[[112]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-112) and [her own fleet](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli%27s_fleet_group "Luminara Unduli's fleet group")[[113]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_Encyclopedia-113) [intercepted](/wiki/Battle_near_the_Kaliida_Nebula "Battle near the Kaliida Nebula") them before they could reach the Kaliida Nebula. Even without those reinforcements, the *Malevolence* was able to hold its own, since its enormous size enabled it to withstand the Republic fleet's barrage of cannonades. Nevertheless, Dooku and Darth Sidious arranged a trap for Padmé Amidala, sending her to the Kaliida Nebula under the premise of negotiating a treaty between the Republic and the InterGalactic Banking Clan. When Amidala arrived, Grievous pulled her [H-type Nubian yacht](/wiki/H-type_Nubian_yacht "H-type Nubian yacht") aboard the *Malevolence* via a [tractor beam](/wiki/Tractor_beam "Tractor beam"), aiming to take the esteemed senator hostage so as to secure safe passage for the *Malevolence*. The tactic worked as Dooku had predicted, with Skywalker ordering the Republic fleet's [gunnery](/wiki/Gunner "Gunner") teams to stand down in order to protect his wife.[[112]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-112)

While Koon, Tano, and Yularen remained behind to command the fleet, Skywalker and Kenobi mounted a rescue mission to save Amidala. After using the *Twilight* to dock with the *Malevolence*, they rendezvoused with Amidala, who had destroyed her H-type Nubian yacht to delay Grievous. Amidala and Skywalker proceeded to the bridge, where they hot-wired the *Malevolence*'s [navigation computer](/wiki/Navigation_computer "Navigation computer") to secretly input a new destination. Kenobi attempted to sabotage the battleship's hyperdrive, but Grievous intercepted him and chased him to the ship's internal [rail jet](/wiki/Rail_jet "Rail jet"), where Kenobi broke off from their duel. He, Amidala, and Skywalker escaped from the *Malevolence* aboard the *Twilight*, but Grievous pursued with a squadron of vulture droids.[[112]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-112)

It was not long before Skywalker's sabotage came to light. Instead of jumping to hyperspace, the *Malevolence* collided with a nearby moon. Disgraced, Grievous fled from the battlefield aboard his personal [starship](/wiki/Belbullab-22_heavy_starfighter "Belbullab-22 heavy starfighter"), *[Soulless One](/wiki/Soulless_One "Soulless One")*. Thanks to that turn of events, the Republic claimed victory in[[112]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-112) the Battle of the Kaliida Nebula,[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) ending the threat of the *Malevolence*.[[112]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-112) A few months later, Unduli would come face-to-face with Grievous on [Nadiem](/wiki/Nadiem "Nadiem") out in the Outer Rim.[[113]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_Encyclopedia-113) In the mean time, however, Grievous would largely manage to stay out of the Republic's sight, being spotted in the [Balmorra system](/wiki/Balmorra_system "Balmorra system") but then remaining off the Republic's radar for weeks.[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

#### War for resources[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: Incursion on Noomis Riga, [Battle of Khorm](/wiki/Battle_of_Khorm "Battle of Khorm") and Attack on Atraken

:   "*I just received word, Sim—the clones have those clankers surrounded. This latest Separatist incursion will be contained within hours! Once they're done mopping up here, our boys can advance all the way to Ukio. Maybe in time to reopen the old kern route before the harvest. That would be a right boon.*"
:   ―Fond Dachris, to Sim Aloo[[114]](#cite_note-Kernels_Husks-114)

As the conflict ground on, it became apparent the Clone Wars was also a war for resources, given the economic toll using clone troopers and battle droids was. As such, economically important worlds became home to multiple battles.[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) The planet of [Ukio](/wiki/Ukio "Ukio") had left the Republic during the Separatist Crisis,[[100]](#cite_note-Propaganda-100) but it was[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) ultimately taken back[[100]](#cite_note-Propaganda-100) by the Republic at some point; due to its usefulness as a granary, Ukio was of interest to both sides.[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) The farmer [Fond Dachris](/wiki/Fond_Dachris "Fond Dachris") had hope that the Grand Army would claim Ukio shortly after its victory on his own argiworld, [Noomis Riga](/wiki/Noomis_Riga "Noomis Riga"), where clone troopers surrounded attacking battle droids during a Separatist incursion. Noomis Riga suffered several such incursions during the war, with Dachris' fellow farmer [Sim Aloo](/wiki/Sim_Aloo "Sim Aloo") taking advantage of the carnage by making himself a notable ally of the Republic military. He reported the Republic-loyal Dachris as a Separatist sympathizer and murdered him as part of his plan to claim his neighbor's farm and expand his power.[[114]](#cite_note-Kernels_Husks-114)

The Confederacy also cut off agricultural trade routes leading to Coruscant, leaving to entire levels suffering from starvation and, in the minds of the Republic citizenry, justifying their government in striking back against the Confederacy.[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17) [Atraken](/wiki/Atraken "Atraken") and [Khorm](/wiki/Khorm "Khorm") were also sought by the Republic and CIS, as they both were home to natural mineral resources.[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) The [Battle of Khorm](/wiki/Battle_of_Khorm "Battle of Khorm") was fought at some point after the Battle of Abregado.[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) General Skywalker and Clone Commander Wolffe led the Republic in the battle,[[116]](#cite_note-FC_Wolffe-116) while Asajj Ventress was present for the Separatists. During a close encounter between the two,[[117]](#cite_note-WolffeDB-117) Wolffe lost his right eye to Ventress,[[116]](#cite_note-FC_Wolffe-116) which forced him to wear a [cybernetic](/wiki/Cybernetics "Cybernetics") replacement.[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) Atraken, meanwhile, would eventually suffer an brutal attack as the war dragged on. The battle technically ended as a Republic victory, but millions were killed in the fighting, and the whole world was left uninhabitable.[[118]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_4-118)

#### Battle over Rishi Station[]

:   "*All right, listen up. There's only one target of interest in this sector: Kamino. It's the closest thing we clones have to a home. Today we fight for more than the Republic. Today, we fight for all our brothers back home. Understood?*"  
    "*Sir, yes, sir!*"
:   ―Rex and rookie soldiers Echo, Fives, and Hevy on defending Rishi Station — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/RexPepTalk-Rookies.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329120042)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:RexPepTalk-Rookies.flac "File:RexPepTalk-Rookies.flac"))[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Defense of Rishi Station](/wiki/Defense_of_Rishi_Station "Defense of Rishi Station")

Concurrent to a period of escalation for the conflict in the Outer Rim, which forced the Republic to rush out new formations of clones before their training was truly complete and assign them out-of-the-way tracking station jobs, the intelligence-gathering arms of the Republic[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82) and Confederate war machines became sources of contention[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26) over the following [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week"). When Grievous targeted Kamino, he knew that the Grand Army's system of listening posts in the vicinity could impede his efforts. To that end, Grievous dispatched a stealth team of [BX-series droid commandos](/wiki/BX-series_droid_commando "BX-series droid commando") to silence [Rishi Station](/wiki/Rishi_Station "Rishi Station"), a Republic outpost located on a [barren moon](/wiki/Rishi_Moon "Rishi Moon") in the [Rishi system](/wiki/Rishi_system "Rishi system"). Under the cover of a [meteor shower](/wiki/Meteor_shower "Meteor shower"), the droid commandos landed on the moon and [raided](/wiki/Defense_of_Rishi_Station "Defense of Rishi Station") Rishi Station, killing most of the facility's garrison. Sergeant [O'Niner](/wiki/O%27Niner "O'Niner"), the station's lead officer, was among the casualties. The droids then hot-wired the station's all-clear signal, preventing the Republic Navy from learning that Grievous and his fleet were approaching Kamino by way of the Rishi system. In addition, Asajj Ventress infiltrated Kamino's defenses and served as a spy for Grievous, completing the preparations for his invasion. All of this occurred while the [Mud Jumpers](/wiki/Mud_Jumpers "Mud Jumpers") of the Republic's [224th](/wiki/224th_Imperial_Armored_Division "224th Imperial Armored Division") were involved in a [separate campaign](/wiki/Battle_of_Mimban "Battle of Mimban") on the planet [Mimban](/wiki/Mimban "Mimban").[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

 [![Commander Cody, Hevy, and Fives defend Rishi Station from Grievous's second wave of droid infantry.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Rookies2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120919230325) [![Commander Cody, Hevy, and Fives defend Rishi Station from Grievous's second wave of droid infantry.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Rookies2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120919230325)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Rookies2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120919230325) 

Commander Cody, Hevy, and Fives defend Rishi Station from Grievous's second wave of droid infantry.

 

In the aftermath of the Separatists' takeover of Rishi Station, Commander Cody and Captain Rex arrived there on a scheduled inspection of the base and were warned of the danger by a flare used by the remaining Clones. After the droid commandos destroyed their [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle"),[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82) the *[Obex](/wiki/Obex "Obex")*,[[119]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia:_Republic_shuttle-119) Cody and Rex fled from the outpost. They soon encountered the remaining survivors of the earlier attack: troopers [Echo](/wiki/Echo "Echo"), [Hevy](/wiki/Hevy "Hevy"), and [Fives](/wiki/Fives "Fives"). Though the rookie soldiers had barely seen any combat action, Cody and Rex rallied them to retake Rishi Station, and they managed to overpower the squad of droid commandos. Yet, their victory was short-lived. Upon losing contact with the droid commandos, Grievous deployed troop reinforcements to ensure that Rishi Station remained under his control.[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

With time running out, Rex decided that instead of trying to disable the all-clear signal, they should destroy Rishi Station. Though Rex's plan was the nuclear option, the cessation of the beacon would alert the Republic fleet to Grievous's invasion. To destroy Rishi Station, Echo suggested the idea of using the outpost's supply of liquid [tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna"), a highly explosive [fuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel") that served as a heat source during the moon's long winter. While Cody, Fives, and Hevy defended the station's main entrance from the incoming battle droids, Rex and Echo linked a trio of[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82) [PLNK-series power droids](/wiki/PLNK-series_power_droid "PLNK-series power droid"),[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) which contained the liquid tibanna, to a detonation system. When Rex encountered problems with the detonator's handset, Hevy remained behind to repair it, while his comrades escaped to the crags beneath the station. However, Hevy was unable to repair the remote, so he chose to manually activate the explosives.[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

Thanks to Hevy's [sacrifice](/wiki/Death "Death"), the destruction of Rishi Station disabled the alert beacon. Anakin Skywalker, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Wullf Yularen subsequently arrived in the Rishi system with a Republic fleet. Knowing his armada lacked the tactical advantage, Grievous conceded defeat and withdrew his forces from the system. After the battle, Kenobi and Skywalker honored Echo and Fives for their efforts, as well as the late Hevy for his sacrifice. Furthermore, Rex inducted Echo and Fives into the 501st Legion.[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82)

#### Intelligence and counterintelligence[]

:   **Kenobi**: "*Our intelligence has confirmed that Grievous's spies have been intercepting our transmissions.*"
:   **Tano**: "*He must have some sort of secret listening post out there somewhere.*"
:   **Skywalker**: "*That would explain how he's been able to ambush our fleets.*"
:   **Kenobi**: "*Split up your squadrons, Anakin. Find that base and destroy it.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, Ahsoka Tano, and Anakin Skywalker[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Skytop Station campaign](/wiki/Skytop_Station_campaign "Skytop Station campaign")
 [![Though the Republic won the Battle of Bothawui, the loss of R2-D2 posed a major threat to its intelligence system.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Battle_of_Bothawui_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921012952) [![Though the Republic won the Battle of Bothawui, the loss of R2-D2 posed a major threat to its intelligence system.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Battle_of_Bothawui_TCW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120921012952)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Battle_of_Bothawui_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921012952) 

Though the Republic won the Battle of Bothawui, the loss of R2-D2 posed a major threat to its intelligence system.

 

Eventually, the Separatists constructed [Skytop Station](/wiki/Skytop_Station "Skytop Station"), a core ship that they converted into a listening post in the [Ruusan system](/wiki/Ruusan_system "Ruusan system"). Skytop Station plagued the Republic's intelligence network by intercepting various transmissions and acquiring vital data for the Confederacy military.[[120]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids_Guide-120) In the midst of this subterfuge, Grievous achieved a [series of victories](/wiki/Skytop_Station_campaign "Skytop Station campaign") that jeopardized the Republic's foothold in the Outer Rim. He [eliminated](/wiki/Battle_of_Falleen "Battle of Falleen") an entire Republic battle group at the planet [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen_(planet) "Falleen (planet)") on his way to conquer [Bothawui](/wiki/Bothawui "Bothawui"), a strategic world[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26) in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories").[[121]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-121) Rex, Skywalker, and Ahsoka Tano thereafter mobilized a Republic task force in defense of Bothawui.[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26)

During the ensuing [Battle of Bothawui](/wiki/Battle_of_Bothawui "Battle of Bothawui"),[[122]](#cite_note-Databank:_R2-D2-122) Rex outflanked Grievous's flotilla using a squad of AT-TE walkers that he had hidden within Bothawui's [asteroid field](/wiki/Fervse%27dra_asteroid_belt "Fervse'dra asteroid belt"). Skywalker and [Gold Squadron](/wiki/Gold_Squadron_(Galactic_Republic) "Gold Squadron (Galactic Republic)"), a unit of [V-19 Torrent starfighters](/wiki/V-19_Torrent_starfighter "V-19 Torrent starfighter"), quickly pressed their advantage and crippled Grievous's frigates, turning the tide of battle in the Republic's favor. However, when Skywalker attempted to prevent Grievous from escaping aboard *Soulless One*, Skywalker instead lost his personal astromech droid, R2-D2, after debris hit his [Delta-7B interceptor](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker%27s_Delta-7B_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Anakin Skywalker's Delta-7B Aethersprite-class light interceptor"). In spite of Grievous's escape, the Republic forces nonetheless emerged victorious at Bothawui.[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26)

The loss of R2-D2 had potentially catastrophic consequences for the Republic. Since Skywalker had never [wiped](/wiki/Memory_wipe "Memory wipe") R2-D2's [memory](/wiki/Memory_bank "Memory bank"), the droid contained a trove of classified Republic Military data. Unbeknownst to the Republic, the [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Gha Nachkt](/wiki/Gha_Nachkt "Gha Nachkt") found R2-D2 and promised the droid to Grievous. When Skywalker and Tano searched Nachkt's freighter,[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26) the *[Vulture's Claw](/wiki/Vulture%27s_Claw "Vulture's Claw")*,[[123]](#cite_note-Databank:_Nachkt-123) they failed to find R2-D2 amidst Nachkt's wares. Adding to Skywalker's problems was the fact that his replacement astromech, [R3-S6](/wiki/R3-S6 "R3-S6"),[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26) was a spy droid for Grievous.[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124)

Once the Republic's intelligence confirmed the existence of the Confederacy's new listening post, Skywalker received orders from Kenobi to find and eliminate the base. While his fleet scoured a targeted region of space, Skywalker elected to undertake a solo [scouting mission](/wiki/Mission_to_suspected_Confederate_space "Mission to suspected Confederate space") to sweep the area's outer corridor. Yet, once Skywalker and R3-S6 were alone in the former's [Delta-7B interceptor](/wiki/Delta-7B_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7B Aethersprite-class light interceptor"), R3-S6 activated the [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter")'s [homing beacon](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon"), leading Grievous and a pair of warships directly to their location. It was only due to the timely intervention of Rex and Tano, who hurriedly assembled a squad of soldiers and arrived aboard the *Twilight*, that Skywalker narrowly escaped demise at Grievous's hands.[[26]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-26)

As Nachkt brought R2-D2 to Skytop Station, the *Twilight* intercepted a transmission from the missing droid. Rex tracked the signal to Skytop Station's location in the upper [atmosphere](/wiki/Atmosphere "Atmosphere") of[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124) one of the planet [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan")'s three moons.[[120]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids_Guide-120) Although Kenobi ordered him to eradicate Skytop Station without rescuing R2-D2, Skywalker made retrieving his droid one of the [mission's](/wiki/Raid_on_Skytop_Station "Raid on Skytop Station") top priorities. While Rex, Tano, and their strike team planted [thermal detonators](/wiki/Thermal_detonator "Thermal detonator") at the facility's [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor"), Skywalker recovered R2-D2 before Grievous's IG-100 MagnaGuards could abscond with the droid. However, R3-S6 delayed Rex, Tano, and their squad of troopers at the reactor room long enough for Skytop Station's security patrols to confront them.[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124)

 [![Aboard Skytop Station, Ahsoka Tano saves Captain Rex from General Grievous.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/AhsokaSavesRex-DotD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921025524) [![Aboard Skytop Station, Ahsoka Tano saves Captain Rex from General Grievous.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/AhsokaSavesRex-DotD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120921025524)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/AhsokaSavesRex-DotD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921025524) 

Aboard Skytop Station, Ahsoka Tano saves Captain Rex from General Grievous.

 

Though Tano and her allies repelled the battle droids, their troubles were far from over. Grievous ambushed them, murdering most of the clone troopers in the process. Tano subsequently engaged Grievous in a lightsaber duel so that Rex and the other surviving soldier,[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124) [Denal](/wiki/Denal "Denal"),[[120]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids_Guide-120) could finish installing the explosives at the reactor. Once they had done so, Denal and Rex rendezvoused with Skywalker, R2-D2, and the *Twilight* in Skytop Station's main hangar. There, R3-S6 revealed his true allegiances by sealing the exits and activating a trio of vulture droids, thus preventing Rex and Skywalker from aiding Tano in her confrontation with Grievous.[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124)

At Skywalker's behest, Rex activated the explosives at the reactor, plunging Skytop Station on a descent into the moon's lower atmosphere. Once R2-D2 opened the hangar door from an exterior terminal, Tano arrived—having broken off from her duel with Grievous—and escaped with Denal, Rex, and Skywalker aboard the *Twilight*. Before they left the Ruusan system, Skywalker personally retrieved R2-D2, who had eliminated R3-S6. Grievous also escaped, though the loss of Skytop Station became yet another blemish on his career.[[124]](#cite_note-Duel_of_the_Droids-124)

#### Separatist leadership targeted[]

:   "*Gunray's capture could be a serious threat to us, my friend. The viceroy will not last long under Jedi interrogation.*"  
    "*I have already put a plan into action, my lord. My best agent, Asajj Ventress, will infiltrate the Jedi ship and either free Gunray or silence him.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Darth Tyranus — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/SidiousDooku-CoD.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329120343)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:SidiousDooku-CoD.flac "File:SidiousDooku-CoD.flac"))[[125]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-125)

As the Clone Wars entered a stalemate,[[126]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-126) several important members of the Confederacy found themselves in the Republic's crosshairs. One such leader was Nute Gunray, who entered into a brief alliance with Senator [Onaconda Farr](/wiki/Onaconda_Farr "Onaconda Farr") of [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia"). Although Rodia was part of the Republic, the Senate proved too slow to aid the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") population after [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") attacks demolished Rodia's inbound supply ships. Consequently, Farr lost faith in the Republic and accepted Gunray's offer to distribute relief supplies to Rodia. In return, Farr helped Gunray capture Padmé Amidala, against whom Gunray still held a grudge, when she came to Rodia on a [diplomatic visit](/wiki/Mission_to_Rodia "Mission to Rodia"). Though Farr was conflicted about betraying Amidala, he incarcerated his old friend in a local detention tower until Gunray's arrival. However, when Gunray came to collect Amidala, Farr was shocked to learn that Gunray intended to execute her.[[27]](#cite_note-Bombad_Jedi-27)

 [![Padmé Amidala and Onaconda Farr arrested Nute Gunray on Rodia, but the Republic's success did not last.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Gunray_surrounded.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921225318) [![Padmé Amidala and Onaconda Farr arrested Nute Gunray on Rodia, but the Republic's success did not last.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Gunray_surrounded.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120921225318)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Gunray_surrounded.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921225318) 

Padmé Amidala and Onaconda Farr arrested Nute Gunray on Rodia, but the Republic's success did not last.

 

Although Amidala escaped from the detention tower, complications arose when Gunray's battle droids targeted both her and Jar Jar Binks, who had accompanied her to Rodia. Binks enlisted the aid of a [large Kwazel Maw](/wiki/Bogey_(Kwazel_Maw) "Bogey (Kwazel Maw)"), which demolished most of Gunray's droids and his [*Sheathipede*-class transport shuttle](/wiki/Sheathipede-class_transport_shuttle "Sheathipede-class transport shuttle"). Moreover, Gunray's indifference to the Rodians' suffering, as well as his brutal treatment of Amidala, convinced Farr that joining the Confederacy was a mistake. Farr aided Amidala in arresting Gunray on behalf of the Republic, concluding Rodia's dalliance with the Separatists. Sheev Palpatine thereafter sent the Rodians a convoy of much-needed supplies.[[27]](#cite_note-Bombad_Jedi-27)

Under the command of Clone Commander [Gree](/wiki/Gree_(clone_trooper) "Gree (clone trooper)"),[[27]](#cite_note-Bombad_Jedi-27) the [41st Elite Corps](/wiki/41st_Elite_Corps "41st Elite Corps")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) arrived on Rodia to take Gunray into Republic custody. The Jedi High Council dispatched Jedi General Luminara Unduli, alongside Ahsoka Tano, to provide further security for Gunray's transfer to Coruscant, where the viceroy would stand trial. Since Darth Sidious believed that Gunray would not be able to withstand the Jedi's interrogation, Dooku tasked Asajj Ventress with rescuing Gunray. Dooku also paid off Captain [Faro Argyus](/wiki/Faro_Argyus "Faro Argyus"), the leader of the [Senate Commando](/wiki/Senate_Commando "Senate Commando") detail that had been assigned to Gunray's transfer, to assist in the operation.[[125]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-125)

Ventress launched her [assault](/wiki/Rescue_on_the_Tranquility "Rescue on the Tranquility") just as Argyus, Gree, Tano, and Unduli were leaving Rodia with Gunray aboard the Star Destroyer *[Tranquility](/wiki/Tranquility "Tranquility")*. A trio of *Droch*-class boarding ships penetrated the *Tranquility*'s [hull](/wiki/Hull "Hull"), then deployed a droid boarding party that eradicated much of the Elite Corps' [Green Company](/wiki/Green_Company "Green Company"). Ventress proceeded to the *Tranquility*'s detention level, where she engaged in a brief rematch with Tano,[[125]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-125) since the two had previously crossed blades during the Battle of Teth.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Though Argyus, Gree, and Unduli came to Tano's aid and prevented Ventress from escaping with Gunray, Ventress used a cache of explosives that she had planted in the *Tranquility*'s [engine](/wiki/Engine "Engine") room to disrupt all of the cruiser's onboard systems. When Unduli pursued Ventress to the engine room, Ventress nearly overwhelmed her, and it was only thanks to Tano's assistance that Unduli was able to continue their lightsaber duel.[[125]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-125)

As Ventress continued to occupy the Jedi's attention, she signaled Argyus to make his move. Argyus gunned down two of his fellow Senate Commandos who were guarding Gunray, then liberated Gunray from his prison cell. Argyus and Gunray resisted Gree's attempts to stop them and commandeered the *Consular*-class frigate that had transferred Gunray to the *Tranquility*. Similarly, Ventress stole an escape pod and joined them aboard their frigate, though she executed Argyus when he insinuated that he would take full credit for the operation's success. Nevertheless, Unduli was able to transmit the tracking data for Gunray's frigate to fellow Jedi General Kit Fisto, whose fleet was close to Gunray's last known position.[[125]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-125)

 [![Nahdar Vebb and Kit Fisto spearhead an effort to detain Grievous at his private fortress on Vassek's third moon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Vebb_Fisto_Grievous.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924014202) [![Nahdar Vebb and Kit Fisto spearhead an effort to detain Grievous at his private fortress on Vassek's third moon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Vebb_Fisto_Grievous.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120924014202)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Vebb_Fisto_Grievous.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924014202) 

Nahdar Vebb and Kit Fisto spearhead an effort to detain Grievous at his private fortress on Vassek's third moon.

 

Since Fisto was leading the hunt to recapture Gunray, Dooku saw an opportunity to test one of his agents. Because Grievous's recent defeats had undermined Dooku's faith in him, Dooku arranged a test for his best general. Using the homing beacon from Gunray's frigate, Dooku lured Fisto and his forces to Grievous's personal [fortress](/wiki/Grievous%27s_fortress "Grievous's fortress")[[126]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-126) on the [third moon](/wiki/Vassek_3 "Vassek 3") of [Vassek](/wiki/Vassek "Vassek"). The Republic's [Outer Rim Command Center](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Command_Center "Outer Rim Command Center") also monitored Clone Commander [Fil](/wiki/Fil "Fil")[[127]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous_Guide-127) and Jedi Knight [Nahdar Vebb](/wiki/Nahdar_Vebb "Nahdar Vebb"), Fisto's former Padawan, who led a team of troopers to assist in the search for Gunray. Grievous remained unaware of Dooku's plan to reevaluate his performance.[[126]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-126)

Fisto, Vebb, and their soldiers [infiltrated](/wiki/Mission_to_Grievous%27s_castle "Mission to Grievous's castle") Grievous's fortress and eliminated a security detail of battle droids that they incorrectly assumed were protecting Gunray. In lieu of the viceroy, Dooku holographically contacted Fisto and Vebb and offered them an alternative prize. Once they realized that the fortress belonged to Grievous, Fisto and Vebb resolved to capture the elusive general, since Grievous's arrest would be pivotal for the Republic's war effort. Yet, when Grievous returned to his fortress, he proved to be far from easy prey. Grievous temporarily evaded the intruders in his lair, but he was forced to undergo repairs from his [medical droid](/wiki/EV-series_medical_droid "EV-series medical droid"),[[126]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-126) [EV-A4-D](/wiki/EV-A4-D "EV-A4-D").[[128]](#cite_note-Databank:_EV-A4-D-128)

After having his IG-100 MagnaGuards lock down the perimeter, Grievous set about reclaiming the upper hand over his would-be captors. He used his fortress's built-in countermeasures—including an incinerator pit and his pet [roggwart](/wiki/Roggwart "Roggwart"), [Gor](/wiki/Gor "Gor")—to assail Fisto, Vebb, and their soldiers. Fil and the rest of his men perished, but Fisto managed to slay the vicious roggwart. Throughout it all, Vebb displayed a growing willingness to use excessive force in response to Grievous's tactics. Matters came to a head when Fisto sneaked into Grievous's control room, and Vebb refused to follow his former Master inside. Instead, Vebb stayed behind to confront Grievous on his own. Unable to help his former Padawan, Fisto could only watch through the surveillance system as Grievous slaughtered Vebb. Before escaping from the moon aboard his [Delta-7B interceptor](/wiki/Kit_Fisto%27s_Delta-7B_starfighter "Kit Fisto's Delta-7B starfighter"), Fisto dueled Grievous and managed to retrieve the late Vebb's lightsaber, which Grievous had claimed as a trophy. Though Grievous had bested Vebb and the clone troopers, Dooku had expected him to do so, and he was not pleased with Grievous's failure to defeat Fisto.[[126]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-126)

#### Dooku's temporary capture[]

:   **Dooku**: "*I'm confident the situation will rectify itself soon.*"
:   **Kenobi**: "*Soon, you'll be brought to trial by the Senate, and most likely spend a very long time in a cell just like this one.*"
:   **Skywalker**: "*And that's if you're lucky.*"
:   ―On Florrum, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker verify in person that Dooku is in the Ohnaka Gang's custody[[129]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-129)

Dooku was the next Confederate official who became a target for the Republic. As part of a manhunt for the Sith Lord, Anakin Skywalker infiltrated Dooku's current flagship, a [*Munificent*-class star frigate](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_frigate "Count Dooku's frigate"), as it was patrolling the Outer Rim. Skywalker allowed himself to be captured in order to lead his forces to the frigate's location. While Obi-Wan Kenobi liberated Skywalker and helped him detain Dooku, Ahsoka Tano and Captain Rex [besieged](/wiki/Skirmish_at_Vanqor "Skirmish at Vanqor") Dooku's frigate from aboard the *Resolute*. However, Dooku fled from the ongoing battle in his solar sailer, with Kenobi and Skywalker in close pursuit aboard a stolen *Sheathipede*-class transport shuttle. All three of them crash-landed on the planet [Vanqor](/wiki/Vanqor "Vanqor"). Whereas Dooku gained safe passage from the [Ohnaka Gang](/wiki/Ohnaka_Gang "Ohnaka Gang"), a band of pirates, to the nearby world of [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum "Florrum"), Kenobi and Skywalker were left stranded on Vanqor, and Tano had to retrieve them from the planet's surface.[[129]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-129)

 [![Count Dooku, Anakin Skywalker, and Obi-Wan Kenobi all became hostages of the Ohnaka Gang on Florrum.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) [![Count Dooku, Anakin Skywalker, and Obi-Wan Kenobi all became hostages of the Ohnaka Gang on Florrum.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120924044609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) 

Count Dooku, Anakin Skywalker, and Obi-Wan Kenobi all became hostages of the Ohnaka Gang on Florrum.

 

Nevertheless, Dooku had not yet reached safety. The Ohnaka Gang took Dooku hostage on Florrum, and the pirates' leader, [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka"), offered him to the Republic in exchange for a hefty sum of one million [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard"), paid in spice. Before Sheev Palpatine agreed to the deal, the Jedi High Council dispatched Kenobi and Skywalker to Florrum to confirm that Ohnaka and his men indeed had custody of Dooku. However, after the Jedi arrived,[[129]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-129) Ohnaka drugged them and also took them prisoner, intending to ransom them to the Republic for an even larger payday. Unaware of Kenobi and Skywalker's situation, Palpatine dispatched Senator [Kharrus](/wiki/Kharrus "Kharrus") and an escort team from the Coruscant Guard to [deliver](/wiki/Mission_to_Florrum "Mission to Florrum") the spice ransom to Florrum and secure custody of Dooku.[[130]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-130)

Rogue elements within the Ohnaka Gang caused further trouble for the Republic. Ohnaka's lieutenant, [Turk Falso](/wiki/Turk_Falso "Turk Falso"), led a faction of pirates who shot down Kharrus's shuttle over Florrum, hoping to steal the ransom. Kharrus and the shuttle's crew died in the crash, leaving Jar Jar Binks, who was part of the delegation, as the ranking commander for Commander [Stone](/wiki/Stone_(clone_trooper) "Stone (clone trooper)") and his soldiers. By the time Binks, Stone, and their squad reached Ohnaka's [base of operations](/wiki/Hondo%27s_complex "Hondo's complex"), Dooku had escaped. He made his getaway by killing Falso and stealing his[[130]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-130) [*Flarestar*-class attack shuttle](/wiki/Flarestar-class_attack_shuttle "Flarestar-class attack shuttle").[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) Rather than arresting Ohnaka, Kenobi and Skywalker left Ohnaka and his pirates alone. The Jedi departed with Binks and the clones aboard the *Twilight*,[[130]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-130) aboard which the Jedi had traveled to Florrum.[[129]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-129) Whereas Ohnaka and the Jedi parted on good terms,[[130]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-130) Dooku harbored a grudge against Ohnaka.[[131]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-131)

#### Crisis after crisis[]

:   "*Count Dooku, I have located a world in which we can test my… Excuse me,* our *new weapon.*"  
    "*I hope it turns out to be worth the* expense*. You may proceed.*"
:   ―Lok Durd and Dooku on testing the Defoliator on Maridun — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/LokDurd3.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329115510)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:LokDurd3.flac "File:LokDurd3.flac"))[[56]](#cite_note-Defenders_of_Peace-56)

 [![Aayla Secura's fleet suffers damage over Quell.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Battle_of_Quell2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120926003442) [![Aayla Secura's fleet suffers damage over Quell.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Battle_of_Quell2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120926003442)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Battle_of_Quell2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120926003442) 

Aayla Secura's fleet suffers damage over Quell.

 

The [Quell system](/wiki/Quell_system "Quell system") became the next flashpoint of the Clone Wars when a Confederate armada intercepted Jedi General Aayla Secura's [fleet](/wiki/Aayla_Secura%27s_task_force "Aayla Secura's task force") of warships.[[132]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-132) In the resulting [Battle of Quell](/wiki/Battle_of_Quell "Battle of Quell"),[[133]](#cite_note-Databank:_Tano-133) the Separatist frigates pummeled Secura's cruisers with heavy bombardment. Soon, only Secura's flagship was maintaining altitude over the planet [Quell](/wiki/Quell "Quell"). Skywalker, Tano, Captain Rex, and Wullf Yularen arrived aboard the *Resolute* to extract Secura; Clone Commander [Bly](/wiki/Bly "Bly"); and their crew from their doomed vessel. Rex, Skywalker, and Tano brought Secura, Bly, and a few of their troops aboard a *Consular*-class cruiser. Before they could reach the *Resolute*, a vulture droid attack inadvertently enabled their frigate's hyperdrive. The Jedi and clones found themselves on an unexpected detour, and they crash-landed on the remote planet [Maridun](/wiki/Maridun "Maridun"). Yularen was left behind to oversee the Republic's campaign over Quell.[[132]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-132)

Stranded on Maridun, Bly, Rex, Secura, and Tano sought out medical attention for Skywalker, who had suffered critical injuries during the escape from Secura's flagship. They brought Skywalker to a [village](/wiki/Lurmen_village "Lurmen village") of Lurmen pacifists, who treated his wounds.[[132]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-132) Just as Skywalker's condition was improving, the Separatist General [Lok Durd](/wiki/Lok_Durd "Lok Durd") selected Maridun as a test site for the Confederacy's newest weapon. Durd had developed the [Defoliator](/wiki/Defoliator "Defoliator"), a cannon that exterminated organic matter while sparing inorganic subjects, such as battle droids. Durd decided to use the Lurmen colonists as test subjects for[[56]](#cite_note-Defenders_of_Peace-56) his [Defoliator Deployment Tank](/wiki/Defoliator_Deployment_Tank "Defoliator Deployment Tank").[[134]](#cite_note-Databank:_DDT-134)

When Durd came to subjugate the Lurmen, the village's elder, [Tee Watt Kaa](/wiki/Tee_Watt_Kaa "Tee Watt Kaa"), persuaded Bly, Rex, Secura, Skywalker, and Tano to leave in order to avoid a potential crossfire. However, the Jedi and clones returned once they realized that Durd was planning to test the Defoliator on the Lurmen village. In the [skirmish](/wiki/Defense_of_Maridun "Defense of Maridun") that followed, the Jedi and clones used a pair of stolen Separatist shield generators to protect the Lurmen from the Defoliator's incendiary capsules. Yet, after Durd's droid infantry breached the Jedi and clones' defenses, [Wag Too](/wiki/Wag_Too "Wag Too")—the village healer and Watt Kaa's son—convinced other young members of the colony to help defend their home. They succeeded, while Skywalker managed to impair the Defoliator and captured Durd. Nevertheless, Watt Kaa questioned whether it had been worth it for Too and his friends to sacrifice their pacifism for the victory.[[56]](#cite_note-Defenders_of_Peace-56)

Shortly thereafter, a brief but bloody conflict erupted on the [glacial](/wiki/Water "Water") world of [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia"). Both the Republic and the Confederacy maintained bases on Orto Plutonia, which attracted attention from a local [settlement](/wiki/Talz_village "Talz village") of [Talz](/wiki/Talz "Talz"). In an effort to protect their solitude, the Talz [obliterated](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Orto_Plutonia "Skirmish on Orto Plutonia") both the Republic and Separatist outposts on their world. The [Pantorans](/wiki/Pantoran "Pantoran"), who inhabited Orto Plutonia's single moon of [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora"), claimed Orto Plutonia as a protectorate. Consequently, Pantoran Chairman [Chi Cho](/wiki/Chi_Cho "Chi Cho") and Senator [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi") requested a detachment of soldiers to investigate the loss of contact with[[135]](#cite_note-Trespass-135) [Glid Station](/wiki/Glid_Station "Glid Station"),[[136]](#cite_note-Trespass_Guide-136) the Republic base on Orto Plutonia. Rex, Skywalker, and Obi-Wan Kenobi oversaw a [platoon](/wiki/Platoon "Platoon")[[135]](#cite_note-Trespass-135) of Rex's troops, who wore the gear of [cold assault troopers](/wiki/Clone_cold_assault_trooper "Clone cold assault trooper") for the mission.[[137]](#cite_note-Armor_history-137)

 [![Riyo Chuchi establishes a peace accord with Thi-Sen.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Chuchi_peace.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928034702) [![Riyo Chuchi establishes a peace accord with Thi-Sen.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Chuchi_peace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120928034702)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Chuchi_peace.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928034702) 

Riyo Chuchi establishes a peace accord with Thi-Sen.

 

When Kenobi and Skywalker made contact with [Chieftain](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [Thi-Sen](/wiki/Thi-Sen "Thi-Sen") of the Talz, he communicated his desire to peacefully resolve the conflict. Yet, Cho dismissed the Talz as savages, declaring that the [Convention of Civilized Systems](/wiki/Convention_of_Civilized_Systems "Convention of Civilized Systems") did not apply to them. Despite efforts from Chuchi, Skywalker, and Kenobi to find a diplomatic solution, the headstrong Cho insisted on declaring war with the Talz in an effort to exterminate them. [Open hostilities](/wiki/One-Day_War "One-Day War") erupted when the Talz ambushed Cho, Rex, and their troops. Many Talz and clone troopers lost their lives until Chuchi received approval from the [Pantoran Assembly](/wiki/Pantoran_Assembly "Pantoran Assembly") to negotiate an end to the bloodshed.[[135]](#cite_note-Trespass-135)

Despite her youth and inexperience, Chuchi mustered the courage to personally establish a peaceful settlement with Thi-Sen. While Cho succumbed to fatal wounds that he had sustained, Chuchi agreed to cede complete jurisdiction of Orto Plutonia to Thi-Sen and the Talz. Chuchi thereafter departed from Orto Plutonia with Kenobi, Rex, Skywalker, and their troops, leaving the Talz in peace.[[135]](#cite_note-Trespass-135) In light of Cho's death, the Pantorans eventually elected [Baron](/wiki/Baron "Baron") [Papanoida](/wiki/Notluwiski_Papanoida "Notluwiski Papanoida") as their new chairman.[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138) Other cold worlds that saw Republic operations were [Toola](/wiki/Toola "Toola") and [Rhen Var](/wiki/Rhen_Var "Rhen Var"), which both saw the deployment of clone cold assault troopers.[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) At some point, Unduli and Secura teamed up in a [confrontation](/wiki/Confrontation_on_Alzoc_III "Confrontation on Alzoc III") against Ventress on[[113]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_Encyclopedia-113) the frozen planet[[139]](#cite_note-HC_2_Databank-139) [Alzoc III](/wiki/Alzoc_III "Alzoc III"). Ventress would be bested and left in an ice cave the two Jedi managed to collapse,[[113]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_Encyclopedia-113) but she escaped and continued to menace the Republic for some time.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) Unduli and Ventress had many more encounters over the course of the conflict.[[113]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_Encyclopedia-113)

#### The Battle of Ryloth ends[]

:   "*The Twi'leks on that planet can't wait forever, Master. The longer the Techno Union keeps control of Ryloth, the more difficult it'll be to free them.*"  
    "*I agree. We don't have much time.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Mace Windu — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/WeDontHaveMuchTime-StormOverRyloth.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329120716)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:WeDontHaveMuchTime-StormOverRyloth.flac "File:WeDontHaveMuchTime-StormOverRyloth.flac"))[[24]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-24)

 [![As the Resolute distracts the Separatist blockade, Ahsoka Tano's squadrons outmaneuver Mar Tuuk's armada.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/MargSablcloseup.png/revision/latest?cb=20121004234048) [![As the Resolute distracts the Separatist blockade, Ahsoka Tano's squadrons outmaneuver Mar Tuuk's armada.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/MargSablcloseup.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121004234048)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/MargSablcloseup.png/revision/latest?cb=20121004234048) 

As the *Resolute* distracts the Separatist blockade, Ahsoka Tano's squadrons outmaneuver Mar Tuuk's armada.

 

The Techno Union continued to subjugate Ryloth, and Wat Tambor gained an appointment as the [emir](/wiki/Emir_of_Ryloth "Emir of Ryloth") of the conquered world.[[140]](#cite_note-Databank:_Tambor-140) The Republic Senate finally authorized an invasion force from the Grand Army to liberate the Twi'lek homeworld, reopening Ryloth as a Republic battlefront. Skywalker, Tano, and Wullf Yularen received the task of eliminating Confederate Captain [Mar Tuuk](/wiki/Mar_Tuuk "Mar Tuuk")'s orbital blockade of Ryloth. The Republic's first assault on the blockade failed, since Tuuk's fleet obliterated the Star Destroyer *[Redeemer](/wiki/Redeemer "Redeemer")* and forced Skywalker's other warships, the *[Defender](/wiki/Defender "Defender")* and the *Resolute*, to retreat from the [Ryloth system](/wiki/Ryloth_system "Ryloth system"). Tano also suffered a devastating blow to her morale when she lost an entire unit of clone pilots, [Blue Squadron](/wiki/Blue_Squadron_(Galactic_Republic) "Blue Squadron (Galactic Republic)"), as part of her first command position.[[24]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-24)

Skywalker and Tano's next strategy had better results. Since the *Defender* had sustained heavy damages, Skywalker sacrificed the cruiser by personally ramming it into Tuuk's [*Lucrehulk*-class Battleship](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_battleship "Lucrehulk-class battleship"). Tuuk fled from his [command ship](/wiki/Command_ship "Command ship") just prior to its demise, thereby ceding command of the blockade to the six frigates' [OOM command battle droids](/wiki/OOM_command_battle_droid "OOM command battle droid"). The ensuing chaos enabled the *Resolute* to return to the Ryloth system. Tano angled the *Resolute*'s ventral hull toward the enemy blockade in order to lure its droid commanders into a trap. Once the frigates moved in, Tano launched several squadrons of starfighters from the *Resolute* and bombarded the frigates, leaving the blockade in disarray.[[24]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-24)

Thanks to Skywalker and Tano's efforts, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu were able to safely enter Ryloth's atmosphere with a [force](/wiki/Ryloth_invasion_fleet "Ryloth invasion fleet") of three *Acclamator*-class transgalactic military [assault ships](/wiki/Assault_ship "Assault ship") containing the invasion force. However, a Separatist encampment in the city of [Nabat](/wiki/Nabat "Nabat") precluded Kenobi and Windu from landing their forces on the surface. From Nabat, the [T-series tactical droid](/wiki/T-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "T-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") [TX-20](/wiki/TX-20 "TX-20") targeted the Republic assault ships with aerial barrages from ground-based[[141]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-141) [J-1 proton cannons](/wiki/J-1_proton_cannon "J-1 proton cannon").[[69]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-69) Windu withdrew the transports to a higher altitude until Kenobi, Commander Cody,[[141]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-141) and the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion")'s[[104]](#cite_note-Databank:_Cody-104) [Ghost Company](/wiki/Ghost_Company "Ghost Company") could eliminate the proton cannons in Nabat. Once there, troopers [Boil](/wiki/Boil "Boil") and [Waxer](/wiki/Waxer "Waxer") befriended [Numa](/wiki/Numa "Numa"), a young Twi'lek orphan who had lost her parents when the Separatists stormed Nabat. With Numa's help, Kenobi and Ghost Company disabled the proton cannons and also rescued Nabat's Twi'lek residents, whom TX-20 had been using as living shields to protect his encampment from attack.
