Once freed, the Twi'leks mobbed TX-20 and destroyed him in retaliation for his subjugation of their home.[[141]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-141)

Ghost Company's liberation of Nabat allowed Windu and his transports to use the city as a landing zone.[[141]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-141) While Skywalker and Tano defeated the remnants of the Confederate blockade and secured the space around Ryloth, Kenobi freed more Twi'lek villages from the Techno Union's occupation. Kenobi soon retook the [Jixuan desert](/wiki/Jixuan_desert "Jixuan desert"), bringing Ryloth's southern hemisphere under Republic control. In response to the Republic's rising victories, Wat Tambor entrenched the majority of his droid infantry within the capital of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City"). It fell to Windu and Commander Ponds to secure Lessu and apprehend Tambor. However, a unit of Armored Assault Tanks inflicted severe casualties to Windu's [Lightning Squadron](/wiki/Lightning_Squadron "Lightning Squadron") during an ambush at a canyon outside of Lessu. Because the Grand Army could not spare any reinforcements, Windu decided to enlist the help of Cham Syndulla and his Twi'lek Resistance.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

 [![Cham Syndulla rallies the combined forces of Lightning Squadron and his Twi'lek Resistance to retake Lessu.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/Syndulla_charge.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005170757) [![Cham Syndulla rallies the combined forces of Lightning Squadron and his Twi'lek Resistance to retake Lessu.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/Syndulla_charge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121005170757)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/Syndulla_charge.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005170757) 

Cham Syndulla rallies the combined forces of Lightning Squadron and his Twi'lek Resistance to retake Lessu.

 

When Windu sought him out, Syndulla still had reservations about working with the Republic, since the Grand Army had previously been unable to aid the Twi'lek Resistance. Syndulla also lacked trust in Ryloth's senator, [Orn Free Taa](/wiki/Orn_Free_Taa "Orn Free Taa"), due to their political rivalry before the war. Yet, Syndulla changed his mind when Dooku ordered Tambor to plunder what he could from the Twi'lek villages, then exterminate everything else. In doing so, Dooku hoped to use Ryloth's demise as a political message about the ramifications of a Republic victory.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

Ponds and Lightning Squadron witnessed Tambor's firebombing campaign firsthand, as [*Hyena*-class Droid Bombers](/wiki/Hyena-class_Droid_Fighter/Bomber "Hyena-class Droid Fighter/Bomber") targeted all villages within range of Lessu, even those that were filled with innocent civilians. Skywalker and Tano concentrated their efforts on eliminating the bombers, but there were too many for their squadrons to handle. Tambor's ruthlessness reminded Syndulla and Taa of their common desire: achieving liberty for Ryloth. Under Windu's mediation, Syndulla promised not to exploit the situation for political power. Taa, meanwhile, agreed to Syndulla's stipulation to preserve Ryloth's independence, by ensuring that the Grand Army refrained from a post-invasion occupation of Ryloth. With that, Syndulla merged his forces with those of Windu, and the new allies organized a joint assault on Lessu.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

Although Dooku ordered him to withdraw from Ryloth, Tambor delayed his departure to maximize the amount of plunder that he could seize from the Twi'leks. As a result, Windu and Advanced Recon Force troopers [Razor](/wiki/Razor "Razor") and [Stak](/wiki/Stak "Stak") infiltrated one of Tambor's inbound [Multi-Troop Transports](/wiki/Multi-Troop_Transport "Multi-Troop Transport") to gain passage across Lessu's [plasma bridge](/wiki/Plasma_bridge "Plasma bridge"), which was the only means of reaching the capital. Once Razor and Stak reactivated the bridge, Syndulla led his Twi'lek freedom fighters and the Republic clone troopers—riding [blurrgs](/wiki/Blurrg "Blurrg") and [All Terrain Reconnaissance Transports](/wiki/All_Terrain_Reconnaissance_Transport "All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport"), respectively—as they charged into Lessu. While Syndulla oversaw the ground campaign, Windu arrested Tambor, who had lingered too long and was thus abandoned when his own tactical droid, [TA-175](/wiki/TA-175 "TA-175"), left aboard his shuttle. Despite Tambor's presence in Lessu, Dooku ordered TA-175 to have their *Hyena*-class bombers lay waste to the capital. However, Skywalker and Tano intercepted the bombers in their Delta-7B interceptors and wiped them out before they reached Lessu. Afterward, Tambor agreed to unconditionally surrender to Syndulla and Windu.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

The Battle of Lessu, as it became known,[[142]](#cite_note-Homecoming-142) finally brought the lengthy Battle of Ryloth to an end. Now free once more, the Twi'leks held a parade in Lessu to celebrate their victory, with Syndulla, Taa, and Windu in attendance.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46) Syndulla and Windu's accomplishments at Lessu led them to become part of Twi'lek folklore, with songs naming their attack the Hammer of Ryloth.[[142]](#cite_note-Homecoming-142)

### Year two (21 BBY–20 BBY)[]

#### The Blue Shadow Virus[]

:   "*Where's the antidote, Vindi?*"  
    "*You mistake my role, Jedi. My job was to manufacture a plague, not to cure it.*"  
    "*We don't have time for games.*"  
    "*Yes, kill me now and spare these old bones the Blue Shadow's dire embrace! Because once the first droid breaks out of that laboratory, all Naboo is doomed!*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Nuvo Vindi after the latter's LEP servant droid detonates a viral bomb in the underground laboratory[[89]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-89)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Raid on Nuvo Vindi's laboratory](/wiki/Raid_on_Nuvo_Vindi%27s_laboratory "Raid on Nuvo Vindi's laboratory")

In the Mid Rim, Naboo became the site of the Confederacy's foray into biological warfare.[[143]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-143) Operating out of a secret Trade Federation [laboratory](/wiki/Trade_Federation_laboratory "Trade Federation laboratory")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) beneath Naboo's [eastern swamps](/wiki/Eastern_swamps "Eastern swamps"), Doctor [Nuvo Vindi](/wiki/Nuvo_Vindi "Nuvo Vindi") succeeded in weaponizing the [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus "Blue Shadow Virus"), a lethal waterborne plague with no known cure, as an airborne strain. He also manufactured [viral bombs](/wiki/Viral_bomb "Viral bomb") to release the plague to key Republic star systems. When the Royal Naboo Security Forces discovered a patrol of Vindi's battle droids, Padmé Amidala and Jar Jar Binks returned to help Queen [Neeyutnee](/wiki/Neeyutnee "Neeyutnee") and Captain [Gregar Typho](/wiki/Gregar_Typho "Gregar Typho") investigate the potential incursion. Amidala and Binks traced the battle droids' point of origin to the eastern swamps, where Vindi's forces captured them.[[143]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-143)

 [![Ahsoka Tano, Captain Rex, and Padmé Amidala contain the Blue Shadow Virus within Nuvo Vindi's laboratory.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/BlueShadowVirus.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002221140) [![Ahsoka Tano, Captain Rex, and Padmé Amidala contain the Blue Shadow Virus within Nuvo Vindi's laboratory.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/BlueShadowVirus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121002221140)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/BlueShadowVirus.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002221140) 

Ahsoka Tano, Captain Rex, and Padmé Amidala contain the Blue Shadow Virus within Nuvo Vindi's laboratory.

 

In response, Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano led a [raid](/wiki/Raid_on_Nuvo_Vindi%27s_laboratory "Raid on Nuvo Vindi's laboratory") on Vindi's laboratory to rescue Amidala and Binks, as well as prevent Vindi from escaping with his cache of bombs. Captain Rex and the clone units[[143]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-143) [Calm Tree](/wiki/Calm_Tree "Calm Tree"), [Snow Wolves](/wiki/Snow_Wolves "Snow Wolves"), and [Wildfire](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire")[[144]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus_Guide-144) provided tactical support for the Jedi's operation. After saving Amidala and Binks, Skywalker aided Kenobi in apprehending Vindi. In addition, the Republic task force's cadre of [clone ordnance specialists](/wiki/Clone_ordnance_specialist "Clone ordnance specialist") managed to disarm Vindi's entire supply of viral bombs before he could release the plague to Naboo.[[143]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-143) Kenobi and Skywalker thereafter escorted Vindi to Naboo's capital, [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed"), to stand trial for his crimes.[[89]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-89)

However, the crisis was not over. Vindi's personal [LEP-series service droid](/wiki/LEP-series_service_droid "LEP-series service droid") had secretly absconded with one of the vials containing the Blue Shadow Virus. The droid used a viral bomb to release the plague within the laboratory. While Kenobi and Skywalker [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Iego "Mission to Iego") to the distant planet Iego to retrieve a potential cure, Amidala and Binks worked with Rex, Tano, and their men to eliminate the laboratory's remaining battle droids. If the droids escaped from the sealed compound, they would spread the outbreak to the rest of Naboo. Although the Blue Shadow Virus infected everyone save for Binks, the Republic personnel managed to eradicate the battle droids.[[89]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-89)

During their journey to Iego, Kenobi and Skywalker deactivated the Separatists' laser web over the planet, liberating the inhabitants from their confinement to the planetary surface. The two Jedi also obtained a sample of [reeksa](/wiki/Reeksa "Reeksa") root, which was used to cure Amidala, Rex, Tano, and their men from the Blue Shadow Virus, bringing the incident to a close.[[89]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-89)

#### Victories and sacrifices[]

:   "*The setback at Felucia has affected our efforts in the whole sector. It'll take weeks before we can…*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[145]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-145)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and their soldiers wait for Plo Koon's gunships to extract them from Felucia.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090926192328) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and their soldiers wait for Plo Koon's gunships to extract them from Felucia.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20090926192328)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090926192328) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker, and their soldiers wait for Plo Koon's gunships to extract them from Felucia.

 

Felucia, a [jungle](/wiki/Tree "Tree") world in the Outer Rim, became a frequent battlefront throughout the war.[[146]](#cite_note-Databank:_Felucia-146) Early on, Felucia's strategic location on the [Perlemian Trade Route](/wiki/Perlemian_Trade_Route "Perlemian Trade Route")[[147]](#cite_note-Galactic_Defense-147) led it to become the site of a [campaign](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia "First Battle of Felucia") between the Confederacy and the Republic. Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano attempted to repel a Separatist military presence from the world, but the battle droids overwhelmed their detachment of clone troopers, led by Commander Cody and Captain Rex. Once Commander Wolffe arrived with a fleet of Star Destroyers and breached the Confederacy's orbital [blockade](/wiki/Felucia_blockade "Felucia blockade"), Plo Koon and clone pilot [Warthog](/wiki/Warthog "Warthog") rushed through the opening with a squadron of LAAT/i gunships.[[145]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-145)

From their starfighters, Koon and Warthog escorted the gunships to the surface, where they extracted Cody, Kenobi, Rex, Skywalker, and their men from the Republic's main staging area. Before leaving Felucia, the gunships also picked up Tano and her patrol of soldiers from elsewhere in the jungle. Though Tano initially refused to retreat, she and her soldiers boarded the gunships right before droid reinforcements compromised their position. The Republic's defeat at Felucia disrupted the Grand Army's efforts in the surrounding [sector](/wiki/Sector "Sector") of space. Tano also faced disciplinary action from the Jedi High Council for disobeying her orders to evacuate from Felucia.[[145]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-145)

[Devaron](/wiki/Devaron "Devaron"), another forested planet, soon became one of the war's next battlefields.[[148]](#cite_note-Cargo_of_Doom-148) Working for Darth Sidious, the bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") collaborated with fellow mercenary [Cato Parasitti](/wiki/Cato_Parasitti "Cato Parasitti") to [steal](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Jedi_Temple "Raid on the Jedi Temple") a [holocron](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") from the Jedi Archives' [Holocron Vault](/wiki/Holocron_Vault "Holocron Vault") on Coruscant.[[145]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-145) Bane then targeted Jedi Master [Bolla Ropal](/wiki/Bolla_Ropal "Bolla Ropal"), the keeper of the Jedi Order's [Kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal "Kyber memory crystal"), a [device](/wiki/Memory_crystal "Memory crystal") that documented all known [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") throughout the galaxy. At Sidious's request, Nute Gunray provided Bane with the Trade Federation's armada of *Munificent*-class star frigates, which Bane used to [besiege](/wiki/Battle_of_Devaron "Battle of Devaron") Ropal's [Republic outpost](/wiki/Devaron_New_Republic_outpost "Devaron New Republic outpost") on Devaron. By the time Rex, Skywalker, Tano, and Wullf Yularen arrived in the [Devaron system](/wiki/Devaron_system "Devaron system") aboard the *Resolute*, Bane had already overrun the Republic base and had abducted Ropal, bringing him aboard [his command ship](/wiki/Cad_Bane%27s_Munificent-class_star_frigate "Cad Bane's Munificent-class star frigate"). The *Resolute* tore through the majority of Bane's frigates and also disabled his command ship's hyperdrive, trapping Bane in-system. Yet, when Ropal refused to use the holocron to access the memory crystal, Bane had his crew of battle droids [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") Ropal to death.[[148]](#cite_note-Cargo_of_Doom-148)

Due to a lack of resources, Rex, Skywalker, and Tano repurposed a trio of AT-TE walkers as unorthodox boarding craft for their assault force, consisting of [Execute Battalion](/wiki/Execute_Battalion "Execute Battalion") and [Carnivore Battalion](/wiki/Carnivore_Battalion "Carnivore Battalion"). Once the Jedi and clones had infiltrated his command ship, Bane lured them into an ambush with his droid infantry on the frigate's gunnery deck. Bane further separated Tano from her allies and took her hostage, using her as leverage to force Skywalker to open the Kyber memory crystal. Because the frigate's [self-destruct sequence](/wiki/Self-destruct_mechanism "Self-destruct mechanism") was active, Rex, Skywalker, Tano, and their detachment commandeered a shuttle and fled from the doomed frigate. Bane, still in possession of the holocron and the memory crystal,[[148]](#cite_note-Cargo_of_Doom-148) stowed away on their shuttle by killing trooper Denal and stealing his [armor](/wiki/Phase_I_clone_trooper_armor "Phase I clone trooper armor").[[149]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force_Guide-149) Once aboard the *Resolute*, Bane seized a V-19 Torrent starfighter and jumped to hyperspace before Skywalker and Tano could apprehend him.[[150]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-150)

 [![Working for Darth Sidious, the bounty hunter Cad Bane became a recurring menace to the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Bane_and_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20130415020831) [![Working for Darth Sidious, the bounty hunter Cad Bane became a recurring menace to the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Bane_and_Sidious.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130415020831)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Bane_and_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20130415020831) 

Working for Darth Sidious, the bounty hunter Cad Bane became a recurring menace to the Jedi Order.

 

Following his victory at Devaron, Bane continued his work for Sidious and set out to abduct four Force-sensitive children who were listed in the Kyber memory crystal. After [kidnapping](/wiki/Mission_to_Glee_Anselm "Mission to Glee Anselm") the [Nautolan](/wiki/Nautolan "Nautolan") [Zinn Toa](/wiki/Zinn_Toa "Zinn Toa") on the planet [Glee Anselm](/wiki/Glee_Anselm "Glee Anselm"), Bane [captured](/wiki/Second_mission_to_Rodia "Second mission to Rodia") [Wee Dunn](/wiki/Wee_Dunn "Wee Dunn") in Rodia's [Kay-Tap square](/wiki/Kay-Tap_square "Kay-Tap square"), thwarting Kenobi's efforts to stop him. However, Skywalker and Tano [intercepted](/wiki/Attempted_kidnapping_of_Roo-Roo_Page "Attempted kidnapping of Roo-Roo Page") Bane before he could snatch a third child, [Roo-Roo Page](/wiki/Roo-Roo_Page "Roo-Roo Page") of the [Gungans](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan"), in [Jan-gwa city](/wiki/Jan-gwa_city "Jan-gwa city") on Naboo. Bane endured a brief tenure in Republic custody, ending when he led Kenobi and Mace Windu into a [trap](/wiki/Mission_to_Black_Stall_Station "Mission to Black Stall Station") on [Black Stall Station](/wiki/Black_Stall_Station "Black Stall Station"), his base of operations. Though Bane escaped, Kenobi and Windu recovered the stolen holocron from his possession. Furthermore, Skywalker and Tano [rescued](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Skywalker_and_Tano) "Mission to Mustafar (Skywalker and Tano)") Dunn and Toa from Sidious's [secret facility](/wiki/Darth_Sidious%27s_secret_facility "Darth Sidious's secret facility") on the [volcanic](/wiki/Magma "Magma") world of [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). Nevertheless, the Jedi Order remained unaware that Sidious was behind the entire ordeal.[[150]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-150)

In spite of its earlier setback at Felucia,[[145]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-145) the Republic maintained a presence in the [Felucia system](/wiki/Felucia_system "Felucia system") in the form of the [Felucia Medical Station HCTFF2](/wiki/Felucia_Medical_Station_HCTFF2 "Felucia Medical Station HCTFF2"), a *Haven*-class medical station. Yet, it was devoid of any countermeasures to defend itself, making it an [easy target](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Felucia_medical_station "Destruction of the Felucia medical station") for a small Confederate flotilla. When Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano investigated the loss of contact with Felucia Medical Station HCTFF2,[[151]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-151) a Separatist [automated vulture droid deployment station](/wiki/Automated_vulture_droid_deployment_station "Automated vulture droid deployment station")[[152]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters_Guide-152) launched a squadron of vulture droids. The droid starfighters attacked the Jedi's [T-6 shuttle](/wiki/T-6_shuttle "T-6 shuttle"), forcing them to crash-land on Felucia. While there, the Jedi helped the mercenaries [Sugi](/wiki/Sugi_(bounty_hunter) "Sugi (bounty hunter)"), [Embo](/wiki/Embo "Embo"), [Seripas](/wiki/Seripas "Seripas"), and [Rumi Paramita](/wiki/Rumi_Paramita "Rumi Paramita") [defend](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Felucia "Skirmish on Felucia") a [Felucian](/wiki/Felucian "Felucian") [farming](/wiki/Farm "Farm") village from extortion by the Ohnaka Gang, which hoped to pillage the [farmers](/wiki/Farmer "Farmer")' [nysillin](/wiki/Nysillin "Nysillin") crops.[[151]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-151)

#### Battle of Malastare[]

:   "*We need that treaty signed so we can gain access to the fuel reserves here on Malastare. Without it, our armies shall be vulnerable.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine reminds Nakha Urus of the necessity of a treaty between the Republic and the Dugs[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Battle of Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare")
 [![During the Battle of Malastare, the Republic detonates Sionver Boll's electro-proton bomb.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911234804) [![During the Battle of Malastare, the Republic detonates Sionver Boll's electro-proton bomb.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120911234804)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911234804) 

During the Battle of Malastare, the Republic detonates Sionver Boll's electro-proton bomb.

 

Concurrent to a Republic offensive, one of the longest and fiercest campaigns of the Clone Wars was[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153) the [Battle of Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare").[[154]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-154) In collaboration with [Doge](/wiki/Doge "Doge") [Nakha Urus](/wiki/Nakha_Urus "Nakha Urus") and his [Dug](/wiki/Dug "Dug") soldiers, Skywalker and Mace Windu led a battle group to safeguard the planet [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare")—whose [fuel](/wiki/Malastarian_fuel "Malastarian fuel") industry was vital to the Republic's war machine and ensuring the continuation of the Republic's offensive—from a Confederate incursion. However, an enormous detachment from the Separatist Droid Army came close to conquering Malastare. Desperate to ensure a Republic victory, Sheev Palpatine authorized the use of the [electro-proton bomb](/wiki/Electro-proton_bomb "Electro-proton bomb"),[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153) an experimental weapon that Doctor [Sionver Boll](/wiki/Sionver_Boll "Sionver Boll") had developed[[155]](#cite_note-Databank:_Boll-155) to disable only mechanical subjects. The electro-proton bomb generated an electromagnetic pulse that rendered all of the Confederacy's battle droids inert. The bomb's detonation zone also produced a massive sinkhole that engulfed some of the Republic's AT-TE walkers and command crews, requiring a rescue effort.[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153)

However, the crater was not the only byproduct of the electro-proton bomb. The blast also awoke a [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Unidentified_Zillo_Beast "Unidentified Zillo Beast"), a member of a colossal [species](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast") that had been thought to be extinct. The Zillo Beast proved to be impervious to everything from blasterfire to Skywalker's [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber"). Because of an ancient enmity between the Dugs and the Zillo Beasts, Urus and[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153) his [Dug Council](/wiki/Dug_Council "Dug Council")[[156]](#cite_note-Aliens_of_the_Galaxy-156) demanded that the Republic help them exterminate the creature. Yet, Windu was adamant against doing so, as the creature could be the last of its kind. Windu's actions strained the Republic's diplomatic relations with the Dugs, since the Grand Army still needed access to Malastare's fuel. In order to appease Urus, Skywalker and Windu used Republic [RX-200 *Falchion*-class assault tanks](/wiki/RX-200_Falchion-class_assault_tank "RX-200 Falchion-class assault tank") to non-lethally immobilize the Zillo Beast, making it appear as though the creature was dead. As a result, Urus and his council signed a [treaty](/wiki/Treaty_of_Malastare "Treaty of Malastare") that provided the Republic with exclusive access to Malastare's fuel reserves.[[153]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-153)

In the wake of the Battle of Malastare, Palpatine ordered Skywalker and Windu to transport the Zillo Beast to Coruscant for study. Palpatine ordered Boll to synthesize the creature's highly durable scales to supplement a new iteration of [clone trooper armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor"). However, the Zillo Beast escaped from the[[154]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-154) [Republic Science and Technical Center](/wiki/Republic_Science_and_Technical_Center "Republic Science and Technical Center")[[157]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Guide-157) and [wreaked havoc](/wiki/Zillo_Beast_incident "Zillo Beast incident") across Coruscant, inflicting massive property damage and sowing terror among the populace. Unable to subdue the creature, the Jedi and their clone troopers were forced to kill the Zillo Beast.[[154]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-154)

#### Second Battle of Geonosis[]

:   "*What I worry about is the way this war seems to be drawing out with no end in sight.*"  
    "*Which it is why it is crucial that our invasion of Geonosis meets with success.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Ki-Adi-Mundi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/NoEndInSight-LaPR.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328195706)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:NoEndInSight-LaPR.flac "File:NoEndInSight-LaPR.flac"))[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Mission to Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia "Mission to Cato Neimoidia"), [Engagement near Dorin](/wiki/Engagement_near_Dorin "Engagement near Dorin"), [Second Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis"), [Second occupation of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_occupation_of_Geonosis "Second occupation of Geonosis") and [Skirmish aboard TB-73](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_TB-73 "Skirmish aboard TB-73")

It was not long before the Clone Wars returned to Geonosis. Though the Republic had occupied the desert world since the war's outset, the Grand Army's pan-galactic war effort required that much of Geonosis's occupying forces be distributed elsewhere. Thanks to the Republic's waning attention, the Confederacy was able to re-establish a major presence on Geonosis.[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) Archduke Poggle the Lesser oversaw the construction of a series of new battle droid [factories](/wiki/Factory "Factory") to expand the ranks of the Separatist Droid Army.[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28) Poggle's [primary foundry](/wiki/Geonosis_primary_droid_foundry "Geonosis primary droid foundry") earned substantial investments from the Trade Federation and the InterGalactic Banking Clan. During a [visit](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia "Mission to Cato Neimoidia") to Lott Dod's [palace](/wiki/Great_Vaults_of_Cato_Neimoidia "Great Vaults of Cato Neimoidia") on [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"), Padmé Amidala discovered a [hologram disc](/wiki/Hologram_disc "Hologram disc") with the factory's coordinates and stole it from the Banking Clan's senator, [Rush Clovis](/wiki/Rush_Clovis "Rush Clovis"). The Republic and the Jedi High Council subsequently learned of the existence of Poggle's new droid foundries.[[158]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-158)

 [![Ki-Adi-Mundi, Ahsoka Tano, Anakin Skywalker, and their combined forces finally reach Point Rain.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101226090521) [![Ki-Adi-Mundi, Ahsoka Tano, Anakin Skywalker, and their combined forces finally reach Point Rain.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20101226090521)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101226090521) 

Ki-Adi-Mundi, Ahsoka Tano, Anakin Skywalker, and their combined forces finally reach Point Rain.

 

Already, the Confederacy's total supply of battle droids far outnumbered the Republic's clone troopers, with Count Dooku claiming that the ratio was as high as one hundred to one.[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87) Hoping to halt the Geonosians' production of new battle droids, the Grand Army committed an immense Jedi-led invasion force to retaking Geonosis. Since Poggle had barricaded himself in his primary foundry, the Jedi mounted a three-pronged assault on the facility's [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield") generator. Jedi General [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi") and Clone Commander [Jet](/wiki/Jet "Jet") led the northernmost strike, while Obi-Wan Kenobi and Commander Cody oversaw the central charge. Anakin Skywalker and Ahsoka Tano—fresh from [routing](/wiki/Engagement_near_Dorin "Engagement near Dorin") Confederate forces near the planet [Dorin](/wiki/Dorin "Dorin")—spearheaded the southward strike with Captain Rex. Wullf Yularen commanded the Republic Navy's efforts, including other areas of the planet-wide campaign.[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28)

As the [Second Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") began,[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) the Geonosian defenses intercepted the majority of the Republic's LAAT/i gunships. Only Cody and his detachment of AT-TE walkers managed to reach [Point Rain](/wiki/Point_Rain "Point Rain"), the Republic's staging area near the ray shield generator, where Cody organized his walkers in a defensive formation. The Geonosians' [LR1K sonic cannons](/wiki/LR1K_sonic_cannon "LR1K sonic cannon") and *Nantex*-class starfighters grounded the rest of the Republic's gunships. Kenobi was severely wounded when his [gunship](/wiki/Bad_Kitty "Bad Kitty") went down, and Cody had to send troopers Waxer and Boil to rescue him and trooper [Trapper](/wiki/Trapper_(clone_trooper) "Trapper (clone trooper)"), the transport's only other survivor. Mundi also sustained injuries when his [gunship](/wiki/Separatist_Nightmare "Separatist Nightmare") crashed, but he and Jet cut through a cave of Geonosian soldiers, where their squad of [clone flametroopers](/wiki/Clone_flametrooper "Clone flametrooper") used [flamethrowers](/wiki/Flamethrower "Flamethrower") to overwhelm the Geonosians. Rex, Skywalker, Tano, and their troops obliterated an enormous canyon barricade of battle droids and rendezvoused with Jet, Mundi, and their men.[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28)

As Cody and Kenobi continued to defend Point Rain from oncoming waves of Geonosian soldiers, Mundi and Skywalker combined their forces and pushed onward to reinforce their comrades. At the same time, Yularen was able to spare a single squadron of Y-wing starfighters to provide aerial support for Mundi and Skywalker's advance. Consequently, the Jedi and clones were able to secure Point Rain. For the final stage of their operation, Skywalker and Tano led a small squad of troopers through the ray shield, and they used a volley of [Electro Magnetic Pulse grenades](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse_grenade "Electromagnetic pulse grenade") to disable the Geonosians' J-1 proton cannons. Once they had done so, Cody moved in with a detail of AT-TE walkers and eliminated the shield generator. The ray shield dissipated, allowing Rex, Mundi, and the main body of troops to land there aboard their gunships. The remaining Geonosians surrendered, thus ending the first phase of the Republic's invasion.[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28)

While Kenobi, Mundi, and the other wounded troops returned to the Republic fleet for medical treatment,[[28]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-28) Rex, Skywalker, and Tano undertook the next phase of the invasion: crippling Poggle's main droid foundry. Luminara Unduli; her Padawan, [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"); and Commander Gree brought in infantry reinforcements to support Skywalker's assault. However, a single bridge was the only means of crossing the chasm that isolated Poggle's factory from the surrounding area. Since the bridge formed a natural bottleneck, the Republic's clone troopers would be completely exposed during their advance on the foundry. As a result, Unduli had Offee memorize the entire labyrinth of catacombs beneath the facility. While Offee and Tano infiltrated the foundry from the catacombs below, Unduli and Skywalker collaborated with Gree and Rex to lead a frontal assault on the facility as a diversionary tactic. Yet, though the droid factory was operating at only half-capacity, Poggle and his tactical droid, [TX-21](/wiki/TX-21 "TX-21"), had already amassed ten garrisons of new troops that were ready for deployment.[[159]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-159)

 [![At the main droid foundry's reactor, TX-21 intercepts Ahsoka Tano and Barriss Offee with a super tank.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Geonosis-ReactorBattle.png/revision/latest?cb=20120901032910) [![At the main droid foundry's reactor, TX-21 intercepts Ahsoka Tano and Barriss Offee with a super tank.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Geonosis-ReactorBattle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120901032910)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Geonosis-ReactorBattle.png/revision/latest?cb=20120901032910) 

At the main droid foundry's reactor, TX-21 intercepts Ahsoka Tano and Barriss Offee with a super tank.

 

As Unduli, Skywalker, and their soldiers made headway against the foundry's droid defenses, Poggle allowed TX-21 to deploy twenty units of their newest creation: the [super tank](/wiki/Separatist_super-tank_prototype "Separatist super-tank prototype"). The super tanks' ray shields enabled them to withstand barrages from the Republic's AV-7 Anti-Vehicle Cannons. In return, the super tanks launched a devastating volley of missiles, inflicting heavy casualties to the Republic troops. Gree and Rex led their soldiers into retreat, thereby drawing the super tanks onto the bridge across the chasm. Skywalker and Unduli climbed across the underside of the bridge, planting thermal detonators on their way to the other side. Once they had reached the factory, Skywalker and Unduli used the explosives to collapse the bridge, plunging the super tanks into the abyss.[[159]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-159)

Meanwhile, Offee and Tano reached the foundry's reactor via the catacombs, but TX-21 intercepted them with a super tank and a squad of Geonosian soldiers. Though Tano destroyed TX-21, the Geonosians purloined her and Offee's supply of thermal detonators. Unable to devise another means of eliminating the reactor, Offee and Tano commandeered the super tank and fired upon the reactor. Their attack generated a chain of explosions that ruptured the foundry's internal structure, bringing it plummeting to the ground.[[159]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-159)

Although Unduli accepted Offee's fate, Skywalker was unwilling to let go of his own pupil, and he frantically joined his troops' search for the lost Padawans. Trapped with Offee in the wreckage of their super tank, Tano used a [power cell](/wiki/Power_cell "Power cell") to boost her comlink's reception, leading their Masters to their location. As a result, Unduli and Skywalker were able to rescue Offee and Tano from the mounds of debris. While the main body of troops continued their cleanup efforts,[[159]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-159) Offee and Tano returned to the fleet for temporary recuperation.[[58]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-58)

As part of its continued campaign on Geonosis, the Grand Army eradicated other key Geonosian droid factories. Yet, Poggle remained at large, since he had escaped from his main foundry prior to its fall. Kenobi, who had recovered from his earlier injuries, joined Unduli in leading the manhunt for Poggle. As a sandstorm brewed, Unduli and trooper [Buzz](/wiki/Buzz "Buzz") tracked Poggle to the [Progate Temple](/wiki/Progate_Temple "Progate Temple"), the headquarters of the Geonosians' secret queen, [Karina the Great](/wiki/Karina_the_Great "Karina the Great"). Karina's minions—in truth, [undead](/wiki/Zombie "Zombie") Geonosians who were being reanimated by her [brain worms](/wiki/Brain_worm "Brain worm")—killed Buzz and abducted Unduli, dragging her into the catacombs beneath the temple. Once the sandstorm had abated, Commander Cody, Kenobi, and Skywalker took a squad of troopers into the catacombs to rescue Unduli. However, the undead Geonosians took advantage of the tunnels' labyrinthine layout to deal casualties to Kenobi and Skywalker's search party.[[58]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-58)

Eventually, Cody Kenobi, Skywalker, and their remaining soldiers reached Karina's throne room, where Poggle had incarcerated Unduli. Despite Kenobi's attempt at negotiation, Karina refused to submit to Republic law. Instead, Karina had Poggle give Unduli a brain worm that would control her mind. Before the brain worm could infect Unduli, Cody and his soldiers turned their headlamps on Karina and the Geonosians, temporarily blinding them. Skywalker freed Unduli from her restraints, and together they handcuffed Poggle and brought him with them as they retreated with the rest of their comrades. Cody and his men eliminated the tunnel's supports on their way out, burying Karina underneath piles of rubble and killing her. Cody, Unduli, Kenobi, Skywalker, and their soldiers managed to escape with Poggle from the Progate Temple just before it collapsed.[[58]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-58) With that, the Second Battle of Geonosis ended in a Republic victory, starting the [second occupation of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_occupation_of_Geonosis "Second occupation of Geonosis").[[160]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-160)

 [![Barriss Offee kills Lieutenant Trap of Tango Company after a Geonosian brain worm infects him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Barriss_stabs_Trap.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091205084245) [![Barriss Offee kills Lieutenant Trap of Tango Company after a Geonosian brain worm infects him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Barriss_stabs_Trap.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20091205084245)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Barriss_stabs_Trap.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091205084245) 

Barriss Offee kills Lieutenant Trap of Tango Company after a Geonosian brain worm infects him.

 

Around the same time as the Republic's successful recapture of Geonosis, Mace Windu oversaw a [campaign](/wiki/Defense_of_Dantooine "Defense of Dantooine") on the planet [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine "Dantooine"). His soldiers sustained numerous injuries, thus requiring relief supplies from a [medical station](/wiki/Ord_Cestus_medical_station "Ord Cestus medical station") near the planet [Ord Cestus](/wiki/Ord_Cestus "Ord Cestus"). Since it was imperative for the Jedi to escort Poggle to Coruscant, Offee and Tano personally embarked on the assignment of picking up the medical shipment from the Ord Cestus medcenter. Kenobi, Mundi, Skywalker, and Unduli separately departed aboard a *Venator*-class Star Destroyer to transport Poggle to Coruscant. Complicating matters was the fact that a Geonosian brain worm infected trooper [Scythe](/wiki/Scythe "Scythe") of [Tango Company](/wiki/Tango_Company "Tango Company"), the troop detail that was escorting Offee and Tano aboard their *Pelta*-class frigate, *[TB-73](/wiki/TB-73 "TB-73")*.[[160]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-160)

Before long, Scythe had infected most of his fellow soldiers with the brain worms. Under the parasites' mind control, the clone troopers gunned down *TB-73*'s clone pilots and activated the bridge's security shields, thereby gaining control of the frigate. Offee and Tano learned of the infection when troopers [Edge](/wiki/Edge "Edge") and [Ox](/wiki/Ox "Ox") [attacked](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_TB-73 "Skirmish aboard TB-73") them in the ship's mess hall. Lieutenant [Trap](/wiki/Trap "Trap"), Tango Company's commanding officer, also opened fire at the Padawans, and Offee killed him in self-defense. In order to contain the parasites aboard their frigate, Offee went to disable the engines, while Tano contacted Kit Fisto, who was overseeing the Ord Cestus medcenter, to warn him of the outbreak. However, Scythe and his comrades intercepted Offee near the reactor room and infected her with a brain worm. With Offee gone, Tano was now the only uninfected person aboard *TB-73*.[[160]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-160)

When Offee confronted her, Tano briefly crossed lightsabers with her friend before escaping to the frigate's ventilation shafts. Meanwhile, after learning of the outbreak from Tano, Skywalker violently interrogated Poggle and learned that the brain worms were susceptible to subzero conditions. Consequently, Tano ruptured *TB-73*'s coolant system, and the intense cold neutralized the brain worms that were controlling the clone troopers. Tano was just in time, as *TB-73* arrived out of hyperspace a short distance away from the medcenter. Although Offee attacked Tano before she could reverse *TB-73*'s engines, a pair of [Republic tugboats](/wiki/TUG-314 "TUG-314") used their tractor beams to reduce the frigate's speed, narrowly preventing a collision with the medcenter. With the brain worms contained, Fisto and his staff provided treatment to Offee, Tano, and the surviving members of Tango Company, guaranteeing a full recovery for all of them.[[160]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-160)

#### Hunt for Grievous[]

:   "*It's time somebody finally put an end to that monster.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker, on General Grievous — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Monster-GI.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328195447)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Monster-GI.flac "File:Monster-GI.flac"))[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29)

 [![Grievous's capture of Eeth Koth prompted the Jedi Order to launch a manhunt for the cyborg general.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/Make_Demands_SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20190319004143) [![Grievous's capture of Eeth Koth prompted the Jedi Order to launch a manhunt for the cyborg general.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/Make_Demands_SWD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20190319004143)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/Make_Demands_SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20190319004143) 

Grievous's capture of Eeth Koth prompted the Jedi Order to launch a manhunt for the cyborg general.

 

Even though the Republic's victories outnumbered its defeats, the Separatist Droid Army continued to make advances in the Outer Rim Territories,[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29) and, following the Second Battle of Geonosis, both sides effectively began to play a game of "cat and mouse" with each other.[[161]](#cite_note-Beginning_of_the_Clone_Wars-161) Soon, Grievous began to specifically target members of the Jedi High Council,[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84) including General [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth").[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29) Deep in the Outer Rim,[[162]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue_Guide-162) while Koth and his [fleet](/wiki/Eeth_Koth%27s_fleet "Eeth Koth's fleet") were investigating [attacks on hyperspace routes](/wiki/Attacks_on_hyperspace_routes "Attacks on hyperspace routes"),[[161]](#cite_note-Beginning_of_the_Clone_Wars-161) Grievous and his [*Recusant*-class Commerce Guild destroyer](/wiki/Recusant-class_light_destroyer "Recusant-class light destroyer") launched an [assault](/wiki/Capture_of_Eeth_Koth "Capture of Eeth Koth") on Koth's flagship,[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29) the [*Steadfast*](/wiki/Steadfast_(Venator-class) "Steadfast (Venator-class)").[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) Grievous then boarded the *Steadfast* with a strike team of BX-series droid commandos, which swiftly overwhelmed the Star Destroyer's detachment of clone troopers.[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29) While Koth ordered Captain [Lock](/wiki/Lock_(Clone_Captain) "Lock (Clone Captain)")[[162]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue_Guide-162) and his troops to evacuate from the *Steadfast*, Koth dueled Grievous aboard the bridge, and he nearly bested Grievous in lightsaber combat despite an arm injury. However, Grievous's IG-100 MagnaGuards electrocuted Koth, allowing Grievous to subdue the Jedi Master and take him hostage.[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29)

When Grievous broadcast his capture of Koth to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, Koth used hand signals to inform the Jedi High Council of his location: the [Saleucami system](/wiki/Saleucami_system "Saleucami system"). Jedi Generals [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia"), Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Anakin Skywalker volunteered to lead the ensuing operation to capture Grievous and rescue Koth. While Wullf Yularen and a Republic armada [assailed](/wiki/Battle_of_Saleucami "Battle of Saleucami") Grievous's fleet above Saleucami, Kenobi and Commander Cody lured Grievous onto their [*Arquitens*-class light cruiser](/wiki/Arquitens-class_light_cruiser "Arquitens-class light cruiser"). With Kenobi dueling Grievous as a diversion, Gallia, Skywalker, Captain Rex, and a squad of troopers arrived aboard an [*Eta*-class shuttle](/wiki/Eta-class_shuttle "Eta-class shuttle") and boarded Grievous's light destroyer to save Koth. Yet, Grievous had anticipated the Republic's tactics and had accordingly delegated command of his flagship to his tactical droid, [TV-94](/wiki/TV-94 "TV-94"). Still, Gallia and Skywalker destroyed TV-94 and his droid commandos aboard the bridge, then freed Koth from his [containment field](/wiki/Containment_field "Containment field") there.[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29)

Aboard Kenobi's light cruiser, things were not going as planned. Kenobi cut down Grievous's MagnaGuards, but neither Kenobi nor Grievous were able to maintain the advantage during their subsequent duel. Grievous soon headed back to the light cruiser's [airlock](/wiki/Airlock "Airlock"), where Cody and three of his men intercepted him. Grievous evaded their attempts to subdue him, then ordered his destroyer's crew to open fire on the light cruiser's engines. The ensuing barrages destabilized the cruiser just as Kenobi, Cody, and their soldiers followed Grievous into the airlock. Grievous engaged in a short rematch with Kenobi and also briefly dueled Gallia, who had come to aid Kenobi's efforts. Yet, when the airlock ruptured, all of the combatants were forced to contend with the breach into the [vacuum](/wiki/Vacuum "Vacuum") of space. While Grievous slipped away, Gallia helped Cody, Kenobi, and the other remaining trooper climb onto the enemy destroyer.[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29)

Grievous boarded a C-9979 troopship to reach Saleucami's surface, forcing Cody, Gallia, and Kenobi to suspend their pursuit of him. Instead, they joined Koth, Rex, and Skywalker aboard their shuttle to withdraw from Grievous's destroyer. Nevertheless, Grievous soon faced ramifications from targeting Kenobi's light cruiser in spite of its close proximity to his flagship. When the cruiser exploded, the debris collided with Grievous's [landing craft](/wiki/Landing_craft "Landing craft"), sending it crashing to Saleucami and forcing Grievous and his crew to transfer to the escape pods. Thanks to that turn of events, the Republic task force refocused its objectives. While Gallia escorted Koth to a medical frigate for treatment, Skywalker and Yularen stayed to complete the fleet's efforts against the remnants of the Confederate armada. Simultaneously, Kenobi headed to Saleucami's surface with Cody, Rex, and a troop contingent to track down the elusive Grievous.[[29]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-29)

On Saleucami, Grievous and his battle droids discovered that their escape pod's [transmitter](/wiki/Transmitter "Transmitter") had not survived the crash, thereby preventing them from contacting their fleet in orbit. Since only one of the other escape pods had survived, Grievous and his crew headed to its location, trekking across Saleucami's farmlands. Meanwhile, after inspecting the C-9979 landing craft's crash site, Kenobi divided his forces. While Rex took a small squad—consisting of 501st troopers [Hardcase](/wiki/Hardcase "Hardcase"), [Jesse](/wiki/Jesse "Jesse"), and [Kix](/wiki/Kix "Kix")—aboard [BARC speeders](/wiki/BARC_speeder "BARC speeder") to scour Saleucami's wetlands for Grievous, Cody and Kenobi remained with their main force of AT-TE walkers to continue the search on the dry territory.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's troop contingent mounts a last-ditch effort to capture Grievous on Saleucami.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/First_Battle_of_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100105142806) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's troop contingent mounts a last-ditch effort to capture Grievous on Saleucami.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/First_Battle_of_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20100105142806)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/First_Battle_of_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100105142806) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi's troop contingent mounts a last-ditch effort to capture Grievous on Saleucami.

 

During the course of Rex's patrol, a pair of droid commandos took a potshot at him, missing his [heart](/wiki/Heart "Heart") by only two inches. Once Hardcase and Jesse had gunned down the droid [snipers](/wiki/Sniper "Sniper"), they and Kix brought Rex to a [nearby farmstead](/wiki/Lawquane%27s_Farm "Lawquane's Farm") that the Lawquane family owned. [Suu Lawquane](/wiki/Suu_Lawquane "Suu Lawquane") agreed to let Rex spend the night in their barn to recover from his condition. After Kix, the squad's [medic](/wiki/Medic "Medic"), dressed his wound with a [bacta bandage](/wiki/Bacta_patch "Bacta patch"), Rex reluctantly let his men resume the search without him, ceding command of the unit to Jesse. As dusk became night, Rex met Suu's husband: Cut Lawquane, a clone trooper who had deserted from the Grand Army. Despite their conflicting ideologies, Rex gradually found common ground with Lawquane based on their dedication to protect those whom they cared about. For Rex, those were his comrades within the Grand Army; for Lawquane, those were his and Suu's two children, [Jek](/wiki/Jek_Lawquane "Jek Lawquane") and [Shaeeah](/wiki/Shaeeah_Lawquane "Shaeeah Lawquane").[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84)

Meanwhile, Hardcase, Jesse, and Kix headed for the C-9979 troopship's final escape pod with Cody, Kenobi, and their forces. Both groups converged on the site just as Grievous arrived there with his own squad of battle droids. After having the escape pod's crew signal his fleet for an extraction from the surface, Grievous marshaled his battle droids in a defense of their position. Though Kenobi engaged Grievous in yet another duel, he was unable to stop Grievous from climbing aboard a *Sheathipede*-class shuttle and reaching his fleet in orbit of Saleucami. Similarly, the Republic fleet failed to intercept Grievous before he departed from the system. Consequently, Kenobi's repeated attempts to detain Grievous ended in frustration.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84)

Back at the Lawquane farmstead, another of the escape pods from the C-9979 landing craft caused trouble for Lawquane and his family. A unit of droid commandos had crashed in an escape pod near the family's homestead, and Jek and Shaeeah inadvertently reactivated all twenty of the lethal droids. While Suu took their children upstairs to take cover, Lawquane entrusted Rex with being the last line of defense for his family. Lawquane, meanwhile, engaged the droid commandos in direct combat when they converged on his homestead. Due to their combined efforts, Lawquane and Rex were able to defeat the droids. The next morning, Rex went to rendezvous with Kenobi and the main body of troops before they departed from Saleucami. Before leaving, Rex promised not to report Lawquane's whereabouts to his superior officers, having reached a better understanding of the former soldier.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-84)

#### Mandalore's fragile neutrality[]

:   "*We mean to* save *your people!*"  
    "*You will turn our planet into a military target, which will bring the war to us. Mandalore* must *remain a neutral system!*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Satine Kryze debate the ramifications of a Republic occupation of Mandalore[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163)

In addition to propagating unrest within the Republic citizenry,[[164]](#cite_note-Lightsaber_Lost-164) the Clone Wars caused an increase in crime throughout the galaxy, especially as the Jedi Order devoted its concentration to the Republic's war effort.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Many star systems became determined to preserve their neutrality from both the Republic and the Confederacy. As a result, over 1,500 systems coalesced into the [Council of Neutral Systems](/wiki/Council_of_Neutral_Systems "Council of Neutral Systems"), a body that advocated for their continued neutrality from the war. Eventually, the council gained a new leader: [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"), who ruled the planet [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") through a pacifistic regime[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48) known as the [New Mandalorians](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians").[[165]](#cite_note-Databank:_New_Mandalorians-165) Yet, Kryze attracted criticism when rumors spread that she was assembling an army for the Confederacy.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48) In truth, the real conspirators were Dooku and Darth Sidious,[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163) who entered into an alliance with the [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch"), a [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") splinter group that was bent on reviving Mandalore's warrior culture. The Death Watch's leader was [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla"), who—as the [governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") of Mandalore's single moon, [Concordia](/wiki/Concordia "Concordia")—pretended to be Kryze's ally while conspiring with Dooku to end her rule.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48)

 [![Pre Vizsla reveals himself as the leader of the Death Watch and duels with Obi-Wan Kenobi on Concordia.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) [![Pre Vizsla reveals himself as the leader of the Death Watch and duels with Obi-Wan Kenobi on Concordia.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20100130031114)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) 

Pre Vizsla reveals himself as the leader of the Death Watch and duels with Obi-Wan Kenobi on Concordia.

 

The Death Watch drew the Republic's attention when [one](/wiki/Unidentified_Death_Watch_saboteur "Unidentified Death Watch saboteur") of its members [assaulted](/wiki/Attack_on_a_Republic_cruiser "Attack on a Republic cruiser") a Republic cruiser, then committed suicide rather than submit to questioning. In response, the Jedi High Council sent Kenobi to investigate Mandalore's potential ties to the Separatists. Kryze, who was old friends with Kenobi, aided his investigation, as did Mandalore's prime minister, [Almec](/wiki/Almec "Almec"). After a [Death Watch bomber](/wiki/Death_Watch_bomber "Death Watch bomber") [demolished](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Memorial_Shrine "Attack on the Memorial Shrine") the [Memorial Shrine](/wiki/Memorial_Shrine "Memorial Shrine") within Mandalore's capital city[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48) of [Sundari](/wiki/Sundari "Sundari"),[[166]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot_Guide-166) the bomber threw himself from a balcony to avoid being captured by Kenobi. Kenobi and Kryze thereafter accompanied the late bomber's body to Concordia, where Vizsla received them.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48)

Kenobi's continuing investigation led him to the Death Watch's [secret base](/wiki/Deathwatch_hideout "Deathwatch hideout") within the Concordian [mines](/wiki/Mining "Mining"), where two Death Watch soldiers [overwhelmed](/wiki/Fight_on_Concordia "Fight on Concordia") him. Only Kryze's intervention saved Kenobi from dying in a rock crusher. While attempting to escape from the base, Kenobi and Kryze came across Vizsla, who revealed himself as Death Watch's leader. Vizsla used the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber"), an ancient weapon dating back to the Old Republic, to engage Kenobi in a lightsaber duel. However, Vizsla proved unable to defeat the Jedi Master, and Kenobi absconded from Concordia with Kryze.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48) Afterward, Kryze resolved to plead her case before the Galactic Senate,[[167]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-167) and Kenobi joined Skywalker, Commander Cody, Captain Rex, and a squad of clone soldiers in providing protection for her voyage to Coruscant.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-48)

Unbeknownst to Kryze, another Death Watch agent was part of her inner circle of advisors. Senator [Tal Merrik](/wiki/Tal_Merrik "Tal Merrik"),[[167]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-167) who represented the planet [Kalevala](/wiki/Kalevala "Kalevala") in the [Mandalore system](/wiki/Mandalore_system "Mandalore system"),[[168]](#cite_note-Databank:_Kalevala-168) smuggled a trio of deadly [assassin probes](/wiki/SD-K4_assassin_droid "SD-K4 assassin droid") onto Kryze's star liner,[[167]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-167) the *[Coronet](/wiki/Coronet "Coronet")*.[[169]](#cite_note-Databank:_Coronet-169) In the [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Coronet "Skirmish aboard the Coronet") that followed, Cody, Rex, and Skywalker destroyed the first assassin probe in the *Coronet*'s cargo hold, but a second one slipped past them and reached the dining chambers, where Kenobi protected Kryze and her retinue. Even after their destruction, both assassin probes deployed an array of minuscule [SD-K4a mini-assassin droids](/wiki/SD-K4a_mini-assassin_droid "SD-K4a mini-assassin droid"), which wreaked havoc on the Jedi and clones, as well as Kryze's contingent of [Mandalorian Protectors](/wiki/Journeyman_Protector "Journeyman Protector"). Once he and his comrades eliminated the majority of the probe killers, Skywalker learned from the *Coronet*'s [cargo manifest](/wiki/Cargo_manifest "Cargo manifest") that a Republic senator had approved the shipment containing the assassin probes. Merrik's ties to the Death Watch finally came to light when Kenobi questioned him and the other senators—Onaconda Farr, Orn Free Taa, and [Kin Robb](/wiki/Kin_Robb "Kin Robb")—who were Kryze's guests aboard the *Coronet*.[[167]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-167)

Although Rex destroyed the third and final assassin probe, Merrik remained at large. Merrik took Kryze hostage and slew all of the *Coronet*'s bridge crew, then requested reinforcements from Vizsla. Once the *Coronet* dropped out of hyperspace, a trio of *Droch*-class boarding ships arrived to cover Merrik's escape. The boarding craft perforated the *Coronet*'s hull and disgorged B2 super battle droids, which went head-to-head with the clone troopers and royal guards in the star liner's hallways. However, Merrik had rigged the *Coronet*'s engines with explosives, and he used both those and Kryze as leverage to reach one of the boarding ships, even as Kenobi pursued him and the captive Kryze there. Kryze disarmed Merrik and pilfered his blaster, but neither she nor Kenobi were willing to kill Merrik with so many lives at stake. Skywalker nonetheless intervened, murdering Merrik and recovering the detonator for his explosives. Cody, Rex, and their men finished routing the Separatist boarding party, thereby ensuring a safe conclusion to the *Coronet*'s eventful journey.[[167]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-167)

 [![Satine Kryze struggles to persuade the Republic Senate to halt a potential occupation of Mandalore.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/KryzeJerecTestimony-DuchessOfMandalore.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214213) [![Satine Kryze struggles to persuade the Republic Senate to halt a potential occupation of Mandalore.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/KryzeJerecTestimony-DuchessOfMandalore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120907214213)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/KryzeJerecTestimony-DuchessOfMandalore.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214213) 

Satine Kryze struggles to persuade the Republic Senate to halt a potential occupation of Mandalore.

 

Even though Kryze had safely reached Coruscant, Vizsla continued to collaborate with the Confederacy to seize control of Mandalore. The Republic Senate was about to [vote](/wiki/Mandalore_Defense_Resolution "Mandalore Defense Resolution") on whether to send a military force to stabilize Mandalore. Since the Mandalorians were not in favor of a Republic occupation, Vizsla and Dooku theorized that such a situation would cause Mandalore's population to view the Death Watch as heroic liberators. To that end, Palpatine had his agents alter a holographic recording of New Mandalorian [Deputy Minister](/wiki/Deputy_Minister "Deputy Minister") [Jerec](/wiki/Jerec "Jerec"), one of Kryze's close allies. When Kryze spoke before the Senate, Palpatine presented Jerec's doctored testimony, which decried Kryze's pacifist policies and advocated for the Republic to intervene in Mandalore's affairs. The Senate session occurred the same day that Jerec perished in a [Death Watch bombing](/wiki/Bombing_on_Kalevala "Bombing on Kalevala") on Kalevala, preventing Kryze from confirming the veracity of her friend's claims.[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163)

Adding to Kryze's troubles was the fact that Vizsla dispatched a [Death Watch assassin](/wiki/Unidentified_Death_Watch_assassin "Unidentified Death Watch assassin") to [murder](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Satine_Kryze "Plot to assassinate Satine Kryze") her on Coruscant. The assassin's first, very public attempt on Kryze's life accelerated the Senate's vote on the occupation of Mandalore, causing the Senate to authorize the invasion. Despite this setback, Kryze refused to back down. She sought out a meeting with [Davu Golec](/wiki/Davu_Golec "Davu Golec"), a Mandalorian contact within the [Republic Ministry of Intelligence](/wiki/Republic_Ministry_of_Intelligence "Republic Ministry of Intelligence"). Golec gave Kryze a disc containing Jerec's original message, but the Death Watch assassin gunned down Golec before he could reveal any more information. Now on the run from[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163) the [Coruscant Security Force](/wiki/Coruscant_Security_Force "Coruscant Security Force"),[[170]](#cite_note-Databank:_Divo-170) Kryze finally decided to reach out to Kenobi for help.[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163)

As Senate [Vice Chair](/wiki/Vice_Chair "Vice Chair") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") demanded that Kryze turn herself in to the Republic authorities, Kenobi and Kryze realized that the conspiracy surrounding Jerec's message had originated in the upper echelons of the Republic. After defeating the Death Watch assassin and forcing him to flee, Kenobi escorted Kryze to the [Senate Building](/wiki/Imperial_Senate_Building "Imperial Senate Building"). There, Kryze turned herself in to the [Senate Guard](/wiki/Senate_Guard "Senate Guard"), while Kenobi transferred the disc containing Jerec's original message to Padmé Amidala. Amidala presented the recording at a following Senate session, convincing the Republic to rescind its occupation of Mandalore. As a result, Kryze managed to preserve her people's neutrality,[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163) while also averting a major expansion of the Republic's war effort.[[65]](#cite_note-Databank:_Senate-65)

Sometime after Kryze's victory in the Senate,[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163) Vizsla's alliance with Dooku disintegrated, and Dooku rescinded his support of the Death Watch. During the meeting between the two of them,[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171) Dooku scarred Vizsla with his lightsaber[[172]](#cite_note-Death_Watch_History_Gallery_12-172) on his face.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171) Furthermore, without the necessary backing of the Mandalorian populace, the Death Watch abandoned its plan to conquer Mandalore. Vizsla and his allies instead roamed the galaxy as vagabonds,[[173]](#cite_note-Databank:_Death_Watch-173) eventually establishing a [presence](/wiki/Carlac_Death_Watch_camp "Carlac Death Watch camp") on the planet [Carlac](/wiki/Carlac "Carlac").[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171) Even though the New Mandalorians maintained their neutrality,[[163]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-163) a number of Mandalorians had chose to enter the Clone Wars at some point. Some of the planet [Concord Dawn](/wiki/Concord_Dawn "Concord Dawn")'s reputed warriors provided training to the Republic Grand Army. Among their number was [Fenn Rau](/wiki/Fenn_Rau "Fenn Rau") of the Mandalorian Protectors, who served as a [flight instructor](/wiki/Flight_instructor "Flight instructor") for the Republic Navy.[[174]](#cite_note-The_Protector_of_Concord_Dawn-174) Rau also commanded [Skull Squadron](/wiki/Skull_Squadron "Skull Squadron"), a Mandalorian unit that supported Republic campaigns.[[44]](#cite_note-Kanan_10-44)

#### Crime on the rise[]

:   "*I'm afraid our neutrality has caused our people to suffer. The war between the Separatists and the Republic rages across our galaxy. It has caused trade routes to be closed to Mandalore, and has forced us to turn to a black market filled with corruption.*"
:   ―Prime Minister Almec's opening remarks during a meeting of the [Mandalorian Government Council](/wiki/Mandalorian_Government_Council "Mandalorian Government Council")[[175]](#cite_note-Corruption-175)

 [![Boba Fett and his fellow bounty hunters Bossk, Castas, and Aurra Sing repeatedly targeted Mace Windu.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/BobaBosskCastasSing-TCWS2E20.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100329192309) [![Boba Fett and his fellow bounty hunters Bossk, Castas, and Aurra Sing repeatedly targeted Mace Windu.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/BobaBosskCastasSing-TCWS2E20.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20100329192309)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/BobaBosskCastasSing-TCWS2E20.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100329192309) 

Boba Fett and his fellow bounty hunters Bossk, Castas, and Aurra Sing repeatedly targeted Mace Windu.

 

As crime continued to plague the war-torn galaxy,[[176]](#cite_note-Revival-176) Mace Windu became the subject of a series of assassination attempts after Boba Fett allied himself with fellow bounty hunters [Aurra Sing](/wiki/Aurra_Sing "Aurra Sing"), [Bossk](/wiki/Bossk%27wassak%27Cradossk "Bossk'wassak'Cradossk"), and [Castas](/wiki/Castas "Castas") to attain justice for Windu's murder of his father, Jango, at the First Battle of Geonosis.[[177]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-177) The young Fett posed as a [cadet](/wiki/Cadet "Cadet") within Clone Sergeant [Crasher](/wiki/Crasher "Crasher")'s [Clone Youth Brigade](/wiki/Clone_Youth_Brigade "Clone Youth Brigade") as the unit embarked on a training mission aboard Admiral [Kilian's](/wiki/Shoan_Kilian "Shoan Kilian") flagship, the *[Endurance](/wiki/Endurance "Endurance")*, just as Windu and Anakin Skywalker came aboard the Star Destroyer for a respite from the war front. After failing to kill Windu in his quarters aboard the *Endurance*, Fett [sabotaged](/wiki/Sabotage_of_the_Endurance "Sabotage of the Endurance") the cruiser's reactor, forcing Kilian to crash-land his vessel on nearby Vanqor.[[178]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-178) Afterward, Fett and his crew abducted Kilian, Commander Ponds, and a [clone navigation officer](/wiki/Clone_navigation_officer "Clone navigation officer") in the hopes that the Confederacy would offer them a reward for their hostages.[[177]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-177)

When Skywalker and Windu traveled to the *Endurance*'s crash site in search of Kilian and his crew, Fett set another trap. He detonated an explosive in the *Endurance*'s bridge, pinning Skywalker and Windu underneath mounds of rubble. Both Jedi survived the attack, albeit barely.[[177]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-177) By this time, the Confederacy had begun to offer bounties on Jedi, some as high as a million credits.[[179]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-179) As a result, Fett and his allies sought to obtain evidence of Skywalker's and Windu's deaths so that they would be able to turn a profit from the incident. However, Skywalker's astromech droid, R2-D2, warded off the bounty hunters and managed to reach the Jedi Temple, where he notified Plo Koon and Ahsoka Tano of Skywalker and Windu's precarious plight. In response, Koon and Tano [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Vanqor "Mission to Vanqor") with Commander Wolffe and his Wolfpack to Vanqor, where they rescued Skywalker and Windu before the remains of the *Endurance* finally collapsed.[[177]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-177)

Now having twice failed to execute Windu, Fett and his crew resorted to other methods to draw out their target. In a direct holotransmission to the Jedi Temple, Sing gunned down Ponds and threatened to kill Killian and his navigation officer in an attempt to provoke Windu into confronting them. Yet, since Windu was still recovering from the injuries that he had sustained on Vanqor, Koon and Tano instead went after Fett and his team. Koon and Tano tracked the bounty hunters to Florrum, where they had sought out Hondo Ohnaka and his pirate gang. Ohnaka, for his part, stayed out of Sing's plot against Windu, even after Sing murdered Castas for trying to sell her out to interested parties. A [lethal confrontation](/wiki/Second_mission_to_Florrum "Second mission to Florrum") ensued when Koon and Tano clashed with Fett and Sing. When Koon captured Fett, Sing abandoned her young protégé and rendezvoused with Bossk, who was guarding Kilian and his navigation officer.[[72]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-72)

Ultimately, Koon convinced Fett—who was already apprehensive of Sing's brutal exploitation of the hostages—to divulge the location of the prisoners. Tano arrived there just in time to prevent Bossk from executing Kilian and the clone officer. Tano also prevented Sing from escaping aboard her crew's [starship](/wiki/Firespray-31-class_patrol_and_attack_craft "Firespray-31-class patrol and attack craft"), *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")*, by severing the craft's port [stabilizer](/wiki/Stabilizer "Stabilizer") in mid-flight. *Slave I* crashed, taking down Sing with it.[[72]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-72) Though Tano and her colleagues assumed that Sing had perished in the crash, Ohnaka later extracted her from *Slave I*'s wreckage, and she returned to her line of work.[[4]](#cite_note-Assassin-4) The Jedi Order, meanwhile, incarcerated Bossk and Fett in the Judiciary Central Detention Center on Coruscant,[[72]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-72) where they remained prisoners for quite some time.[[180]](#cite_note-Deception-180)

 [![Prime Minister Almec nearly deposed his longtime leader, Duchess Satine Kryze, by way of a black market crisis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/ForcedConfession2-TA.png/revision/latest?cb=20130511155853) [![Prime Minister Almec nearly deposed his longtime leader, Duchess Satine Kryze, by way of a black market crisis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/ForcedConfession2-TA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130511155853)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/ForcedConfession2-TA.png/revision/latest?cb=20130511155853) 

Prime Minister Almec nearly deposed his longtime leader, Duchess Satine Kryze, by way of a black market crisis.

 

In the meantime, the Mandalorians discovered that their hard-won neutrality was not without cost. The Clone Wars disrupted intergalactic trade, depriving many star systems of their much-needed supplies. The situation forced Mandalore to resort to the [black market](/wiki/Black_market "Black market") for food and other necessities. In Sundari, [Tee Va](/wiki/Tee_Va "Tee Va") and his fellow [Moogan](/wiki/Moogan "Moogan") smugglers exploited corruption within the [Mandalorian Guard](/wiki/Mandalorian_Guard "Mandalorian Guard"), as well as the city's customs and education systems, to distribute [slabin](/wiki/Slabin "Slabin")-diluted [tea](/wiki/Tea "Tea") to local schools. While visiting Mandalore, Padmé Amidala helped Satine Kryze [dismantle](/wiki/Skirmish_at_the_Sundari_docks "Skirmish at the Sundari docks") the Moogans' operation because the mixture of tea and slabin had a lethal affect on Sundari's youth.[[175]](#cite_note-Corruption-175)

Furthermore, a [crisis](/wiki/Mandalorian_black_market_conspiracy "Mandalorian black market conspiracy") arose when Prime Minister Almec used the black market to monopolize the planet's imports of supplies. Ahsoka Tano, who was serving as a guest instructor at Mandalore's [Royal Academy of Government](/wiki/Imperial_Academy_of_Mandalore "Imperial Academy of Mandalore"), helped Kryze and a group of young cadets—[Amis](/wiki/Amis "Amis"), [Lagos](/wiki/Lagos "Lagos"), [Soniee](/wiki/Soniee "Soniee"), and Kryze's nephew [Korkie](/wiki/Korkie_Kryze "Korkie Kryze")—expose Almec as the culprit and arrested him.[[181]](#cite_note-The_Academy-181) The Clone Wars continued to change the galaxy, cultivating greed and corruption throughout the Republic and beyond.[[175]](#cite_note-Corruption-175) The bounty hunter [Durge](/wiki/Durge "Durge") was active during the Clone Wars[[182]](#cite_note-Launchpad_203-182) as a hired hand for the Separatists[[183]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Bounty_Hunters-183) who worked on his own time.[[184]](#cite_note-Hot_Shots_Aces_Separatist_Transmissions-184) An assassin by the name of [Ochi](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi") was also active, starting his career in Jedi hunting.[[185]](#cite_note-Final_Order-185)

Whereas Palpatine assured the Senate that the Republic's war effort was faring well, some sources reported otherwise.[[175]](#cite_note-Corruption-175) Even as the Republic made efforts to reinforce its fleet on the [Hydian Way](/wiki/Hydian_Way "Hydian Way"), where they hoped to counter Grievous's own efforts,[[177]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-177) and deployed the [Third Legion](/wiki/Third_Legion "Third Legion") into a large-scale [civil war](/wiki/Balith%27s_Civil_War "Balith's Civil War") on the planet [Balith](/wiki/Balith "Balith"), another crisis unfolded. The war displaced countless civilians, leading Bail Organa, Padmé Amidala, and Senator [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma")[[4]](#cite_note-Assassin-4) of [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila")[[186]](#cite_note-Databank:_Mothma-186) to host the [Alderaan Refugee Conference](/wiki/Alderaan_Refugee_Conference "Alderaan Refugee Conference").[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) Amidala served as the keynote speaker at the summit, which addressed the Republic's efforts to aid the refugees. The conference was interrupted when Ziro the Hutt hired Aurra Sing to kill Amidala in revenge for his imprisonment on Coruscant. Ahsoka Tano and Gregar Typho both helped Amidala subdue Sing,[[4]](#cite_note-Assassin-4) who was nonetheless liberated from her ensuing incarceration[[187]](#cite_note-Databank:_Sing-187) and soon resumed her bounty hunting career.[[188]](#cite_note-Hostage_Crisis-188)

#### The Shadowfeeds of Murkhana[]

:   "*Yes, Count Dooku succeeded in using the HoloNet for Separatist propaganda purposes, but Republic forces were quick to shut down those Shadowfeeds. If memory serves, COMPOR itself was established as a result of the navy's actions at the time.*"
:   ―Five years after the Clone Wars, Imperial Vice Admiral [Dodd Rancit](/wiki/Dodd_Rancit "Dodd Rancit") recalls the Republic's assault on Murkhana[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1)

 [![Wilhuff Tarkin leads the Republic campaign to dismantle Murkhana's Shadowfeed operations.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Tarkin-Battle_of_Murkhana.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141106053010) [![Wilhuff Tarkin leads the Republic campaign to dismantle Murkhana's Shadowfeed operations.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Tarkin-Battle_of_Murkhana.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141106053010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Tarkin-Battle_of_Murkhana.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141106053010) 

Wilhuff Tarkin leads the Republic campaign to dismantle Murkhana's Shadowfeed operations.

 

Nine [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") into the Clone Wars, the Confederacy used the planet [Murkhana](/wiki/Murkhana "Murkhana"), one of its major Outer Rim bastions, as the site of an important operation. Based in [Murkhana City](/wiki/Murkhana_City "Murkhana City"), a team of Confederate scientists deployed a series of [hyperwave transceiver](/wiki/Hyperwave_transceiver "Hyperwave transceiver") nodes to [slice](/wiki/Slicer "Slicer") into the [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet"), the Republic's intergalactic network for news and communication.
