Yet, instead of quietly collecting data on the Republic's military operations, Dooku exploited his infiltration of the HoloNet to launch an unprecedented [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") campaign. The Confederacy hijacked the HoloNet and disseminated [Shadowfeeds](/wiki/Shadowfeed "Shadowfeed") about Separatist accounts of wartime victories and falsifications of Republic war crimes. As a result, the populations of the Republic's Core Worlds began to fear that the Confederacy was on the verge of winning the war.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1)

In order to shut down the Confederacy's Shadowfeeds, the Republic sent Captain Wilhuff Tarkin—the same man who had served as Governor of Eriadu and rejected Dooku's offers to join the CIS—and numerous platoons from the [12th Sector Army](/wiki/12th_Sector_Army "12th Sector Army") to invade Murkhana. During the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Murkhana "Battle of Murkhana"), Tarkin personally led the first waves of clone troopers into Murkhana City. After overwhelming the Separatist ground forces, Tarkin and his soldiers detained the scientists who were operating the Shadowfeeds. Tarkin then tortured the enemy scientists into divulging the details of their jamming and steganographic technology, allowing Republic cryptanalysis operatives to dismantle the Shadowfeeds. The Republic forces also destroyed Murkhana's sole HoloNet relay to stop the Shadowfeeds from reaching worlds along the Perlemian Trade Route. Murkhana retained its Separatist ties, but much of Murkhana City remained littered with refuse from the battle.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1)

In the wake of his victory on Murkhana, Tarkin executed thousands of beings who had abetted Dooku's takeover of the HoloNet, precluding the possibility of another communication breakdown. The Republic Navy's actions at Murkhana also led to the creation of the [Commission for the Protection of the Republic](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Protection_of_the_Republic "Commission for the Protection of the Republic"). Tarkin, for his part, spent the next year serving Sheev Palpatine in a covert capacity. Tarkin garnered a number of similar victories for the Republic, eventually winning the captaincy of a Star Destroyer under Jedi General [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell").[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) All the while, the Shadowfeed was, ultimately, able to return to operation and even survived the war.[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17)

#### Battle of Kamino[]

:   "*The clone planet of Kamino will be a dangerous target.*"  
    *"Just make sure you hold up* your *half of the mission. We must stop the production of new clones if we are to win this war.*"
:   ―Asajj Ventress and General Grievous[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Battle of Kamino](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino") and [Battle of Kamino (Kit Fisto)](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino_(Kit_Fisto) "Battle of Kamino (Kit Fisto)")

Even though Grievous and Asajj Ventress failed in their first attempt to invade Kamino,[[82]](#cite_note-Rookies-82) the clone homeworld remained a critical target for the Confederacy. Therefore, Dooku opted to authorize a second invasion of Kamino. He placed Grievous in overall command of the mission, while sending Ventress ahead of the assault to infiltrate Kamino's defenses aboard her personal starship, the *Trident*. However, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker learned of the imminent invasion from an intercepted transmission between Grievous and Ventress. Acting quickly, Kenobi and Skywalker traveled to Kamino aboard the *Resolute*, bringing along Commander Cody, Captain Rex, and elements of the 501st Legion to bolster Tipoca City's defenses. Shaak Ti,[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) who supervised clone cadet training in Tipoca City,[[81]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-81) also committed her efforts to helping Lama Su secure the Republic's fortifications of the cloning facilities.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

 [![Clone troopers defend Kamino's capital, Tipoca City, from aqua droids and Trident-class assault ships.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505070137) [![Clone troopers defend Kamino's capital, Tipoca City, from aqua droids and Trident-class assault ships.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130505070137)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505070137) 

Clone troopers defend Kamino's capital, Tipoca City, from aqua droids and *Trident*-class assault ships.

 

When Grievous entered the [Kamino system](/wiki/Kamino_system "Kamino system") with a fleet of warships, Wullf Yularen was ready with the Republic's blockade. Utilizing attack formation [Echo-3](/wiki/Echo-3 "Echo-3"), Grievous [engaged](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino") Yularen's opposing [fleet](/wiki/Kamino_blockade "Kamino blockade") in combat. At Ti's command, Skywalker mobilized the Republic Navy's air strike, leading clone pilots aboard [ARC-170](/wiki/Aggressive_ReConnaissance-170_starfighter "Aggressive ReConnaissance-170 starfighter"), V-19, and Y-wing starfighters into orbit to hamper Grievous's warships. As the space battle raged around them, Grievous headed for Kamino's oceans with a contingent of battle droids. To bypass the Republic blockade, Grievous disguised his landing craft as debris from his destroyed warships. Ventress was waiting for Grievous deep beneath Kamino's waves with the *Trident* and her detachment of [AQ-series battle droids](/wiki/AQ-series_battle_droid "AQ-series battle droid"). Once Grievous and his troops had arrived, Ventress dispatched her aqua droids to reassemble the fragments of [*Trident*-class assault ships](/wiki/Trident-class_assault_ship "Trident-class assault ship") that Grievous had brought with him.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

Even as Skywalker pressed his assault on the Confederate armada, both Kenobi and Ti sensed that something was amiss. By sacrificing his transports to protect his flagship, Grievous was exhibiting uncharacteristic recklessness. Suspicious of Grievous's tactics, Kenobi ventured into the oceans in a [Kamino sub](/wiki/KE-UW33 "KE-UW33") to investigate the wreckage from the downed Confederate vessels. Near the ocean floor, Kenobi witnessed the aqua droids readying the Confederacy's assault craft. When the aqua droids attacked his starship, Kenobi escaped back to sea level with the help of an [aiwha](/wiki/Aiwha "Aiwha").[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

Having diverted the Republic's attention to the space battle, Grievous and Ventress initiated their primary assault: the ground campaign. They launched from the oceans aboard their *Trident*-class assault ships, which clambered onto[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) the [Tipoca City Military Complex](/wiki/Tipoca_City_Military_Complex "Tipoca City Military Complex")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) and drilled entry points for their troops. In doing so, the assault ships inflicted severe structural damage to the Military Complex and its array of cloning facilities. Kenobi quickly recalled Skywalker from the battle above Kamino, and they and Ti rushed to scramble their units of clone troopers in defense of Tipoca City. Since Grievous and Ventress did not have enough battle droids to seize control of the city, they sent their main body of troops to distract the Jedi and clones. After rendezvousing and meeting face-to-face for the first time, Grievous and Ventress split up to pursue separate objectives. While Grievous besieged the Military Complex's troop [barracks](/wiki/Barracks "Barracks"), Ventress went after the last remaining sample of Jango Fett's DNA. The Confederacy hoped to use Fett's DNA to unlock new tactical possibilities against the Grand Army.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

Before reaching the [clone DNA room](/wiki/Clone_DNA_room "Clone DNA room"), Ventress slew[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) Commander [Colt](/wiki/Colt "Colt") of the [Advanced Recon Commandos](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando").[[81]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-81) Yet, before Ventress could abscond with the sample of Fett's DNA, Skywalker intercepted her at the DNA chamber and engaged her in a lightsaber duel. Similarly, Kenobi confronted Grievous outside the barracks, where they began yet another rematch as part of their longstanding rivalry. Meanwhile, 501st troopers Fives and Echo rallied a squad of young clone cadets to protect their home. Once Cody, Rex, and maintenance clone [99](/wiki/Clone_99 "Clone 99") brought them a supply of [DC-15A blaster carbines](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine") and thermal detonators from the nearby armory, the cadets aided their commanding officers in defending the barracks from Grievous's B1 battle droids, capturing the droids in a classic pincer movement. Though the cadets and troopers successfully routed the droids, 99 died from enemy blasterfire while attempting to resupply his comrades. Cody, Echo, Fives, and Rex all mourned the loss of 99,[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) for even though his cloning malformation barred him from active duty,[[81]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-81) they believed that their comrade had died as a true soldier.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

 [![Shaak Ti leads the Grand Army in repelling Separatist battle droids from Tipoca City's main hangar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/TiDefendsHangar-ARCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505220033) [![Shaak Ti leads the Grand Army in repelling Separatist battle droids from Tipoca City's main hangar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/TiDefendsHangar-ARCT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130505220033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/TiDefendsHangar-ARCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505220033) 

Shaak Ti leads the Grand Army in repelling Separatist battle droids from Tipoca City's main hangar.

 

When aqua droids breached Tipoca City's command center, Shaak Ti left Lama Su at the command post, while she personally led the front-line offensive against the invading troops. Ti and her clone troopers succeeded in repelling the aqua droids to the Military Complex's main hangar, where the clone soldiers unleashed barrages of blasterfire upon the enemy droids[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) with their [Z-6 rotary blaster cannons](/wiki/Z-6_rotary_blaster_cannon "Z-6 rotary blaster cannon").[[189]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers_Guide-189) The clones also used [RPS-6 rocket launchers](/wiki/RPS-6_rocket_launcher "RPS-6 rocket launcher")[[190]](#cite_note-Databank:_RPS-6-190) to dislodge the *Trident*-class assault ships from their grip on the exterior walls of the Military Complex. As a result, the Grand Army made steady progress in its efforts to retake Tipoca City.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

Ultimately, both Grievous and Ventress failed to achieve their objectives. Kenobi pursued Grievous to Tipoca City's exterior platforms, where Grievous evaded his foe and commandeered a [Kaminoan flight pod](/wiki/Kaminoan_flight_pod "Kaminoan flight pod"). Similarly, Skywalker's duel with Ventress moved to the outer platforms, where Skywalker finally retrieved the sample of Fett's DNA from her. A squad of nearly twenty clone troopers came to Skywalker's aid and surrounded Ventress. Though Skywalker intended to let his soldiers execute Ventress, she escaped with Grievous in his stolen flight pod. Nevertheless, the Confederacy failed to win[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) the Battle of Kamino,[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) and the Republic emerged triumphant.[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30)

A number of Republic personnel received various forms of commendation for their performance in the Battle of Kamino. Cody and Rex promoted both Echo and Fives to the prestigious rank of Advanced Recon Commando,[[30]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-30) while Wilhuff Tarkin was decorated for his involvement in the campaign.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) The Kaminoans resumed their production of clone troopers for the Republic,[[66]](#cite_note-Fugitive-66) and Ti continued to collaborate with Kamino's cloners to train and expand the ranks of the Grand Army for the remainder of the war.[[38]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-38) At another point, Kit Fisto was involved in [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino_(Kit_Fisto) "Battle of Kamino (Kit Fisto)") on Kamino, during which he fought against Separatist droids.[[191]](#cite_note-The_Lightsaber_Collection-191)

#### Political intrigues[]

:   "*The Trade Federation is neutral in this, but Pantora must pay its debt before we can resume commerce with the system.*"  
    "*That is a lie! It is well-known that the Trade Federation is aligned with the Separatists.*"  
    "*Slanderous! We are not Separatists simply because we do business with them. How many times must I remind you of the Commerce Treaty of 1647? The Trade Federation is* neutral*.*"  
    "*I beg the Senate to listen to our pleas! Ignore the Trade Federation's* feeble *attempt to paint this as a domestic financial issue, and allow us to resume trade.*"
:   ―Lott Dod and Riyo Chuchi's addresses to the Republic Senate reflect the wider conflict between the Trade Federation and the Pantorans[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)

Not all battles of the Clone Wars were fought between the Republic's clone troopers and the Confederacy's battle droids. Occasionally, Dooku relied on his contacts in the trade guilds to engineer plots that forced planets into joining the Confederacy. One such scheme involved the moon Pantora, which was a member of the Republic. Under the pretext that the Pantorans owed outstanding debts, the Trade Federation suspended all commerce with the [Pantora system](/wiki/Pantora_system "Pantora system") and [blockaded](/wiki/Blockade_of_Pantora "Blockade of Pantora") Pantora. When the Republic Senate appeared unsympathetic to their plight, the Pantorans began to rally against the Republic. Complicating matters was Dooku's offer to aid the Pantorans on the condition that they join the Confederacy. The incident occurred not long into Baron Papanoida's first term as chairman of Pantora. In response to the unfolding crisis, Papanoida sent Senator Riyo Chuchi to Coruscant to convince the Senate to side with Pantora.[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)

 [![The Trade Federation's blockade of Pantora nearly caused the Pantorans to join the Confederacy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/PantoraBlockade-SoI.png/revision/latest?cb=20130508003755) [![The Trade Federation's blockade of Pantora nearly caused the Pantorans to join the Confederacy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/PantoraBlockade-SoI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130508003755)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/PantoraBlockade-SoI.png/revision/latest?cb=20130508003755) 

The Trade Federation's blockade of Pantora nearly caused the Pantorans to join the Confederacy.

 

Hoping to legitimize the blockade of Pantora, Lott Dod reiterated the Trade Federation's claims of neutrality, which the [Commerce Treaty of 1647](/wiki/Commerce_Treaty_of_1647 "Commerce Treaty of 1647") guaranteed. Still, Chuchi refused to back down in her rebuttals of Dod's claims, earning the support of colleagues like Padmé Amidala. Yet, Dooku resorted to other tactics to convince the Pantorans to join the Confederacy. After Papanoida and his family arrived on Coruscant to meet with Chuchi, the Separatists hired [Greedo](/wiki/Greedo "Greedo") and [another bounty hunter](/wiki/Unidentified_Gotal_bounty_hunter "Unidentified Gotal bounty hunter") to [kidnap](/wiki/Kidnapping_of_the_Papanoida_daughters "Kidnapping of the Papanoida daughters") Papanoida's two daughters, [Chi Eekway](/wiki/Chi_Eekway_Papanoida "Chi Eekway Papanoida") and [Che Amanwe](/wiki/Che_Amanwe_Papanoida "Che Amanwe Papanoida"), from the family's [apartment](/wiki/Papanoida%27s_Coruscant_apartment "Papanoida's Coruscant apartment"). At the same time, Dooku personally offered to help Papanoida find his daughters.[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)

Ahsoka Tano, who was good friends with Chuchi, volunteered to aid Papanoida's search for his daughters. Papanoida and his son, [Ion](/wiki/Ion_Papanoida "Ion Papanoida"), tracked down Greedo at Jabba's Palace on Tatooine. Speaking to Jabba, Papanoida cited the Hutt Clan's treaty with the Republic and persuaded Jabba to let him confirm that Greedo was one of the kidnappers, by matching Greedo's blood against a blood sample from the crime scene. Once Greedo admitted to abducting Amanwe and Eekway, he took Papanoida and his son to Mos Eisley's [cantina](/wiki/Chalmun%27s_Spaceport_Cantina "Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina"), where Amanwe was being held. After a [short shootout](/wiki/Rescue_in_Chalmun%27s_Cantina "Rescue in Chalmun's Cantina") with Greedo's comrades, Papanoida and Ion managed to rescue Amanwe.[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)

Meanwhile, Chuchi and Tano paid a [diplomatic visit](/wiki/Rescue_on_the_Pantora_Droid_Control_Ship "Rescue on the Pantora Droid Control Ship") to the Trade Federation's Droid Control Ship that was blockading Pantora. Aboard the vessel, they located and liberated Eekway from a holding cell. Chuchi also convinced the battleship's officer, [Sib Canay](/wiki/Sib_Canay "Sib Canay"), as well as a [fellow envoy](/wiki/Unidentified_Neimoidian_envoy "Unidentified Neimoidian envoy") to end the blockade due to their illicit involvement in the abduction of Papanoida's daughters. Canay took the fall for the whole debacle, with Dod publicly claiming that the influence of Viceroy Nute Gunray[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)—whom Dod described as an extremist,[[109]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-109) since Gunray was a member of the Separatist Council[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)—extended to misguided officers like Canay. In the end, the Trade Federation relinquished its blockade of Pantora and resumed trade with the Pantorans.[[138]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-138)

A potential rift later emerged between the Republic and the Hutt Clan,[[179]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-179) which had been allies ever since Dooku and Ziro the Hutt's plot to overthrow Jabba.[[23]](#cite_note-TCWf-23) Since Ziro possessed a [holodiary](/wiki/Holodiary "Holodiary") that [documented](/wiki/Hutt_Council_records "Hutt Council records") the [Grand Hutt Council](/wiki/Grand_Hutt_Council "Grand Hutt Council")'s illicit dealings, Jabba and the Hutt Council decided to forcefully obtain custody of Ziro from the Republic.[[179]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-179) To that end, the Hutts hired Cad Bane to spring Ziro from the Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center. Bane did so by collaborating with fellow bounty hunters Aurra Sing, [Shahan Alama](/wiki/Shahan_Alama "Shahan Alama"), and [Robonino](/wiki/Robonino "Robonino") to engineer a [hostage crisis](/wiki/Senate_hostage_crisis "Senate hostage crisis") in the Republic Senate.[[188]](#cite_note-Hostage_Crisis-188) Bane's high-profile breach of Coruscant's security[[192]](#cite_note-Databank:_Coruscant-192) consequently forced Sheev Palpatine to release Ziro from prison.[[188]](#cite_note-Hostage_Crisis-188) Jedi Masters Obi-Wan Kenobi and [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") tried to recapture Ziro, but Ziro's ex-lover, the renowned [singer](/wiki/Musician "Musician") [Sy Snootles](/wiki/Sy_Snootles "Sy Snootles"), killed him on Teth and retrieved the Hutt Council records as part of a prior arrangement with Jabba. Due to the Confederacy's million-credit bounties on Jedi, Bane—who had also pursued Ziro to Teth—[attacked](/wiki/Showdown_on_Teth "Showdown on Teth") Kenobi and Vos, but their skirmish resulted in a draw.[[179]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-179)

#### No end in sight[]

:   "*After our attack, the chances of peace will disappear. The Banking Clan, the Trade Federation, and the Techno Union will all get their fair share…and* then *some.*"
:   ―Dooku conspires with a cabal of Republic senators to sabotage a peace initiative between the Confederacy and the Republic[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

Over a year into the Clone Wars,[[193]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides_Date-193) figures on both sides of the conflict nearly succeeded in ending the bloodshed. Their venture for peace emanated from the Republic Senate's endless debates about escalating its campaign against the Confederacy.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) Many of the Republic's social services—including education, infrastructure, health care, and basic amenities—had suffered from budget cuts in favor of military spending. Furthermore, the war effort's fiscal cost dragged the Republic into debt,[[194]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-194) leaving it on the verge of bankruptcy.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) Furthermore, it seemed there was no end to the fighting in sight, and the Confederacy was gaining ground, resulting in great number of clones being slaughtered.[[195]](#cite_note-Peace_short_story-195) In response, Senator [Gume Saam](/wiki/Gume_Saam "Gume Saam") proposed a [bill](/wiki/Republic_financial_reform_bill "Republic financial reform bill") to open new lines of credit with the InterGalactic Banking Clan, which would facilitate future loans for the Grand Army's expenses. In truth, Saam's proposal was a war profiteering ploy, since the legislation would deregulate the banks and thus allow the Banking Clan, the Trade Federation, and the Techno Union to reap immense profits from the war.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

 [![By proxy, the Sith thwarted Mina Bonteri's proposal to open peace negotiations, and Dooku later had her killed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002081123) [![By proxy, the Sith thwarted Mina Bonteri's proposal to open peace negotiations, and Dooku later had her killed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20161002081123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002081123) 

By proxy, the Sith thwarted Mina Bonteri's proposal to open peace negotiations, and Dooku later had her killed.

 

Though Bail Organa persuaded the Senate to table Saam's bill, Padmé Amidala remained concerned about the war's pervasive bloodshed. Consequently, she sought out a private meeting with her old friend Mina Bonteri,[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) who represented her homeworld of [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon") in the Separatist Senate.[[196]](#cite_note-Databank:_Mina_Bonteri-196) In doing so, Amidala circumvented the Republic's [law](/wiki/Republic_Senate_non-communication_law "Republic Senate non-communication law") against speaking with Confederate officials, a policy that prevented the Republic from recognizing the Confederacy as a legitimate state. Amidala and Ahsoka Tano used the latter's special Jedi clearance to smuggle themselves onto Raxus, where Amidala persuaded Bonteri to introduce a proposal to the Separatist Senate to initiate diplomatic negotiations with the Republic. Bonteri's [measure](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_initiative "Confederate–Republic peace initiative") passed, thereby raising the prospect of an end to the war.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

A potential resolution to the Clone Wars jeopardized the Sith's plans for galactic conquest, since their endgame had not yet come to fruition. Moreover, Saam and other Confederate-leaning members of the Republic Senate, including Lott Dod and [Nix Card](/wiki/Nix_Card "Nix Card") of the Banking Clan, were determined to pass the financial deregulation bill by any means necessary. Card proposed that they engineer a Confederate assault on Coruscant, which had not experienced a large-scale attack in over a millennium. Dooku agreed to Card's idea, since it would sow fear on the Republic capital and thus motivate the Senate into approving Saam's bill. Grievous subsequently sent a six-member team of [demolition droids](/wiki/Infiltrator_demolition_droid "Infiltrator demolition droid") to sabotage Coruscant's [central power distribution grid](/wiki/Central_power_distribution_grid "Central power distribution grid"). Their [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_Coruscant%27s_central_power_distribution_grid "Bombing of Coruscant's central power distribution grid") coincided with the Separatist Senate's offer for peace talks, thereby sullying the apparent sincerity of Bonteri's monumental peace initiative.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54)

As Grievous's bombing plunged Coruscant into a planet-wide blackout, Dod and Saam decried the Confederacy for its unprovoked assault. As Card had predicted, the Senate voted to deregulate the Banking Clan, with multiple senators calling for an expansion of the Grand Army.[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) Even as Amidala and her like-minded allies advocated for reductions to military spending, the Sith derailed her and Bonteri's joint initiative for peace.[[194]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-194) Dooku had his agents murder Bonteri,[[197]](#cite_note-Databank:_Dooku-197) then alleged that Bonteri had perished in a [Republic assault](/wiki/Attack_on_Confederate_people "Attack on Confederate people"), which he used as justification to withdraw the Separatist Senate's offer for negotiations.[[194]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-194) Bonteri was survived by her son, [Lux](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri"), who embarked on a quest to kill Dooku in retaliation for his mother's death.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

In the absence of the peace initiative, both sides of the conflict escalated their war efforts, further prolonging the Clone Wars. The Confederacy secured a loan from the Banking Clan to finance three million new battle droids for the Separatist Droid Army. Concurrently, Republic Senator [Halle Burtoni](/wiki/Halle_Burtoni "Halle Burtoni") of Kamino introduced an [emergency appropriations bill](/wiki/Republic_military_enhancement_bill "Republic military enhancement bill") to produce five million more clone troopers for the Grand Army, using funding from the Banking Clan. However, the Banking Clan issued an interest rate hike on all loans due to its newfound deregulation. Moreover, Dooku utilized scare tactics by hiring the bounty hunters Robonino and [Chata Hyoki](/wiki/Chata_Hyoki "Chata Hyoki") to intimidate numerous senators into supporting Burtoni's pro-military proposal. Even though Amidala convinced the Senate to defeat Burtoni's resolution,[[194]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-194) a pair of assassinations—Senators Onaconda Farr of Rodia and [Mee Deechi](/wiki/Mee_Deechi "Mee Deechi")[[198]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-198) of [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara")[[199]](#cite_note-Databank:_Deechi-199)—destabilized the situation once more. Ultimately, the Senate's militarist faction won out, rejecting Amidala's [proposal](/wiki/Reduced_military_spending_bill "Reduced military spending bill") to reduce military spending in favor of a scheduled increase in clone trooper production.[[198]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-198)

#### Other incidents of year two[]

:   "*Yes, Boo! I do recall the* journey *of Q5-7070, the most unfortunate droid of the* Clone Wars!"
:   ―[CR-8R](/wiki/CR-8R "CR-8R")[[200]](#cite_note-The_Big_March-200)

At some point during the second year of the war, a squad of B1 battle droids, acting under a T-series tactical droid and a [B1 lieutenant](/wiki/Unidentified_B1_battle_droid_lieutenant_(Opop_Hibbedit) "Unidentified B1 battle droid lieutenant (Opop Hibbedit)"), was sent to the astronomical object [Opop Hibbedit](/wiki/Opop_Hibbedit "Opop Hibbedit"), where they searched through a region until the T-1 declared it uninhabited. As the squad moved on to continue their search by securing themselves aboard their flying MTT variant, the fasteners keeping B1 unit [Q5-7070](/wiki/Q5-7070 "Q5-7070") in placed snapped, leaving the droid to tumble to the ground below. Engaging his homing protocol to reunite with his squad, Q5-7070 endured a series of challenges from the local wildlife and plant-life, encountering [sentient carnivorous plants](/wiki/Unidentified_Opop_Hibbedit_species "Unidentified Opop Hibbedit species"), [magnetic rock chimps](/wiki/Magnetic_rock_chimp "Magnetic rock chimp"), and finally a large [bird](/wiki/Bird "Bird") that ate him over the course of his long march. Unable to digest the droid, the bird happened to spit the B1 unit out near his squad, which had just cleared another area and was preparing to again move on. Ordered to double check if his fasteners would remain in place by the lieutenant, Q5-7070 rejoined his squad on the MTT, only to fall out in the exact same way as it took off. Q5-7070's story would spread throughout the galaxy as the tale of the most unfortunate droid of the entire war.[[200]](#cite_note-The_Big_March-200)

### Year three (20 BBY–19 BBY)[]

#### The apprentices of Count Dooku[]

:   "*You have failed me for the last time. You are no longer my apprentice. And now, you shall die.*"
:   ―Dooku betrays Asajj Ventress, sparking a chain of events leading to the ascension of Savage Opress[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31)

 [![Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress unleashes her fury on Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/VentressChokesKenobiSkywalker-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521041044) [![Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress unleashes her fury on Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/VentressChokesKenobiSkywalker-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130521041044)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/VentressChokesKenobiSkywalker-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521041044) 

Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress unleashes her fury on Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker.

 

As the war's second year progressed, a cycle of betrayals and vengeance consumed the Sith hierarchy, which in turn affected a number of campaigns between the Confederacy and the Republic.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) At the [Battle of Sullust](/wiki/Battle_of_Sullust "Battle of Sullust"),[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) Asajj Ventress spearheaded the Separatist navy's strike on a Republic fleet. Flying her personal [*Ginivex*-class fanblade starfighter](/wiki/Ginivex-class_fanblade_starfighter "Ginivex-class fanblade starfighter"), Ventress led the [droid tri-fighters](/wiki/Droid_tri-fighter "Droid tri-fighter") of [Trident groups one](/wiki/Trident_group_one "Trident group one") and [two](/wiki/Trident_group_two "Trident group two") in overwhelming the *Resolute*.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) Wullf Yularen narrowly escaped from his flagship before it went down.[[202]](#cite_note-Nightsisters_Guide-202) Building on her success, Ventress gave chase to Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker in their Delta-7B interceptors. However, both Kenobi and Ventress crashed in the hangar of the Separatist [command ship](/wiki/Unidentified_Providence-class_carrier/destroyer_(Battle_of_Sullust) "Unidentified Providence-class carrier/destroyer (Battle of Sullust)"), with Skywalker following them there.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31)

From afar, Darth Sidious sensed Ventress's growing power in the Force, and he recognized her as a threat. Suspecting that Dooku was training Ventress as a means of supplanting him, Sidious demanded that Dooku prove his allegiance to him by eliminating Ventress. Though reluctant to do so, Dooku obeyed his Master's wishes. Dooku recalled Confederate reinforcements that were inbound to the [Sullust system](/wiki/Sullust_system "Sullust system"), then informed Ventress that she was no longer his apprentice—and that she would die. Shell-shocked from Dooku's betrayal, Ventress dueled Kenobi and Skywalker until Dooku ordered [TJ-912](/wiki/TJ-912 "TJ-912"), the tactical droid in charge of the Separatist [armada](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress%27s_fleet "Asajj Ventress's fleet") over [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"), to sacrifice their flagship and obliterate it.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31)

 [![Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress returns to her homeworld of Dathomir.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/At_Odds_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428222816) [![Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress returns to her homeworld of Dathomir.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/At_Odds_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20190428222816)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/At_Odds_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428222816) 

Betrayed by Dooku, Asajj Ventress returns to her homeworld of Dathomir.

 

Kenobi and Skywalker made it off the enemy command ship,[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) but both they[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) and Dooku presumed that Ventress died when the *Providence*-class Dreadnought was destroyed from friendly fire. Afterward, Dooku had TJ-912 withdraw their fleet from the Sullust system, conceding victory to the Republic. In actuality, Ventress had survived, albeit barely. Captain [Ratch](/wiki/Ratch "Ratch") and his band of scavengers found her in the wreckage of her starfighter and brought her aboard their freighter,[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31) the [*Raider*](/wiki/Raider_(salvage_freighter) "Raider (salvage freighter)").[[202]](#cite_note-Nightsisters_Guide-202) Ventress slew Ratch and his crew and returned home to Dathomir, where her people, the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters"), nursed her back to health. When Ventress and her fellow Nightsisters [Naa'leth](/wiki/Naa%27leth "Naa'leth") and [Karis](/wiki/Karis "Karis") failed to [assassinate](/wiki/Mission_to_Serenno_(Nightsisters) "Mission to Serenno (Nightsisters)") Dooku at his palace on Serenno, Ventress conspired with [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Talzin](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin"), the leader of her Nightsister clan, to exact her revenge on Dooku by different means.[[31]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-31)

From Dathomir's [village](/wiki/Nightbrother_village "Nightbrother village") of subservient [Nightbrothers](/wiki/Nightbrothers "Nightbrothers"), Ventress [procured](/wiki/Selection "Selection") a formidable warrior who would replace her as Dooku's next apprentice: [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress"). Before gifting Opress to Dooku, Talzin and her Nightsister [witches](/wiki/Witch "Witch") imbued Opress with their [magicks](/wiki/Magick "Magick"), bringing him under their control. Officially, Talzin declined Dooku's proposal for an alliance between the Nightsisters and the Confederacy, as her clan had no interest in becoming involved in the Clone Wars;[[203]](#cite_note-Monster-203) although some Nightsisters were seen fighting for the Separatist cause during the war,[[204]](#cite_note-Ghosts-204) a formal alliance never emerged.[[205]](#cite_note-Massacre-205) In any case, Dooku opted to assess Opress's abilities by sending him to an active battlefront on Devaron. There, the Separatist Droid Army was [laying siege](/wiki/Devaron_massacre "Devaron massacre") to the [Temple of Eedit](/wiki/Temple_of_Eedit "Temple of Eedit"), a [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") that doubled as an outpost for the Grand Army. Opress was the sole survivor of the battle, as he butchered[[203]](#cite_note-Monster-203) Clone Commander [Trauma](/wiki/Trauma "Trauma")[[206]](#cite_note-Monster_Guide-206) and his clone soldiers, as well as Jedi Master [Halsey](/wiki/Halsey "Halsey") and his Padawan, [Knox](/wiki/Knox "Knox").[[203]](#cite_note-Monster-203)

Impressed by Opress's performance,[[203]](#cite_note-Monster-203) Dooku trained his new apprentice in the ways of the Sith,[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) hoping to depose Sidious in accordance with the Rule of Two.[[203]](#cite_note-Monster-203) Opress's next task was to abduct King Katuunko of Toydaria, for Dooku still harbored a grudge against Katuunko[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) due to the latter's refusal to ally Toydaria with the Confederacy.[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87) However, Opress's massacre on Devaron had caught the attention of the Jedi High Council.[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) After [Delta Squad](/wiki/Delta_Squad "Delta Squad"), a [clone commando](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") unit composed of Sergeant [Boss](/wiki/Boss_(clone_commando) "Boss (clone commando)"), [Fixer](/wiki/Fixer_(clone_commando) "Fixer (clone commando)"), [Sev](/wiki/Sev "Sev"), and [Scorch](/wiki/Scorch "Scorch"),[[207]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist_Guide-207) recovered Halsey's and Knox's bodies from the Temple of Eedit, Kenobi and Skywalker went to investigate Opress's connection to Dathomir. The two Jedi headed to Toydaria after learning from Talzin that Opress was currently there.[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201)

 [![Savage Opress ruins Asajj Ventress's scheme to kill Dooku by turning on both of them.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/SavageChokesMasters-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111010225733) [![Savage Opress ruins Asajj Ventress's scheme to kill Dooku by turning on both of them.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/SavageChokesMasters-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20111010225733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/SavageChokesMasters-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111010225733) 

Savage Opress ruins Asajj Ventress's scheme to kill Dooku by turning on both of them.

 

Everything [came to a head](/wiki/Showdown_at_Toydaria "Showdown at Toydaria") at Toydaria. Opress cut through the [Toydarian Royal Palace](/wiki/Toydarian_Royal_Palace "Toydarian Royal Palace")'s [royal guards](/wiki/Toydarian_Guard "Toydarian Guard"), but when Kenobi and Skywalker interfered, Opress [Force-choked](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") Katuunko to death. When Opress brought Katuunko's corpse aboard Dooku's [*Providence*-class Dreadnought](/wiki/Dooku%27s_Providence-class_carrier/destroyer "Dooku's Providence-class carrier/destroyer") in orbit of Toydaria, Dooku was furious that Opress had disobeyed his orders to keep Katuunko alive. At that moment, Ventress entered Dooku's chambers and activated the spell that ensured Opress's loyalty to her. An intense duel erupted as Opress and Ventress tried to kill Dooku, but it escalated into a three-way confrontation when Opress broke free of Ventress's control and turned on both of his former masters. Evading Opress, Ventress pursued Dooku to the lower decks. But even in single combat, she was unable to defeat the Sith Lord. Ventress barely made it into an escape pod, and she departed from Dooku's dreadnought, now facing an uncertain future.[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201)

Meanwhile, Opress again encountered Kenobi and Skywalker after they reached Dooku's dreadnought aboard the *Thief's Eye*, the personal yacht of the late Katuunko. When Dooku's battle droids opened fire on them in the main hangar, Opress and his Jedi adversaries escaped separately from the cruiser, bringing the showdown to an end. Opress limped home to Dathomir, where Talzin sent him on a quest to save his long-lost brother Maul,[[201]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-201) who had once been Sidious's apprentice[[61]](#cite_note-Episode_I-61) and was in fact Talzin's son.[[208]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_2-208)

#### Republic defeat at Sarrish[]

 [![Gregor (pictured) was clone commando who served in the devastating Battle of Sarrish.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/GregorInAction.png/revision/latest?cb=20131023180029) [![Gregor (pictured) was clone commando who served in the devastating Battle of Sarrish.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/GregorInAction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20131023180029)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/GregorInAction.png/revision/latest?cb=20131023180029) 

Gregor (pictured) was clone commando who served in the devastating Battle of Sarrish.

 

The grueling [Battle of Sarrish](/wiki/Battle_of_Sarrish "Battle of Sarrish")[[209]](#cite_note-Gregor_databank-209) was also fought in 20 BBY. It occurred between Ventress's failed assassination attempt on Serenno and Talzin's offer of Savage Oppress to Dooku.[[210]](#cite_note-Timelines-210)

The battle became one of the Republic's greatest defeats, with many[[211]](#cite_note-Missing_in_Action-211) clone troopers[[212]](#cite_note-Gregor_bio_5-212) killed in action. The elite [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") of [Foxtrot Group](/wiki/Foxtrot_Group "Foxtrot Group"), meanwhile,[[211]](#cite_note-Missing_in_Action-211) were reported missing in action.[[213]](#cite_note-Gregor_bio_4-213) Commando captain [Gregor](/wiki/Gregor "Gregor") survived the battle but suffered amnesia after a shuttle crash, finding himself on the distant planet [Abafar](/wiki/Abafar "Abafar") with no memory of his past as a soldier.[[209]](#cite_note-Gregor_databank-209)

#### Citadel prison break[]

:   "*There have not been battles like these since the days of the Old Republic.*"
:   ―Saesee Tiin[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Battle of Lola Sayu](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu "Battle of Lola Sayu")
 [![Even Piell and his crew escape from incarceration in the Citadel with the help of a Republic strike team.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/MissiontotheCitadel-The_Citadel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110925021312) [![Even Piell and his crew escape from incarceration in the Citadel with the help of a Republic strike team.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/MissiontotheCitadel-The_Citadel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20110925021312)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/MissiontotheCitadel-The_Citadel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110925021312) 

Even Piell and his crew escape from incarceration in the Citadel with the help of a Republic strike team.

 

A year and nine months into the Clone Wars,[[214]](#cite_note-The_Citadel_Date-214) the [Nexus Route](/wiki/Nexus_Route "Nexus Route")—a little-known hyperspace lane that connected Coruscant with the heart of Separatist space—gained critical importance for both the Republic and the Confederacy. When Jedi General Even Piell and his crew unearthed the coordinates of the Nexus Route, the Confederacy targeted him for capture. As a Confederate flotilla [overwhelmed](/wiki/Capture_of_Even_Piell "Capture of Even Piell") his Star Destroyer, Piell divided the Nexus Route's coordinates with his naval captain, Wilhuff Tarkin. Both of them memorized half of the information as a safeguard against torture. The Separatists thereafter abducted Piell, Tarkin, and their clone navigation officers and incarcerated them in Lola Sayu's infamous Citadel prison, which was being overseen by [Warden](/wiki/Warden "Warden") [Osi Sobeck](/wiki/Osi_Sobeck "Osi Sobeck").[[32]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-32)

After receiving word of Piell's capture, the Jedi High Council assembled an infiltration team to rescue him and his crew from the Citadel. Kenobi and Skywalker received command of a squad of clone troopers, with additional support from Commander Cody, Captain Rex, and ARC troopers Echo and Fives. Much to Skywalker's later consternation, Ahsoka Tano joined the mission even though he ordered her not to do so. At the Jedi Temple, the Jedi and clones [encased](/wiki/Carbon-freezing "Carbon-freezing") themselves in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite") to mask their life form signatures from the Confederacy's blockade of Lola Sayu. The [dangerous operation](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu "Battle of Lola Sayu") began when R2-D2 and a [squad](/wiki/R2-D2%27s_battle_droid_squadron "R2-D2's battle droid squadron") of reprogrammed B1 battle droids transported the Jedi and clones to[[32]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-32) the [Lola Sayu system](/wiki/Lola_Sayu_system "Lola Sayu system")[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) aboard a pilfered *Sheathipede*-class shuttle. Once they had bypassed the blockade and reached Lola Sayu's surface, R2-D2 unfroze his comrades from their carbonite blocks.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-32)

Despite Tano's unexpected appearance, Kenobi and Skywalker let her join their operation. After free-climbing a cliff to reach the Citadel, the infiltration team rescued Piell, as well as Tarkin and their clone officers. Along the way, they evaded Sobeck's countermeasures, which ranged from wall-mounted [blaster cannons](/wiki/Blaster_cannon "Blaster cannon") and electrical emitters, to elite BX-series droid commandos. Nevertheless, the squad incurred casualties from Sobeck's traps. As part of their plan's next stage, Kenobi and Skywalker divided their forces. While Skywalker and Tano brought Tarkin, Rex, Fives, Echo, and several troopers into the caverns beneath the Citadel, Kenobi, Piell, Cody, and the other soldiers created a diversion by exploding one of the Citadel's upper decks.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-32) Yet, complications arose as both squads headed to their separate extraction points. R2-D2 and his reprogrammed droids landed the shuttle at the Citadel's rear landing pad, but Sobeck's tactical droid, [K2-B4](/wiki/K2-B4 "K2-B4"), intercepted them there. Moreover, Sobeck recaptured Cody, Kenobi, Piell, and their men, but R2-D2 and his battle droids freed them from Sobeck's droid security teams.[[215]](#cite_note-Counterattack-215)

To reach their extraction point at the Citadel's external fuel pipeline, Skywalker, Tano, Tarkin, and their soldiers used thermal detonators to rupture a blocked cavern as well as a pursuing squad of battle droids. However, when R2-D2 and the shuttle missed their scheduled rendezvous, Skywalker and Tano resorted to their backup plan. After using more of their explosives to detonate the fuel in the exterior pipeline, Skywalker, Tano, Tarkin, and their men proceeded to the prison's main landing pad. They arrived at the airfield just as Kenobi, Piell, and their squad mounted a desperate offensive to eliminate the battle droids that had separated them from their shuttle. While Kenobi, Piell, Skywalker, and Tano concentrated on destroying an incoming squad of battle droids aboard [Single Trooper Aerial Platforms](/wiki/Single_Trooper_Aerial_Platform "Single Trooper Aerial Platform"), Echo and Fives focused their attention on the ground-level enemy infantry. Yet, just as Echo tried to board the shuttle, a droid commando fired a turret blast at the craft, causing a fiery explosion that consumed the shuttle and, presumably, Echo.[[215]](#cite_note-Counterattack-215)

 [![Before dying, Even Piell passes on his half of the Nexus Route's coordinates to Ahsoka Tano.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EvenPiellDying-CR.png/revision/latest?cb=20130529003627) [![Before dying, Even Piell passes on his half of the Nexus Route's coordinates to Ahsoka Tano.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EvenPiellDying-CR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130529003627)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EvenPiellDying-CR.png/revision/latest?cb=20130529003627) 

Before dying, Even Piell passes on his half of the Nexus Route's coordinates to Ahsoka Tano.

 

Without their shuttle, the four Jedi escaped from the Citadel's airfield with Tarkin, as well as Cody, Rex, Fives, and their remaining troopers. As they made their way across Lola Sayu's inhospitable terrain, Kenobi and Skywalker notified the Jedi High Council that they would require an extraction from Lola Sayu.[[215]](#cite_note-Counterattack-215) Consequently, the Council sent four of its members—Kit Fisto, Adi Gallia, Plo Koon, and [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin")—to the Lola Sayu system with a battle group of four Star Destroyers. In the meantime, Piell and his allies headed for an island that the Council had selected as their extraction point. En route, an endless number of battle droid squads pursued the Jedi and clones, leading R2-D2 to sacrifice his reprogrammed battle droids to delay the enemy forces as long as possible.[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62)

It was not long before Sobeck personally took charge of the effort to recapture his prisoners. Under pressure from Dooku to recover the Nexus Route intelligence, Sobeck dispatched a hunting party of ravenous [anoobas](/wiki/Anooba "Anooba") to locate the Jedi and clones, then followed with a squad of droid commandos. Although the Jedi and clones defeated Sobeck's anoobas and [LM-432 crab droids](/wiki/LM-432_crab_droid "LM-432 crab droid"), their momentary victory came at a severe cost. Piell died from fatal wounds from one of the anoobas, using his final breaths to pass his half of the Nexus Route coordinates to Tano. She and her comrades took a brief respite from the battle to lay Piell to rest, cremating his body in one of Lola Sayu's rivers of [sulfurous](/wiki/Sulfur "Sulfur") lava.[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62)

Shortly thereafter, Fisto, Gallia, Koon, and Tiin arrived in the Lola Sayu system with their [fleet](/wiki/Lola_Sayu_task_force "Lola Sayu task force") of Star Destroyers. While Admiral [Barton Coburn](/wiki/Barton_Coburn "Barton Coburn") commanded the Republic fleet's assault on K2-B4's [blockade](/wiki/Lola_Sayu_defense_fleet "Lola Sayu defense fleet") of warships, Fisto, Gallia, and Tiin served as [wing commanders](/wiki/Wing_Commander "Wing Commander") and, in their Delta-7B interceptors, escorted Koon and Commander Wolffe's [space gunship](/wiki/Space_gunship "Space gunship") so that they could extract their comrades from the surface. Koon and Wolffe reached the appointed rendezvous point just after Sobeck arrived there with his battle droids to recapture Kenobi, Skywalker, Tano, Tarkin, and their soldiers. Frustrated by his prisoners' periodic evasion of recapture, Sobeck simply decided to kill Tarkin to ensure that his half of the Nexus Route intelligence died with him. Yet, Tano saved Tarkin by igniting her [shoto lightsaber](/wiki/Shoto_lightsaber "Shoto lightsaber") through Sobeck, killing him. Tano and her allies then escaped with Koon and Wolffe aboard their gunship, and all of them safely returned to Coburn's fleet with Fisto, Gallia, and Tiin. The Republic armada jumped to hyperspace, thereby resulting in a major defeat for the Confederacy.[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62)

On Coruscant, the Jedi Council was saddened to learn of Piell's sacrifice. Moreover, the Jedi encountered difficulties before they could debrief the Nexus Route coordinates. Whereas Tarkin had orders to provide his half of the information directly to Sheev Palpatine, Tano remained committed to Piell's dying wish that she deliver her share of the coordinates only to the High Council. Master Yoda subsequently met with Palpatine to figure out a solution to the matter. The entire incident also led Skywalker and Tarkin to find common ground based on their similar criticisms of the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") and the Jedi Order's role as generals.[[62]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-62) In addition, though Echo was presumed dead during the escape from the Citadel,[[216]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-216) he had in fact survived.[[217]](#cite_note-A_Distant_Echo-217) The Techno Union purchased Echo from the Separatists and subjected him to extensive [reconstructive surgery](/wiki/Reconstructive_surgery "Reconstructive surgery"), fusing him with a large amount of cybernetics as part of a research project.[[218]](#cite_note-On_the_Wings_of_Keeradaks-218)

#### Conflict returns to Felucia[]

:   "*Droid reinforcements have just arrived. We shall break into three groups to divide their defenses. I'll take the left flank. Skywalker, attack the front gate, Ahsoka, you scale the back wall, we'll meet in the middle.*"
:   ―Plo Koon — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/SecondBattleofFelucia1.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250327205652)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:SecondBattleofFelucia1.flac "File:SecondBattleofFelucia1.flac"))[[219]](#cite_note-Padawan_Lost-219)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Second Battle of Felucia](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Felucia "Second Battle of Felucia")
 [![During the Battle of Felucia, Ahsoka Tano leads the Republic's charge into Separatist-held territory.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TanoRexFelucia-PL.png/revision/latest?cb=20130530012950) [![During the Battle of Felucia, Ahsoka Tano leads the Republic's charge into Separatist-held territory.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TanoRexFelucia-PL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20130530012950)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TanoRexFelucia-PL.png/revision/latest?cb=20130530012950) 

During the Battle of Felucia, Ahsoka Tano leads the Republic's charge into Separatist-held territory.

 

Later in the war, the Grand Army reopened Felucia as a battlefront against the Separatist Droid Army. As part of the [Second Battle of Felucia](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Felucia "Second Battle of Felucia"), Rex, Skywalker, and Tano led [divisions](/wiki/Division "Division") of AT-TE walkers and [HAVw A6 Juggernauts](/wiki/HAVw_A6_Juggernaut "HAVw A6 Juggernaut") deep into Confederate-controlled territory. To preserve his grip on the Felucia system, General Grievous dispatched a C-9979 landing craft with droid reinforcements to tactical droid [TZ-33](/wiki/TZ-33 "TZ-33")'s [outpost](/wiki/Separatist_outpost_(Felucia) "Separatist outpost (Felucia)") on Felucia. With the aid of Plo Koon, Skywalker and Tano mounted a three-pronged offensive on TZ-33's base. Once their AT-TE walkers launched a volley of fire at the outpost and baited TZ-33 to deploy his droid infantry through the facility's front gate, Rex and Skywalker led a squad to breach the front gate's defenses. While Koon, Commander Wolffe, and their jetpack-equipped troopers charged the outpost's left flank, Tano worked with Sergeant Sinker, [Corporal](/wiki/Clone_Corporal "Clone Corporal") [Comet](/wiki/Comet_(clone_trooper) "Comet (clone trooper)"), and Boost and other soldiers to scale the rear wall. All three teams converged at the outpost's central command post, where they eliminated TZ-33 and his remaining infantry.[[219]](#cite_note-Padawan_Lost-219)

However, Tano found herself unable to help her allies sack TZ-33's outpost. She was declared missing in action after [Trandoshan](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan") hunters captured her and brought her to the moon [Wasskah](/wiki/Wasskah "Wasskah"), where the Trandoshans [hunted](/wiki/Battle_on_Wasskah "Battle on Wasskah") her and other captives for sport. In spite of numerous perimeter sweeps of TZ-33's outpost, Koon and Skywalker failed to find Tano, and they withdrew their forces from Felucia the following morning.[[219]](#cite_note-Padawan_Lost-219) Nevertheless, Tano returned to active duty after escaping from Wasskah with several Jedi younglings, who had also been stranded there for quite some time.[[220]](#cite_note-Wookiee_Hunt-220)

#### Civil war on Mon Cala[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Battle of Mon Cala](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala")

 [![Mon Calamari warriors combat Quarren warriors](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022032555) [![Mon Calamari warriors combat Quarren warriors](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20111022032555)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022032555) 

Mon Calamari warriors combat Quarren warriors

 

Following the murder of [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") King, [Yos Kolina](/wiki/Yos_Kolina "Yos Kolina"), the Separatists and the Republic sent representatives to assist in the ascension of a new king. The [Quarren Isolation League](/wiki/Quarren_Isolation_League "Quarren Isolation League") under Chieftain [Nossor Ri](/wiki/Nossor_Ri "Nossor Ri") wanted a [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") king, not Kolina's son, [Prince](/wiki/Prince "Prince") [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char"), to rule. The Separatist observer Commander [Riff Tamson](/wiki/Riff_Tamson "Riff Tamson") stirred the Quarren against the Republic, Mon Calamari and the Prince. The Prince's military, Captain [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar"), Senators Padmé Amidala, and [Meena Tills](/wiki/Meena_Tills "Meena Tills") tried to negotiate with the Quarren to no avail. The Jedi Council then sent Master Kit Fisto and Commander Ahsoka Tano to reinforce Anakin Skywalker and the [Mon Calamari Guard](/wiki/Mon_Calamari_Guard "Mon Calamari Guard") against the Quarren's and Tamson's forces.[[33]](#cite_note-Water_War-33)

At first, the Republic and the Mon Calamari held out against the Separatist forces after Commander [Monnk](/wiki/Monnk "Monnk")'s [SCUBA troopers](/wiki/Clone_SCUBA_trooper "Clone SCUBA trooper") reinforced them. However, the Republic forces were forced to retreat with the prince to the depths below when Tamson blew up their ship.[[33]](#cite_note-Water_War-33)

Meanwhile, the Jedi High Council had called the Gungan Grand Army to reinforce the prince and his forces. Tamson countered this when he rallied his Trident ships to create whirlpools around the battle sites. Tamson attempted to personally take out the prince, but Kit Fisto engaged him long enough for Lee-Char and Ahsoka Tano to escape.[[39]](#cite_note-Gungan_attack-39)

Skywalker, Amidala, Fisto, and Binks were eventually captured by Tamson, who tortured them for answers using [Mon Calamari eels](/wiki/Mon_Cala_eel "Mon Cala eel"), although to no avail. To get an answer faster, Tamson bit a hole in Amidala's helmet. However, he soon rushed back to the throne room when he learned that Lee-Char was apprehended. With Tamson gone, Fisto and Skywalker used the Force to remove the water from Amidala's helmet, and Binks sealed the puncture with his saliva.[[42]](#cite_note-Prisoners-42)

 [![Prince Lee-Char killed Riff Tamson when the Confederate warlord attacked him, helping to bring an end to the Battle of Mon Cala.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Lee-charkillstamson-TCW-S4E3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924181411) [![Prince Lee-Char killed Riff Tamson when the Confederate warlord attacked him, helping to bring an end to the Battle of Mon Cala.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Lee-charkillstamson-TCW-S4E3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110924181411)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Lee-charkillstamson-TCW-S4E3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924181411) 

Prince Lee-Char killed Riff Tamson when the Confederate warlord attacked him, helping to bring an end to the Battle of Mon Cala.

 

Meanwhile, Tamson sentenced Lee-Char to public execution while proclaiming leadership over both the Quarren and Mon Calamari. This caused Nossir Ri to doubt what Tamson had initially promised. As the prisoners were brought to witness the execution, Ri communicated the Quarren's support to Ackbar, who united all the prisoners. Just before the prince was executed, the Quarren, Mon Calamari, Jedi, Gungans, and clones engaged the droids in battle once again. Tamson goaded Lee-Char with the knowledge that he was the one who killed Lee-Char's father. The prince pursued him as he tried to escape by throwing explosive knives at the Mon Calamari. Lee-Char stabbed Tamson with one of the knives and shot it, killing the Separatist warlord and leaving his remains to sink.[[42]](#cite_note-Prisoners-42)

After the battle and the defeat of the CIS forces, Lee-Char was crowned the new king of the Quarren and Mon Calamari.[[42]](#cite_note-Prisoners-42)

#### Failed peace conference on Mandalore[]

:   "*The Republic recognizes the tragedy of war, but there is nothing we can change that has already occurred.*"  
    "*Say it aloud before this gathering—as representative for Chancellor Palpatine that* you *declare, without reservation, the Separatist state* legitimate*.*"
:   ―Senators Padmé Amidala and Voe Atell[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Confederate–Republic peace conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference")

In an effort to end the Clone Wars, the Republic and Separatists held their first ever sanctioned [peace conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference") on Mandalore, as the planet was neutral ground. Many held hope for the meeting, and Senator Amidala, who was joined by Padawan Tano, was one of the Republic's representatives. During the conference, after Confederate Senator [Voe Atell](/wiki/Voe_Atell "Voe Atell") demanded her to, Amidala was reluctant to declare the CIS a legitimate government. At that moment, however, their meeting was interrupted by the uninvited Lux Bonteri, who told those assembled that his mother Mina had been killed by Count Dooku. [Separatist Congress Leader](/wiki/Separatist_Congress_Leader "Separatist Congress Leader") [Bec Lawise](/wiki/Bec_Lawise "Bec Lawise") immediately rejected the claim and ordered their commando droids to take the so-called traitor away.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

 [![Members of the Republic and Separatist Senates meet on Mandalore in an ultimately failed peace conference.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) [![Members of the Republic and Separatist Senates meet on Mandalore in an ultimately failed peace conference.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20121211041358)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) 

Members of the Republic and Separatist Senates meet on Mandalore in an ultimately failed peace conference.

 

Afterward, while Lawise was willing to continue the meeting, Amidala secretly allowed Tano,[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171) who had met Bonteri during Amidala and Mina's earlier peace initiative,[[54]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-54) to follow the droids, as the Jedi Padawan knew her friend's life was in danger. Unknown to her, Bonteri had planned on being captured, as he had wanted to get Dooku's attention. Believing they were a noble group, Bonteri had allied with Death Watch, who also wanted revenge on the Count, and planned on using a [holotrace device](/wiki/Holotrace_device "Holotrace device") to locate Dooku, which would allow Death Watch to attack him.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

Brought into a C-9979 landing craft by the pair of commandos, Bonteri was dropped before a hologram of the Count. While Bonteri was able to activate his holotrace device, Dooku ordered the droids to kill the young man, but, after the Count's hologram deactivated, Tano entered the room and took out the commandos. During their escape, Tano contacted R2-D2, ordering him to activate the engines on their [GX1 short hauler](/wiki/GX1_short_hauler "GX1 short hauler"), the [*Phoenix*](/wiki/Phoenix_(GX1_short_hauler) "Phoenix (GX1 short hauler)"), and she and Bonteri were chased by a force of commando droids. Staying ahead of the droids, they reached the starship and were given covering fire by Captain [Taggart's](/wiki/Taggart_(Senate_Guard) "Taggart (Senate Guard)") forces.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

Aboard the GX1 with R2, they spoke with General Skywalker over hologram, who revealed the peace conference had all but collapsed. Although Tano intended to bring Bonteri to safety on Coruscant, where she and Skywalker could discuss giving the former Separatist amnesty, he zapped her unconscious and took the *Phoenix* to Death Watch on Carlac. [During their time there](/wiki/Battle_on_Carlac "Battle on Carlac"), Bonteri gave the holotrace to Pre Vizsla, but he also saw the group's true colors when they burned a [Ming Po Town](/wiki/Ming_Po_Town "Ming Po Town"). With the help of a group of droids Death Watch had been keeping as target practice, he, Tano, and R2 escaped the terrorists. Thinking he could not go with her, Bonteri still refused to go to the Republic and, after promising Tano that he would see her again, left the *Phoenix* aboard an escape pod.[[171]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-171)

#### Cortosis plot[]

##### Involvement of the Chiss and Grysks[]

One month before the [mission to Batuu](/wiki/Mission_to_Batuu "Mission to Batuu"), R2-D2 was shot by a [B2-RP super battle droid](/wiki/B2-RP_battle_droid "B2-RP battle droid") when he had wanted to see what was unfolding; it had then taken technicians three days to rebuild R2.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) Meanwhile, the [Chiss Ascendancy](/wiki/Chiss_Ascendancy "Chiss Ascendancy"), an empire that controlled part of the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions"),[[221]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New-221) kept watch on the rest of the galaxy[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) and came to learn that a massive war was being fought there. Though their reports were unconfirmed, the [Chiss](/wiki/Chiss "Chiss") also learned that one side largely used droids in combat. During the [Nikardun conquests](/wiki/Nikardun_conquests "Nikardun conquests") they faced at the same time as the Clone Wars, Chiss [Senior Captain](/wiki/Senior_Captain "Senior Captain") [Mitth'raw'nuruodo](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"), also known by his [core name](/wiki/Core_name "Core name") of "Thrawn," and Force-sensitive [sky-walker](/wiki/Sky-walker "Sky-walker") navigator [Che'ri](/wiki/Che%27ri "Che'ri") journeyed into the galaxy to search for allies against the [Nikardun](/wiki/Nikardun "Nikardun"). Che'ri's [caregiver](/wiki/Caregiver "Caregiver"), [Mitth'ali'astov](/wiki/Mitth%27ali%27astov "Mitth'ali'astov") "Thalias," was originally supposed to come with them, although she remained in the Ascendancy in order to complete her [Mitth family](/wiki/Mitth_family "Mitth family") [Trials](/wiki/Trials "Trials").[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2)

 [![Senior Captain Thrawn of the Chiss Ascendancy became involved in the Clone Wars while looking for allies.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/GreaterGood-OOP-Art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220915163616) [![Senior Captain Thrawn of the Chiss Ascendancy became involved in the Clone Wars while looking for allies.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/GreaterGood-OOP-Art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/253?cb=20220915163616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/GreaterGood-OOP-Art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220915163616) 

Senior Captain Thrawn of the Chiss Ascendancy became involved in the Clone Wars while looking for allies.

 

After finding nothing of value on the first four worlds they checked, Thrawn and Che'ri spotted a force of Separatist droid starfighters stationed at[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) the planet [Mokivj](/wiki/Mokivj "Mokivj"). The Confederacy had taken over Mokivj after a then-unknown species—the [Grysks](/wiki/Grysk "Grysk")—provided intelligence to Dooku by telling him the metal [cortosis](/wiki/Cortosis "Cortosis") could block lightsaber strikes. Dooku dispatched Duke [Solha](/wiki/Solha "Solha"), as well as the Duke's [brother](/wiki/Solha%27s_brother "Solha's brother") and [sister](/wiki/Solha%27s_sister "Solha's sister"), to oversee a [cortosis mine](/wiki/Cortosis_mine "Cortosis mine") and [droid factory](/wiki/Mokivj_droid_factory "Mokivj droid factory"), the latter producing[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) the [C-B3 cortosis battle droid](/wiki/C-B3_cortosis_battle_droid "C-B3 cortosis battle droid"),[[222]](#cite_note-Official_Magazine_118-222) a B2-series super battle droid with cortosis armor able to block blasters and lightsabers. To the confusion of the Grysks, the factory also produced clone trooper armor made from cortosis, as Darth Sidious planned to use the metal to help in the execution of Order 66. The factory was protected by a deflector shield,[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) which Thrawn spotted and realized could be of great use to the Ascendancy.[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2)

Directly afterward, Thrawn and Che'ri spotted another ship watching the droid starfighters, so the Senior Captain ordered Che'ri to navigate their ship to the first planet they had investigated in order to get there first, reasoning that, by being the most populous, it was the most likely destination for the other craft to rendezvous or send a message from. Indeed being the first to arrive at the planet, which was the Outer Rim world of [Batuu](/wiki/Batuu "Batuu"), Thrawn sent a communication in several [trade languages](/wiki/Trade_language "Trade language") to the other ship after it emerged from hyperspace, introducing himself as a Senior Captain of the Ascendancy and getting an answer in [Meese Caulf](/wiki/Meese_Caulf "Meese Caulf"), the second-to-last trade language he had used. The pilot of the other ship was [Duja](/wiki/Duja "Duja"),[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) who had been a [handmaiden](/wiki/Handmaiden "Handmaiden") to Padmé Amidala and had uncovered the Separatist conspiracy unfolding on Mokivj. As such, she sent that information to Amidala.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

Nevertheless, in addition to rotating her ship slightly so she could fire upon the Chiss if need be, she only told the two her name before asking whether the Chiss supported the Republic or Confederacy. When Thrawn clarified that their government served neither, she decided she had no reason to speak with the Senior Captain, only asking if he had seen a Nubian ship arrive. When Thrawn confirmed they had not, Duja ended their conversation, leaving Thrawn with the feeling she was a scout or spy. As he explained to Che'ri, who had expected him to call Duja back, her armed ship and slight rotation confirmed she had training, but he understood she was not a warrior. Thus, he reasoned the two of them would wait until a warrior arrived.[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2)

##### Mission to Batuu[]

:   «*This is no longer merely a search for a missing ambassador. It's become an important part of your Clone War. Remember that victory is the goal.*»
:   ―Senior Captain Thrawn, to Anakin Skywalker[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Mission to Batuu](/wiki/Mission_to_Batuu "Mission to Batuu")

Having received Duja's vague message that there was some kind of Separatist operation around Batuu, Republic High Command found the report too vague to act on, so Amidala decided to investigate it herself. Although she told Skywalker of her plan, noting that she would not be alone because of Duja's presence on Batuu, her husband was unable to go with her, needing to serve as the leader for an upcoming battle. Skywalker also claimed to her that the Clone Wars would indeed end one day, but he understood that everyone was questioning if the conflict would end, with only the Chancellor holding the Republic together. Promising to spend time with him once she returned, Amidala departed, and Skywalker went onto lead the battle; like many others, the engagement saw minor advancements and losses amid destruction and death. Skywalker's forces were weary after the end of the battle, returning to Coruscant after it, and Skywalker found that Amidala had yet to return nor had she sent any messages.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

With Dooku making another advance, the Jedi Council denied Skywalker's request to search for her, as he instead had to fight in another, albeit quick, battle. When he returned to Corsucant again, still without any messages, Skywalker uncovered that her Nubian ship was abandoned on Batuu.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) From space, Thrawn and Che'ri had seen Amidala's ship approach, with it arriving three days after they had spoken with Duja.[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) Amidala had tried to send messages to her husband, but Skywalker had not received them. After learning that Duja had died, Amidala retrieved a beacon call from her fallen friend's brooch, teaching her that the Separatist operation was a factory. She departed Batuu, which was only being used by Separatist smugglers to get supplies to the factory, aboard Duja's ship, the *[Possibility](/wiki/Possibility "Possibility")*,[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) a few hours after she had arrived. Thrawn and Che'ri saw the ship depart, with the navigator waiting for Nubian to follow it, only to see it remained hidden on the planet below. Days passed before[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) Skywalker arrived out of hyperspace, flying his [Eta-2 *Actis*-class light interceptor](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker%27s_Eta-2_Actis-class_interceptor "Anakin Skywalker's Eta-2 Actis-class interceptor") with R2-D2.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

 [![Senator Padmé Amidala undertook an investigation on Batuu after receiving a warning from her old friend Duja.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/PadmeAmidala-ThrawnAlliancesBNExclusivePoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20180713035357) [![Senator Padmé Amidala undertook an investigation on Batuu after receiving a warning from her old friend Duja.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/PadmeAmidala-ThrawnAlliancesBNExclusivePoster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/248?cb=20180713035357)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/PadmeAmidala-ThrawnAlliancesBNExclusivePoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20180713035357) 

Senator Padmé Amidala undertook an investigation on Batuu after receiving a warning from her old friend Duja.

 

Seeing the [hyperspace transport ring](/wiki/Hyperspace_transport_ring "Hyperspace transport ring") the Eta-2 had used to exit hyperspace, Thrawn had his ship move closer to it in order to study it, which caught the attention of R2-D2 and Skywalker. Not wanting to lose his way out of the system, Skywalker sent out a transmission in [Galactic Basic Standard](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard "Galactic Basic Standard") before repeating it in Meese Caulf, asking for the identity of the crew and identifying himself. While he responded, Thrawn doubted Skywalker's claim that he was on a mission, understanding that a government at war would not send a lone starfighter. Lying by insisting he was not on a personal quest, Skywalker claimed that Palpatine, who actually did not know Skywalker was at Batuu, had sent him on the mission, understanding that the man he was speaking with likely knew of the Chancellor if he knew of the war. When Thrawn revealed he knew where the Nubian was, having deduced Skywalker was looking for the ship, he offered an alliance, claiming to be alone before Skywalker felt Che'ri's presence through the Force. Nevertheless, Thrawn went onto mention his "pilot" before learning R2 would be joining them for their mission. Upon the Chiss explaining he wanted to know more about the Clone Wars before it could sweep in the Ascendancy's own worlds, he also finally introduced himself.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

However, Thrawn claimed to be a commander, instead of stating his actual rank of Senior Captain, and never mentioned his desire to take the shield generator[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) from Mokivj. Skywalker agreed to the alliance, hoping the Ascendancy he now knew of may become an ally to the Republic. While Skywalker elected to fly down to Batuu in his Eta-2, Thrawn elected to take a shuttle to lead the way to the Nubian's location,[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) as he ordered Che'ri to take their ship back to the [Mokivj system](/wiki/Mokivj_system "Mokivj system") so that, when he arrived, she could fly down to retrieve the shield generator. He ordered her to use as many decoys as needed to keep the droid starfighters away once he signaled her.[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) Upon landing, after he fought a group of smugglers who had found the ship, Skywalker investigated the Nubian while Thrawn and R2 remained outside to search for clues.
