All three then departed for [Black Spire Outpost](/wiki/Black_Spire_Outpost "Black Spire Outpost") aboard Thrawn's shuttle.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

##### Devastation of Mokivj[]

:   "*But you really should reconsider Padmé's offer. The Republic's going to win this war, and Chancellor Palpatine is the one who'll lead us to that victory. The Chiss Ascendancy would do well to establish good relations with him.*"  
    "*Perhaps someday. But for now, I must depart. I'll wait in orbit until you depart to guard against further attacks. Safe travels to you both.*"
:   ―Jedi General Anakin Skywalker and Senior Captain Thrawn[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Mission to Mokivj](/wiki/Mission_to_Mokivj "Mission to Mokivj")

In time, Skywalker and Thrawn learned of the smuggling operation for Mokivj, which they learned was under the command of Solha, and that a [ring of thieves](/wiki/Unidentified_ring_of_thieves "Unidentified ring of thieves") was stealing from the operation. Before leaving Batuu, Skywalker informed Thrawn about Dooku, Grievous, and Palpatine, and Thrawn advised him to remember that, in war, his goal should remain victory instead of revenge. On Mokivj, Amidala, having crashed landed the *Possibility* after being attacked by a vulture droid, bribed three locals named [Cimy](/wiki/Cimy "Cimy"), [Huga](/wiki/Huga "Huga"), and [LebJau](/wiki/Nodlia "Nodlia") to keep her presence a secret, and Thrawn, Skywalker, and R2 landed at the Separatist factory with the captured CIS freighter *[Larkrer](/wiki/Larkrer "Larkrer")*, initially pretending to be its crew before they were captured. The Chiss and Jedi ultimately escaped their improvised cells. Joined by Huga and Cimy, Amidala, who had witnessed the arrest of her husband and his allies, and her allies disguised themselves as maintenance workers to head to the detention block, with the Senator taking out two B1 battle droids guarding it. Upon entering, she united with Skywalker and Thrawn. As Skywalker served as a distraction, Amidala and Thrawn journeyed to retrieve the Jedi's lightsaber.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

 [![General Anakin Skywalker and Senior Captain Thrawn worked together to investigate a Separatist conspiracy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223163431) [![General Anakin Skywalker and Senior Captain Thrawn worked together to investigate a Separatist conspiracy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/255?cb=20200223163431)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223163431) 

General Anakin Skywalker and Senior Captain Thrawn worked together to investigate a Separatist conspiracy.

 

Amidala also convinced Lebjau to evacuate the workers for their plan to destroy the factory. Skywalker found himself in the B2 assembly line, where he saw Solha, his brother, and his sister in suits of clone trooper armor. As Skywalker distracted the duke and his forces in the assembly room, Thrawn and Amidala found Skywalker's lightsaber, but the Chiss used the blade to cut out the shield generator core, claiming he had been given a mission to retrieve the generator. While Amidala protested the idea of him leaving, Thrawn remained steadfast in his commitment to the Chiss and additionally asked why the Republic had not allowed the Confederacy to secede peacefully. After she stated the Confederacy had attacked first, Thrawn advised her to use the south end's door before she was out of his sight.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

However, Thrawn made sure to return to helping shortly afterward, wielding a [lightning gun](/wiki/Lightning_gun "Lightning gun") to help take down the cortosis B2s. He also explained what the metal, which Skywalker had realized—in his battle against the droids—could resist lightsaber strikes, was and how it was rare. Additionally, the team elected to discover what the northern wing of the factory was producing. After R2 worked to reprogram the B2 factory, Amidala was confronted by Solha, while Skywalker and Thrawn uncovered the north wing was producing cortosis-weaved clone armor; Skywalker quickly assumed Dooku was planning a mass-[Serennian](/wiki/Serennian "Serennian") infiltration of the clone army as a surprise attack. After Amidala knocked out Sophla, Skywalker ensured the factory was destroyed, yet he also sought to destroy the Cortosis mine. Thrawn confided to Amidala that he believed the Jedi General's plan was reckless, arguing that it would be better for the CIS to waste resources on Mokivj than to make them to look elsewhere.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

Although she agreed, the Senator understood that her husband could not be talked out of his plan, even though Thrawn warned her it could be a threat to Mokivj. He also declined her offer to return to Coruscant with them to create a more formal Chiss—Republic alliance, stating he had other duties to attend to and that he was not tasked with such a role. Before departing, Thrawn also advised them that the clone armor may have not been intended for an infiltration, as such operations had a high risk of failing. Although Thrawn disagreed, Skywalker was certain that they did not need to worry about the plan. Skywalker's plan to collapse the mining tunnels would indeed have unintended consequences; as he, Amidala, and LebJau, who had asked to leave with them to start a new life on Batuu, watched from their ship, the cortosis redirected the explosives' heat, causing a [catastrophe](/wiki/Mission_to_Mokivj "Mission to Mokivj") that, despite not moving towards the people of Mokivj, would devastate the environment of the world. While Amidala promised they would talk to the Senate about providing aid, all three understood it would do nothing, and they departed from the planet.[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47)

Upon his return to the Republic, Skywalker told Palpatine about Thrawn and praised the tactician. Thrawn, meanwhile, respected Skywalker greatly,[[94]](#cite_note-Thrawn-94) although he had come to the conclusion that the Republic was not a suitable ally for his people.[[221]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New-221) Additionally, he used the shielding technology from Mokivj to great effect in the [battle over Primea](/wiki/Battle_over_Primea "Battle over Primea"), blocking blasts from the [Nikardun Battle Dreadnought](/wiki/Nikardun_Battle_Dreadnought "Nikardun Battle Dreadnought") *[Deathless](/wiki/Deathless "Deathless")* in order to board its bridge. After the Chiss victory in that battle, the [Nikardun Destiny](/wiki/Nikardun_Destiny "Nikardun Destiny") and its conquests came to an end.[[2]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-2) Rumors of a blue alien forming an alliance with Skywalker also spread in the galaxy, with the story coming to reach at least as far as the [Thrugii asteroid belt](/wiki/Thrugii_asteroid_belt "Thrugii asteroid belt").[[94]](#cite_note-Thrawn-94) Rather than correctly report[[222]](#cite_note-Official_Magazine_118-222) on Skywalker triggering the catastrophe that devastated Mokivj,[[47]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-47) [Clone Intelligence](/wiki/Clone_Intelligence "Clone Intelligence") reported that the Chiss Expansionary Defense Fleet was responsible for the catastrophe.[[222]](#cite_note-Official_Magazine_118-222)

### Last days of the Republic[]

#### Final days of democracy[]

:   "*Thank you all for attending. I know we can count on the signatures, but I've invited this group to discuss the exact wording of the petition.*"  
    "*In broad strokes, our demands are that Chancellor Palpatine relinquish the emergency war powers granted to him, abolish the Sector Governance Decree, and begin cease-fire talks with Count Dooku's Separatists.*"  
    "*Are we going too far? The war is popular in my sector. We would be seen by many as obstructing an inevitable victory.*"  
    "*People are dying, Senator. The longer this conflict drags out, the more loopholes Palpatine will find for amending the constitution.*"
:   ―Bail Organa, Mon Mothma, Terr Taneel, and Padmé Amidala discuss the Petition of 2,000[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223)

 [![Palpatine controlled the Clone Wars to consolidate the powers of the Republic in his own hands, setting the stage for his reign as Emperor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/InSidiousSmile-Revival.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121010231653) [![Palpatine controlled the Clone Wars to consolidate the powers of the Republic in his own hands, setting the stage for his reign as Emperor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/InSidiousSmile-Revival.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20121010231653)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/InSidiousSmile-Revival.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121010231653) 

Palpatine controlled the Clone Wars to consolidate the powers of the Republic in his own hands, setting the stage for his reign as Emperor.

 

Thanks to the Emergency Powers Act from the beginning of the Separatist Crisis, Palpatine remained in power for the entirety of the Clone Wars,[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) although his prolonged time in office did begin to draw suspicion from the Jedi as the war reached its end[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) and relations between the Jedi and the Chancellor continued to break down.[[60]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-60) As per his plans to transform the Republic into an autocracy with himself at its top,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) Palpatine used the Clone Wars to further cement his political power and undermine the democracy[[224]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Beginning-224) he claimed to represent.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) By the end of the war, Maul had come to believe the Republic was long since dead and there was nothing the Jedi could do to save it.[[225]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-225) Indeed, while senators like Mon Mothma, who would oppose Palpatine's power grabs, were distracted by the conflict with the Separatists, Palpatine, Amedda, and his other supporters waged a war of their own in the field of public relations, securing the love and mandate of the people.[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17)

Palpatine managed to amend the [Galactic Constitution](/wiki/Galactic_Constitution "Galactic Constitution") again and again, always using the war as his excuse[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) to secure more power for himself.[[226]](#cite_note-Bail_SWE-226) Although the Enhanced Privacy Invasion Bill was defeated in the Senate,[[13]](#cite_note-Rise-13) a number of other emergency war powers were passed,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) with Palpatine becoming the most powerful chancellor since the [Ruusan Reformations](/wiki/Ruusan_Reformations "Ruusan Reformations"). In particular, four amendments to the constitution were cemented in law: one of the four was the [Reflex Amendment](/wiki/Reflex_Amendment "Reflex Amendment"), which granted Palpatine expansive powers by ceding near-total power over the Republic Military to Palpatine, who could thus bypass the Senate on military decisions.[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) The [Sector Governance Decree](/wiki/Sector_Governance_Decree "Sector Governance Decree") was an amendment passed near the end of the war on the claim that it would bring unity and sure up the supply line; under the decree, Palpatine was granted the ability to name individuals[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) regional governors,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) who would then unify neighboring star systems and focus their resources on the production of war materiel.[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115)

In practice, however, the existence of regional governors served to circumvent the power of the Senate by creating a new group of officials,[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) named by Palpatine himself,[[115]](#cite_note-OF84-115) with power over star systems.[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) Despite Palpatine's efforts to consolidate power attracting criticism from some senators, most defended it as a necessary evil in the name of defeating the Confederacy, which Dooku exercised near-total control over.[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) Dooku's own war powers saw opposition from his senate's Peace Faction,[[13]](#cite_note-Rise-13) but he continued to enjoy wide support amongst the Confederacy overall.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21) However, the Sector Governance Decree proved to be the final erosion of senatorial authority for a group of like-minded senators who became known as the [Delegation of 2,000](/wiki/Delegation_of_2,000 "Delegation of 2,000"). Under the leadership of Senators Organa, Amidala, and Mothma,[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) who specifically recognized Palpatine as a threat to democracy but failed to understand the scope of his ambitions,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) the group created a formal petition[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) known as the [Petition of 2,000](/wiki/Petition_of_2,000 "Petition of 2,000") in protest of the Chancellor's conduct[[228]](#cite_note-Meena_Tills-228) and acquired powers.[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40)

 [![Several members of the Delegation of 2,000 discuss Palpatine's growing wartime powers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8a/2000_meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20160817194033) [![Several members of the Delegation of 2,000 discuss Palpatine's growing wartime powers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8a/2000_meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20160817194033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8a/2000_meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20160817194033) 

Several members of the Delegation of 2,000 discuss Palpatine's growing wartime powers.

 

Broadly, the petition had three demands: Palpatine was to give up his emergency powers[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) by returning those powers to the Senate at the end of the war,[[228]](#cite_note-Meena_Tills-228) abolish the Sector Governance Decree in particular, and open a cease-fire with the Confederacy. In what would end up being the final month of the war,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) the three leaders of the delegation[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) began the [Cantham House meetings](/wiki/Cantham_House_meetings "Cantham House meetings") by gathering a select number of like-minded senators to discuss and finalize their petition,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) which they intended to present once it acquired two thousand signatures. By its end, the Clone War was losing the support of the public. The conflict brought great suffering, war taxes, and rationing, with even the Core Worlds being affected.[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40) Although the war remained popular in the [Senex sector](/wiki/Senex_sector "Senex sector"), whose people saw a Republic victory as an inevitability,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) a number of other senators faced great pressure from those they represented to push for peace. However, powerful lobbyists in the Senate managed to vote down those efforts in order to protect their war profits.[[40]](#cite_note-Collapse-40)

While she was indeed worried about Palpatine's growing power,[[229]](#cite_note-Terr_Taneel_Files-229) Senator [Terr Taneel](/wiki/Terr_Taneel "Terr Taneel") of the Senex sector was nervous about pressing for the end of the war and noted as such during a Cantham House meeting, citing her sector's support for the conflict. Amidala, however, defended it as necessity to both stop the bloodshed and Palpatine's excuse for creating amendments.[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) The delegation backed public calls for Palpatine to abandon his increased power as their public tactic. The group secretly prepared itself to go beyond the Senate and form a resistance effort should that be needed.[[230]](#cite_note-Rebel_Alliance_DB-230)

#### Battle over Coruscant[]

:   "*Ahsoka, surely you understand this is a pivotal moment in the Clone Wars? The heart of the Republic is under attack!*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Ahsoka Tano[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91)

 [![Towards the end of the war the Separatists launched a large-scale attack on the Republic's capital, Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/SiegeOfCoruscantScenarioPack-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20220718004934) [![Towards the end of the war the Separatists launched a large-scale attack on the Republic's capital, Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/SiegeOfCoruscantScenarioPack-SWZ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220718004934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/SiegeOfCoruscantScenarioPack-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20220718004934) 

Towards the end of the war the Separatists launched a large-scale attack on the Republic's capital, Coruscant.

 

The [super tactical droid](/wiki/ST-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") General [Kalani](/wiki/Kalani "Kalani") would state his calculations showed the Separatists were on the verge of victory at the war's end.[[231]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-231) Alternatively, the war's third year made others assume that the Republic now held all of the momentum.[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51) Ultimately, however, both sides were in crisis by the end of the war.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51) The Republic was crumbling due to Separatist attacks ordered by Dooku,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) while the Separatists had been pushed back to the spiral arms of the galaxy. A campaign called the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges") would result in most of the Republic's Jedi and military forces fighting on these outer worlds.[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51) However, another part of the sieges occurred when Grievous launched a massive assault that pushed the Republic Military to the brink, so Jedi Generals were also sent far from the Core Worlds to help the clone army because of that offensive.[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91)

Ultimately, while the Republic had begun to overwhelm the Separatist armies and the Confederacy had lost much of its territory, with what remained being targeted in the sieges,[[232]](#cite_note-CIS_History_Gallery_Image_1-232) Grievous's overwhelming offensive was still a threat,[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91) and the Republic Army was also engaging in desperate campaigns across the galaxy, while the Separatists were encircling the Republic, moving ever-nearer to the systems of the Core.[[96]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles_2018-96) Nevertheless, despite being a bitter stalemate for a time,[[233]](#cite_note-Separatist_Racketeer-233) the sieges would ultimately turn the tide of the conflict to be in the Republic's favor.[[234]](#cite_note-SW_Book-234)

During the Outer Rim sieges, Kenobi, Skywalker, and their troops [captured](/wiki/Battle_of_Yerbana "Battle of Yerbana") [Yerbana](/wiki/Yerbana "Yerbana") from the Confederacy. Following the victory, one of their "[Fulcrum](/wiki/Fulcrum "Fulcrum")" contacts reached out to them. At first, Skywalker believed it was Gerrara requesting aid from the Republic due the [Siege at Onderon](/wiki/Siege_at_Onderon "Siege at Onderon"). In was revealed that Fulcrum was Skywalker's former apprentice, Ahsoka Tano. She was working with [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze") and the [Mandalorian resistance](/wiki/Mandalore_resistance "Mandalore resistance") in tracking down Maul[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91), following his brief [capture](/wiki/Battle_of_Mandalore "Battle of Mandalore")[[6]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-6) and escape from Lord Sidious on Dathomir.[[235]](#cite_note-Son-235) Kryze informed Kenobi and Skywalker that Maul was in Sundari according to transmissions between the Pykes and Maul. Kenobi and Skywalker were willing to speak the Jedi Council on this matter and help her.[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91)

During the final days of the conflict, the Republic space station *[Sentinel Flare](/wiki/Sentinel_Flare "Sentinel Flare")* was [attacked](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Sentinel_Flare "Attack on the Sentinel Flare") by the Confederacy, which left the station severely damaged.[[236]](#cite_note-Fully_Operational-236) Prior to the war's end, Jedi General [Weren Dal](/wiki/Weren_Dal "Weren Dal") was shot down over Dathomir by an elite Separatist group.[[237]](#cite_note-Savage-237) Due to most Jedi and clones fighting in the Outer Rim, the Republic's capital of Coruscant was left relatively undefended. However, Republic strategists did not worry. They believed the Separatists would not dare attack the capital, but Grievous and Dooku launched a massive [assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") on Coruscant. The inexperienced [Coruscant Home Defense Fleet](/wiki/Coruscant_Home_Defense_Fleet "Coruscant Home Defense Fleet") was taken by surprise, and Grievous was able to sneak onto the surface of the planet.[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51)

 [![The leader of the Separatist Alliance, Count Dooku, was killed by Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210063803) [![The leader of the Separatist Alliance, Count Dooku, was killed by Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130210063803)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210063803) 

The leader of the Separatist Alliance, Count Dooku, was killed by Anakin Skywalker.

 

Grievous eventually managed to capture Palpatine and hold him hostage. Palpatine's capture was actually orchestrated by Sidious, as the latter desired Anakin to kill Dooku, in order to seduce the young Jedi to the dark Side and eventually have him replace Dooku as Sidious's apprentice, though both Dooku and Grievous were unaware of the Sith Lords' true intention. Grievous brought the Chancellor back to his flagship, the *[Invisible Hand](/wiki/Invisible_Hand "Invisible Hand")*.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) After sending the [332nd Division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division") under Commanders Rex and Tano to assist Lady Kryze in hunting Maul Down on Mandalore, Kenobi and Skywalker took their forces to Coruscant.[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91) The large-scale naval battle between the Separatist and Republic forces continued, and during this attack Kenobi and Skywalker raced to save the Chancellor. Dooku was defeated by Anakin and subsequently betrayed by Sidious who had him killed by Anakin.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) Dooku's death was a massive blow to the Separatists and left Grievous as its new [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State").[[51]](#cite_note-OTFL-51) The Separatists, however, were unaware that Sidious orchestrated Dooku's death. The Jedi managed to escape the ship along with the Chancellor. Grievous also escaped and fled to the planet [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

#### Siege at Mandalore[]

During the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore"), Tano, Kryze, and their force of clone troopers and Mandalorians led their attack against the [Mandalorian super commandos](/wiki/Mandalorian_super_commando "Mandalorian super commando") under Prime Minister Almec and Gar Saxon. Tano and Kryze were able to capture Almec but Maul and Saxon hid in the undercity.[[91]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-91)

Maul and Saxon were able to elude Tano, her troops, and Kryze's Mandalorians. During this time, Kenobi told Tano and Kryze about Darth Sidious, the man behind events leading up to and during the Clone Wars.[[225]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-225)

#### Rise of the New Order[]

:   "*After you have killed all the Jedi in the Temple, go to the Mustafar system. Wipe out Viceroy Gunray and the other Separatist leaders. Once more the Sith will rule the galaxy! And we shall have… peace.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious to his new apprentice, Darth Vader[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![The Republic launched an invasion against Utapau led by Obi-Wan Kenobi to confront Grievous and end the war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) [![The Republic launched an invasion against Utapau led by Obi-Wan Kenobi to confront Grievous and end the war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130215052829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) 

The Republic launched an invasion against Utapau led by Obi-Wan Kenobi to confront Grievous and end the war.

 

On Utapau, Grievous, along with the rest of the leaders of the Confederacy of Independent Systems, awaited instructions from Sidious, who soon enough sent the Confederacy to the Mustafar system before Republic [forces](/wiki/Obi-Wan%27s_fleet "Obi-Wan's fleet") arrive. Not long after, Republic forces led by Obi-Wan Kenobi attacked the base. Kenobi managed to confront Grievous and the two began to fight. In the hassle, Kenobi managed to rip open the armor covering Grievous' gut sack. The Jedi then shot it with the General's blaster several times, killing the cyborg. The death of Grievous put Nute Gunray in charge. Meanwhile, on Coruscant, Palpatine revealed his true nature as the Dark Lord of the Sith to Skywalker, prompting him to inform Jedi Master Windu. Not long after, Windu along with Fisto, Tiin, and [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar") attacked the Chancellor. Palpatine quickly admitted to this and killed Windu's team. Despite being disarmed and nearly killed by Windu, a desperate Anakin Skywalker who needed Sidious to save his wife Padmé from death, betrayed Windu which allowed Sidious to kill the Jedi. The Sith quickly declared the Jedi the enemies of the Republic and sent out Order 66,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) which saw the biochips set off[[238]](#cite_note-Shattered-238) and brainwash the clones into betraying and turning on their Jedi generals.[[239]](#cite_note-Journeys_Beginnings-239)

Skywalker betrayed the Jedi and surrendered to Sidious, so the Sith Lord dubbed him Darth Vader. Vader was sent to the Jedi Temple where he killed every Jedi left in it. On Utapau, after Clone Commander Cody received Order 66 from Sidious, which led to his biochip immediately brainwashing him into believing that Kenobi was a traitor to the Republic, he ordered his men to fire upon Kenobi, but the Jedi survived this. On [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), Commander Gree with another clone attempted to assassinate Grand Master Yoda, however the master beheaded the two with his lightsaber before they could blast him. Many other Jedi were killed during Order 66, including Ki-Adi-Mundi, Aayla Secura, Plo Koon, [Stass Allie](/wiki/Stass_Allie "Stass Allie"), etc.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![Newly christened Darth Vader kills Viceroy Nute Gunray.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/TheDeathofNuteGunray.png/revision/latest?cb=20130213234924) [![Newly christened Darth Vader kills Viceroy Nute Gunray.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/TheDeathofNuteGunray.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130213234924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/TheDeathofNuteGunray.png/revision/latest?cb=20130213234924) 

Newly christened Darth Vader kills Viceroy Nute Gunray.

 

After murdering the Jedi on Coruscant, Vader followed Sidious's next command by heading to Mustafar to eliminate Viceroy Gunray and the rest of the Separatist leaders, who were hiding on the planet. Earlier, Sidious had duped the council into believing that Vader would protect them. After murdering the council, the fallen Jedi turned Sith Lord then received an order from Sidious to send a shutdown signal that mute all remaining Separatist droids, thus ending the war in the process.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

## Aftermath[]

### The new era[]

:   "*I take it we met during the* Clone Wars*—and that you were on the side of the* "Republic." *I wonder… How do you like your Republic now? Understand, as a* Separatist*, I fought for* freedom *but put my trust in a* corrupt *leadership.*"  
    "*You* were *the leadership—a* General*.*"  
    "*The* Jedi *were Generals. Do you truly believe they* comprehended *the cause they served? Holster your weapon, boy. We are no longer enemies. Perhaps we never were.*"
:   ―Separatist General [Kleeve](/wiki/Kleeve "Kleeve") to surviving Jedi Commander [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus")[[240]](#cite_note-Kanan_4-240)

 [![Darth Vader and the stormtroopers became symbols of the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/DarthVaderStormtrooperArmy-2015DarthVader11.png/revision/latest?cb=20240131063205) [![Darth Vader and the stormtroopers became symbols of the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/DarthVaderStormtrooperArmy-2015DarthVader11.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240131063205)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/DarthVaderStormtrooperArmy-2015DarthVader11.png/revision/latest?cb=20240131063205) 

Darth Vader and the stormtroopers became symbols of the Galactic Empire.

 

The cataclysmic[[96]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles_2018-96) Clone Wars had raged for three,[[241]](#cite_note-Clone_troopers_databank-241) almost four, years by the end[[242]](#cite_note-HC_15-242) and accomplished exactly what Palpatine had set out to achieve; the Jedi Order was destroyed, the Republic was transformed into the first [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), and the Galactic Senate into the Imperial Senate, with Palpatine as its [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) Nevertheless, during the following early months of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), the Clone Wars were not entirely over, as minor pockets of resistance, including a [force of rebels on Umbara](/wiki/Rebellion_on_Umbara "Rebellion on Umbara"), continued to fight the Republic's successor state. Accordingly, the newly formed [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") was dispatched to crush these remaining obstacles to bring about the Empire's view of peace.[[11]](#cite_note-Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel-11) The galaxy at large, however, welcomed the Empire as a way to move forward from the destruction and devastation of war. [Miyuki Trade League](/wiki/Miyuki_Trade_League "Miyuki Trade League") member [Jet Kordo](/wiki/Jet_Kordo "Jet Kordo") was not surprised by the rise of the Empire, but reflected solemnly in a journal that they did not expect the people of the galaxy to wake up to the price they were paying in return for the conflict's end.[[243]](#cite_note-Outlaws-243)

In the aftermath of the conflict and with the dawn of the Empire, Senator Organa reflected that he was unsure if there was a "right side" to the Clone Wars. In regards to the CIS, he still opposed what he deemed the cruel, destructive tactics of the CIS military and the greed of its corporate sponsors, but he did recognize there were well-meaning people amongst the Separatist state. Nonetheless, he still believed that non-violent routes had still been open for the Separatists instead of deciding to go to war. As for the Republic, meanwhile, he had come to ponder if the war had been a misdirection of sorts by those in the government who already wanted to transform the government into the Empire. He recognized that Palpatine and his followers had pushed for the fighting[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17)—something Palpatine had tried to cover up with public apprehension about going to war[[11]](#cite_note-Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel-11)—and had his own thoughts on Dooku, although he believed the particulars of Dooku's situation were not as important. Overall, he was forced to admit that, by taking part in the war, himself and everyone else involved had played into Palpatine's plan to establish the Empire.[[17]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-17)

The last remnants of the Confederacy, known as the [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts"), continued to fight the Empire.[[11]](#cite_note-Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel-11) The [Imperial Navy](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") justified its existence by claiming there was an unending war against the holdouts and a dissident rebellion against the Empire.[[96]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles_2018-96) Imperial [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") were deployed to bring former Confederate planets under the Empire's control;[[14]](#cite_note-USW-14) even the former CIS capital world of Raxus Secundus fell under [occupation](/wiki/Occupation_of_Raxus "Occupation of Raxus") during the early reign of the Empire.[[20]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-20) A day into the Imperial Era, sixty-three members of the Delegation of 2,000 were [arrested](/wiki/Senatorial_arrests "Senatorial arrests") by clone troopers on the claim that they had helped the Jedi rebellion. Organa and Mothma were among those arrested but were released by publicly declaring their loyalty lied with the Empire,[[223]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-223) which both continued to serve as senators. In secret, both used their positions as senators as a cover for rebellion.[[244]](#cite_note-Aldhani-244)[[245]](#cite_note-Part_VI-245) Amidala's death, meanwhile, was blamed on the Jedi rebellion.[[246]](#cite_note-Mon_Mothma_Base_1-246)

Also during the early reign of the Empire, the future [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") Wilhuff Tarkin led a brutal purge on the moon Antar 4 that became known as the [Antar Atrocity](/wiki/Antar_Atrocity "Antar Atrocity"). Imperial forces rounded up and killed many Koorivar and Gotals including Republic loyalists. Media coverage of the Antar Atrocity attracted considerable outrage in the Core Worlds and forced the Emperor to reassign Tarkin to overseeing the [pacification operations](/wiki/Pacification_operations_in_the_Western_Reaches "Pacification operations in the Western Reaches") in the [Western Reaches](/wiki/Western_Reaches "Western Reaches"). The brutality of the Antar Atrocity prompted other former Separatist worlds such as [Kooriva](/wiki/Kooriva "Kooriva"), Murkhana, and Raxus to surrender former Separatists to the Empire to avoid the same fate as Antar 4. Tarkin's actions earned him the animosity of former [Republic Intelligence](/wiki/Republic_Intelligence "Republic Intelligence") operatives [Berch Teller](/wiki/Berch_Teller "Berch Teller") and [Knotts](/wiki/Knotts "Knotts"), who founded a [insurgent group](/wiki/Berch_Teller%27s_rebel_cell "Berch Teller's rebel cell") consisting of survivors and witnesses of the Antar Atrocity. In [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"),[[247]](#cite_note-Tarkin_date-247) Berch Teller's cell embarked on a [campaign](/wiki/Berch_Teller_campaign "Berch Teller campaign") against Tarkin and the Empire, but it was defeated.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1)

### The unofficial conclusion[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Mission to Agamar (2 BBY)](/wiki/Mission_to_Agamar_(2_BBY) "Mission to Agamar (2 BBY)")

:   **Rex**: "*No, it was a victory. We all just won the Clone War, and you ended it, Ezra. A galaxy of senators couldn't do that. An army of Jedi, clones, and droids couldn't find the middle ground, but you did.*"
:   **Ezra**: "*Rex, all I did was point out that none of you were meant to win. You couldn't.*"
:   **Rex**: "*And we needed to hear it.*"
:   **Kalani**: "*Agreed. I am satisfied if you are, Captain.*"
:   **Rex**: "*I am.*"
:   ―Rex, Ezra Bridger, and Kalani bring an unofficial end to the Clone Wars[[231]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-231)

In [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"), a last unofficial [skirmish](/wiki/Mission_to_Agamar_(2_BBY) "Mission to Agamar (2 BBY)") occurred when the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") rebel cell encountered a Separatist holdout of still functioning battle droids, led by the [super tactical droid](/wiki/ST-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") [Kalani](/wiki/Kalani "Kalani"), while attempting to scavenge the wreckage of a Separatist supply ship. Kalani took the Spectres prisoner and, upon confirming that the group contained Clone Captain Rex, who had joined with the rebellion instead of supporting the Empire, Jedi Knight [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), and his padawan [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), forced them to run through a tactical scenario, intending to prove that the Separatists had a higher chance of victory and end the Clone Wars with a victory for the Confederacy.[[231]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-231)

While running through the scenario, Ezra Bridger observed that Rex was acting little better than a droid himself, and was struck by the futility of the exercise. While Rex and Kalani debated the meaning of the outcome, Bridger interrupted them. The young man successfully argued that the Clone Wars were never intended to be won and were only a means to an end by the faction that would become the Galactic Empire; now their goals in fighting against the Emprie aligned. After escaping from an Imperial capture attempt, both Rex and Kanan Jarrus observed that Bridger had done something that a galaxy of senators and soldiers were unable to do: get representatives of all the factions to find a middle ground, bringing a peaceful end to the Clone Wars.[[231]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-231)

### Legacy[]

:   "*I survived one war. I'm not ready for another one. I saw what it did.*"  
    "*To the Jedi?*"  
    "*To everyone.*"
:   ―Kanan Jarrus and Hera Syndulla[[248]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Rebels:_The_Siege_of_Lothal-248)

Following its creation, the Galactic Empire tried to sweep away the memories of the troubled times of the Clone Wars[[22]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-22) but also used the memory of the conflict to justify its expansion; the Empire expanded its reach across the galaxy, using the memory of the Clone Wars by promising order to a galaxy tired of war.[[249]](#cite_note-sweGE-249) After it became clear that the Empire was oppressive, however, the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") was created to oppose the Empire's rule.[[250]](#cite_note-sweRA-250) The seeds of the Alliance dated back to the Clone Wars: its roots came from the local resistance cells established by the Jedi on Confederate worlds and from the Delegation of 2,000, fulfilling that group's fear that armed resistance would be needed to restore democracy.[[230]](#cite_note-Rebel_Alliance_DB-230) Palpatine's victory in the Clone Wars lasted just over two decades, as the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") led to the fall of Palpatine and his Empire, as well as the redemption of Anakin Skywalker who renounced the persona of Vader, before dying peacefully.[[251]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-251)

Many Imperials—such as the ambitious Imperial Navy officer Thrawn, the very same Chiss who had met Anakin Skywalker during the conflict—remembered the Clone Wars as the cause of billions of deaths, hundreds of destroyed worlds, and thousands of ruined worlds clawing back from the brink. He regarded secessionist movements such as the [one](/wiki/Battle_for_Botajef "Battle for Botajef") on [Botajef](/wiki/Botajef "Botajef") as a repeat of that horror. His colleague [Eli Vanto](/wiki/Eli_N._Vanto "Eli N. Vanto") believed that the Clone Wars had bred animosity between humans and [aliens](/wiki/Alien "Alien") since several alien species had fought on the side of the Separatists. While several aliens had fought on the side of the Republic, this sentiment gave rise to a level of [xenophobia](/wiki/Xenophobia "Xenophobia") within the human-dominated Empire. Thrawn was even reprimanded by his superior, [Filia Rossi](/wiki/Filia_Rossi "Filia Rossi"), the captain of the [Blood Crow](/wiki/Blood_Crow "Blood Crow") ship, for having equipment used by the Separatists in his possession.[[94]](#cite_note-Thrawn-94) Droids were also suspect in some beings' eyes; [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin"), for example, hated all droids because Separatist battle droids had destroyed his family.[[252]](#cite_note-Chapter_8-252)

The Empire also housed veterans of the struggle in poorly maintained places like [Crispus Commons](/wiki/Crispus_Commons "Crispus Commons"), where they were forced to deal with shabby maintenance and low-paying jobs. The conspiracy behind the conflict had not yet been brought to public light, and nearly the entirety of the galaxy's population believed the war to have been exactly what it had seemed; a rebellion initiated by numerous worlds of the Mid and Outer Rims desiring independence from a corrupt and decadent central government. Despite this, some, such as [Skelly](/wiki/Skelly "Skelly"), pieced together there was a greater truth about the Clone Wars.[[22]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-22) Some individuals took part in historical re-enactments of the Clone Wars and there was also a section on the Clone Wars in the [Emperor's Museum](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Museum "Emperor's Museum") on Coruscant and although they used real footage they told a false history, which was seen by the [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature") on a tour in [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY").[[253]](#cite_note-Leia-253)

 [![In her message for Obi-Wan Kenobi, Leia Organa mentions Kenobi serving alongside her father during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915071603) [![In her message for Obi-Wan Kenobi, Leia Organa mentions Kenobi serving alongside her father during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/340?cb=20200915071603)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915071603) 

In her message for Obi-Wan Kenobi, Leia Organa mentions Kenobi serving alongside her father during the Clone Wars.

 

Wilhuff Tarkin also remained suspicious of the cause of the war even after its conclusion, and believed that some group of elite outsiders had manufactured the war for their own purposes.[[1]](#cite_note-Tarkin-1) There were those, such as Bail Organa, who remembered the bravery of those like the Jedi Knights during the Clone Wars who passed this knowledge to his daughter, Princess [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo")[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) as well as the stories such as that of the Senate hostage crisis as well as several about Obi-Wan Kenobi.[[253]](#cite_note-Leia-253) Leia would later sent a holographic message to Kenobi appealing to him in the name of his service alongside her father during the Clone Wars.[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) A couple of months after the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), a Separatist droid factory under the city of [Myrra](/wiki/Myrra "Myrra") on Akiva still had marks of Jedi lightsabers.[[92]](#cite_note-Aftermath_novel-92) It remained one of the most destructive conflicts in galactic history, with billions of casualties on both sides.[[254]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-254) After Sidious's ultimate defeat in the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") of [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[210]](#cite_note-Timelines-210) historian [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") carried out the [Exegol Excavation Project](/wiki/Exegol_Excavation_Project "Exegol Excavation Project") and discovered the extent of Palpatine's treachery in the Sith records, publishing his deception and manipulation of the Clone Wars in his historical book *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire")*.[[255]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-255)

## Behind the scenes[]

The Clone Wars were first mentioned in [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") in the [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977") original *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* film, [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope").[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) The canon details of the conflict were first revealed in the [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy") films [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones")[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) and [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

The first reference to the Clone Wars dates back to [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas")' [third draft](/wiki/The_Star_Wars:_From_The_Adventures_of_Luke_Starkiller "The Star Wars: From The Adventures of Luke Starkiller") for Episode IV, which mentioned the grizzled cyborg General Kenobi's "diary of the Clone Wars."[[256]](#cite_note-AoLS-256) The passing mentions of the Clone Wars in *A New Hope* were the only mentions of the conflict in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy").[[227]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-227) While developing the script for the [1980](/wiki/1980 "1980") sequel [*Star Wars*: Episode V *The Empire Strikes Back*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_V_The_Empire_Strikes_Back "Star Wars: Episode V The Empire Strikes Back"), Lucas considered introducing a clone character who was involved in the conflict. In [Leigh Brackett](/wiki/Leigh_Brackett "Leigh Brackett")'s first draft for Episode V, Lando Calrissian was a clone from a clone planet that was nearly ravaged in the Clone Wars, with Boba Fett being a member of a group of shocktroopers nearly wiped out by Jedi Knights during conflict.[[257]](#cite_note-Annotated_screenplay-257)

The Clone Wars was first adapted in *[Star Wars: Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: Clone Wars")* in [2003](/wiki/2003 "2003"), which has since been [retconned](/wiki/Retroactive_continuity "Retroactive continuity") by the inception of the [2008](/wiki/2008 "2008") film *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(film) "Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)")*, as well as the [animated television series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") by the same title.[[87]](#cite_note-Ambush-87) By [2014](/wiki/2014 "2014"), both *The Clone Wars* film and the television series are part of the *Star Wars* canon, as they reflected the vision of Lucas.[[258]](#cite_note-End_of_EU-258)[[259]](#cite_note-SDCC_Live_Blog-259)

In the attempt to keep the *Star Wars* toy line active after the final film in the original trilogy, [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"), [Kenner Products](/wiki/Kenner_Products "Kenner Products") devised a toy extension entitled *[The Epic Continues](/wiki/The_Epic_Continues "The Epic Continues")* that would have involved the return of an [exiled](/wiki/Exile_(punishment)/Legends "Exile (punishment)/Legends") "genetic terrorist" known as [Atha Prime](/wiki/Atha_Prime/Legends "Atha Prime/Legends"), one of the architects of the Clone Wars, and his [Clone Warriors](/wiki/Clone_Warrior "Clone Warrior").[[260]](#cite_note-topt-260) In *Attack of the Clones*, it was seen that Darth Sidious and Count Dooku fill that role.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)
